### 9.3 K8s Helm Chart鏍稿績閰嶇疆

```yaml
# values.yaml (鐢熶骇鐜)
replicaCount: 2
image:
  repository: Magic-Octopus-Data-Verse/backend
  tag: v5.0.0

ingress:
  enabled: true
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: nginx
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: letsencrypt-prod
  hosts:
    - host: api.Magic-Octopus-Data-Verse.ai
      paths: ["/"]

database:
  postgresql:
    enabled: true
    postgresqlUsername: Magic-Octopus-Data-Verse
    postgresqlPassword: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    postgresqlDatabase: Magic-Octopus-Data-Verse
    persistence:
      size: 100Gi
  redis:
    enabled: true

minio:
  enabled: true
  persistence:
    size: 500Gi

env:
  - name: IMDF_REQUIRE_REAL_ENGINES
    value: "1"
  - name: AUDIT_CHAIN_SECRET
    valueFrom:
      secretKeyRef:
        name: Magic-Octopus-Data-Verse-secrets
        key: audit-secret
  - name: JWT_SECRET
    valueFrom:
      secretKeyRef:
        name: Magic-Octopus-Data-Verse-secrets
        key: jwt-secret

autoscaling:
  enabled: true
  minReplicas: 2
  maxReplicas: 10
  targetCPUUtilizationPercentage: 70

resources:
  requests:
    memory: "2Gi"
    cpu: "1"
  limits:
    memory: "8Gi"
    cpu: "4"

livenessProbe:
  httpGet:
    path: /healthz
    port: 8000
  initialDelaySeconds: 30
  periodSeconds: 10

readinessProbe:
  httpGet:
    path: /readyz
    port: 8000
  initialDelaySeconds: 10
  periodSeconds: 5
```

### 13.1 璺ㄦ暟鎹簱鍏煎灞?

```python
# db/compatibility.py
from sqlalchemy import JSON, TypeDecorator
from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB, UUID
import json
import numpy as np

class CompatibleJSON(TypeDecorator):
    """璺ㄦ暟鎹簱JSON绫诲瀷锛孭G鐜浣跨敤JSONB鎻愬崌鎬ц兘"""
    impl = JSON
    cache_ok = True

    def load_dialect_impl(self, dialect):
        if dialect.name == 'postgresql':
            return dialect.type_descriptor(JSONB())
        else:
            return dialect.type_descriptor(JSON())

    def process_bind_param(self, value, dialect):
        if value is not None:
            return json.dumps(value) if not isinstance(value, str) else value
        return value

    def process_result_value(self, value, dialect):
        if value is not None:
            return json.loads(value) if isinstance(value, str) else value
        return value

class CompatibleVector(TypeDecorator):
    """璺ㄦ暟鎹簱鍚戦噺绫诲瀷锛孭G鐜浣跨敤pgvector"""
    impl = JSON
    cache_ok = True

    def __init__(self, dim=1024, *args, **kwargs):
        self.dim = dim
        super().__init__(*args, **kwargs)

    def load_dialect_impl(self, dialect):
        if dialect.name == 'postgresql':
            from pgvector.sqlalchemy import Vector
            return dialect.type_descriptor(Vector(self.dim))
        else:
            return dialect.type_descriptor(JSON())

    def process_bind_param(self, value, dialect):
        if dialect.name == 'postgresql':
            return value
        return value.tolist() if hasattr(value, 'tolist') else value

    def process_result_value(self, value, dialect):
        if dialect.name == 'postgresql':
            return value
        return np.array(value) if value else None
```

```python
# models/capability.py (鏂板琛?
class Capability(Base, TimestampMixin):
    """鑳藉姏娉ㄥ唽琛?鈥?鏀寔217涓兘鍔?""
    __tablename__ = "capabilities"
    
    id = Column(String(50), primary_key=True)  # collect.t2i.sft.crawl
    name = Column(String(100), nullable=False)
    
    # 鏂扮殑鍒嗙被浣撶郴 (鎸夋暟鎹敓浜у叏閾捐矾鍒嗗眰)
    category = Column(String(50), nullable=False, index=True)  # collect/clean/dedupe/synth/label/qc/export/version/lineage
    
    # 灞傜骇缁嗗垎
    layer = Column(String(20), nullable=False)  # collection/cleaning/dedupe/synthesis/annotation/qc/export/version/lineage
    sub_layer = Column(String(30))  # t2i/i2v/agent/audio/text/multimodal/3d
    
    # 妯″瀷绫诲瀷涓庤缁冮樁娈?
    model_type = Column(String(50), index=True)  # text_to_image/image_to_video/text/audio/3d/agent/multimodal
    phase = Column(String(20), index=True)  # pretrain/sft/dpo/rl/lora
    
    # 鏁版嵁鐢熶骇璺緞
    path = Column(String(20))  # crawl/import/upload (閲囬泦灞? 鎴?synth (鍚堟垚灞?
    
    description = Column(Text)
    input_schema = Column(CompatibleJSON)
    output_schema = Column(CompatibleJSON)
    processing_pipeline = Column(CompatibleJSON)  # 澶勭悊姝ラ鍒楄〃
    dependencies = Column(CompatibleJSON)  # 渚濊禆鐨勮兘鍔汭D鍒楄〃
    
    # 浣跨敤缁熻
    invocation_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    success_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    avg_duration_ms = Column(Float, default=0.0)
    
    # 鐘舵€?
    status = Column(Enum('active', 'deprecated', 'draft', name='capability_status'), default='draft')
    version = Column(String(20), default='1.0.0')
    
    __table_args__ = (
        Index('ix_capabilities_category_layer', 'category', 'layer'),
        Index('ix_capabilities_model_phase', 'model_type', 'phase'),
    )
```

### 13.3 鏍稿績琛ㄥ畬鏁村瓧娈靛畾涔?

#### 13.3.1 `datasets` 鈥?鏁版嵁闆嗚〃 (鏁版嵁鐢熶骇鏍稿績)

```python
# models/dataset.py
from sqlalchemy import Column, String, Integer, DateTime, ForeignKey, JSON, Boolean, Enum, Text, Float
from sqlalchemy.dialects.postgresql import JSONB, ARRAY
from db.compatibility import CompatibleJSON, CompatibleVector
from models.base import Base, TimestampMixin
import uuid

class Dataset(Base, TimestampMixin):
    __tablename__ = "datasets"
    
    id = Column(String(24), primary_key=True, default=lambda: f"ds_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}")
    name = Column(String(200), nullable=False, index=True)
    description = Column(Text)
    
    # 妯℃€佷俊鎭?
    modality = Column(String(50), nullable=False, index=True)  # image/video/text/audio/multimodal/3d/panoptic
    sub_modality = Column(String(50))  # 瀛愭ā鎬? natural_image/medical/satellite/...
    
    # 鐗堟湰绠＄悊
    version = Column(String(20), default="1.0.0")
    parent_version_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("datasets.id"))
    branch = Column(String(50), default="main")
    
    # 缁熻淇℃伅
    total_samples = Column(Integer, default=0)
    total_size_bytes = Column(Integer, default=0)
    files_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # 鏍囩鍒嗗竷
    label_distribution = Column(CompatibleJSON, default={})  # {"cat": 1000, "dog": 800}
    class_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # 璐ㄩ噺鎸囨爣
    quality_score = Column(Float)  # 0-1
    defect_rate = Column(Float)  # 缂洪櫡鐜?
    
    # 鐘舵€?
    status = Column(Enum('draft', 'importing', 'processing', 'ready', 'exporting', 'exported', 'archived', 
                         name='dataset_status'), default='draft', index=True)
    
    # 鍏宠仈
    project_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("projects.id"), index=True)
    requirement_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("requirements.id"), index=True)
    created_by = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("users.id"), index=True)
    owner = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("users.id"), index=True)
    
    # 瀛樺偍浣嶇疆
    storage_backend = Column(String(20), default="minio")
    storage_bucket = Column(String(100))
    storage_prefix = Column(String(200))
    
    # 瀵煎嚭閰嶇疆
    export_config = Column(CompatibleJSON, default={})
    # {
    #   "formats": ["coco", "yolo"],
    #   "image_size": 1024,
    #   "normalize": true,
    #   "split": {"train": 0.8, "val": 0.1, "test": 0.1}
    # }
    
    # 琛€缂?
    source_chain = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])  # 瀹屾暣鏉ユ簮閾?
    
    # 鍏冩暟鎹?
    tags = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])
    metadata = Column(CompatibleJSON, default={})
    
    # 璁粌闃舵鏍囩
    training_phase = Column(String(50), index=True)  # pretrain/sft/dpo/rlhf/lora
    training_purpose = Column(String(200))
    
    __table_args__ = (
        Index('ix_datasets_modality_status', 'modality', 'status'),
        Index('ix_datasets_project_status', 'project_id', 'status'),
        Index('ix_datasets_training_phase', 'training_phase'),
    )
```

#### 13.3.2 `assets` 鈥?璧勪骇琛?(鏁版嵁鐢熶骇鍘熸潗鏂?

```python
# models/asset.py
class Asset(Base, TimestampMixin):
    __tablename__ = "assets"
    
    id = Column(String(28), primary_key=True, default=lambda: f"asset_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}")
    name = Column(String(200), nullable=False)
    description = Column(Text)
    
    # 鏂囦欢淇℃伅
    file_type = Column(String(50), nullable=False, index=True)  # image/video/audio/text/3d
    file_format = Column(String(20))  # jpg/png/mp4/wav/mp3/glb/obj
    file_size = Column(Integer)  # bytes
    file_hash = Column(String(64))  # SHA256
    file_path = Column(String(500))
    
    # 濯掍綋淇℃伅
    width = Column(Integer)
    height = Column(Integer)
    duration = Column(Float)  # 绉?(瑙嗛/闊抽)
    channels = Column(Integer)  # 闊抽閫氶亾鏁?
    sample_rate = Column(Integer)  # 闊抽閲囨牱鐜?
    bit_depth = Column(Integer)  # 鍥惧儚浣嶆繁
    frames = Column(Integer)  # 瑙嗛甯ф暟
    
    # 鍏冩暟鎹?
    metadata = Column(CompatibleJSON, default={})
    # {
    #   "camera_make": "Canon",
    #   "camera_model": "EOS 5D",
    #   "focal_length": 50,
    #   "aperture": 2.8,
    #   "iso": 100,
    #   "exposure_time": "1/1000",
    #   "gps": {"lat": 39.9, "lng": 116.4}
    # }
    
    # 鏍囩
    labels = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])  # [{"name": "cat", "confidence": 0.95}]
    tags = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])
    
    # 璐ㄩ噺璇勫垎
    quality_score = Column(Float)  # 0-1
    aesthetic_score = Column(Float)  # 0-1
    custom_score = Column(Float)  # 0-1
    
    # 鏉ユ簮
    source = Column(String(50))  # uploaded/crawled/api/imported
    source_url = Column(String(500))
    source_chain = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])  # 婧簮閾?
    
    # 璁稿彲璇?
    license_type = Column(String(50))  # cc-by/cc-by-sa/public-domain/apache/internal
    license_url = Column(String(500))
    
    # C2PA绛惧悕
    c2pa_signature = Column(String(500))
    c2pa_verified = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    
    # 褰掑睘
    owner = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("users.id"), index=True)
    project_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("projects.id"), index=True)
    dataset_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("datasets.id"), index=True)
    
    # 鐘舵€?
    status = Column(Enum('uploaded', 'processing', 'processed', 'labeled', 'verified', 'archived', 
                         name='asset_status'), default='uploaded', index=True)
    
    # 瀹℃牳
    review_status = Column(String(20))  # pending/approved/rejected
    review_comment = Column(Text)
    reviewed_by = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("users.id"))
    
    # 宓屽叆鍚戦噺 (鐢ㄤ簬璇箟鎼滅储)
    embedding = Column(CompatibleVector(1024))
    
    # 绱㈠紩
    __table_args__ = (
        Index('ix_assets_file_type_status', 'file_type', 'status'),
        Index('ix_assets_project_dataset', 'project_id', 'dataset_id'),
        Index('ix_assets_owner', 'owner'),
    )
```

```python
# models/pack.py
class Pack(Base, TimestampMixin):
    __tablename__ = "packs"
    
    id = Column(String(24), primary_key=True, default=lambda: f"pack_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}")
    name = Column(String(200), nullable=False)
    description = Column(Text)
    
    # 绫诲瀷
    pack_type = Column(Enum('data_pack', 'task_pack', name='pack_type'), nullable=False)
    
    # 鐘舵€佹満 (7鎬?
    status = Column(Enum(
        'created', 'ready', 'in_annotation', 'annotated', 
        'reviewed', 'qc_passed', 'delivered',
        name='pack_status'
    ), default='created', index=True)
    
    # 鏁版嵁鍐呭
    asset_ids = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])  # 鍖呭惈鐨勮祫浜D鍒楄〃
    annotation_ids = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])  # 鏍囨敞ID鍒楄〃
    
    # 浠诲姟閰嶇疆
    task_type = Column(String(50))  # annotation/review/qc
    geometry_type = Column(String(50))  # rect/polygon/point/keypoint/obb/mask/3d_cuboid
    label_schema = Column(CompatibleJSON, default={})
    
    # 鍒嗛厤淇℃伅
    assignee = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("users.id"), index=True)
    assigned_at = Column(DateTime)
    
    # 杩涘害
    total_items = Column(Integer, default=0)
    completed_items = Column(Integer, default=0)
    progress = Column(Float, default=0.0)  # 0-1
    
    # 璐ㄩ噺
    quality_score = Column(Float)
    defect_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    
    # 鍏宠仈
    project_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("projects.id"), index=True)
    requirement_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("requirements.id"), index=True)
    dataset_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("datasets.id"), index=True)
    delivery_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("deliveries.id"), index=True)
    
    # 璺敱淇℃伅
    route_strategy = Column(String(50))  # collection/annotation/review
    route_history = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])
    
    # 浼樺厛绾?
    priority = Column(Integer, default=0)  # 0-10
    deadline = Column(DateTime)
    
    __table_args__ = (
        Index('ix_packs_status_priority', 'status', 'priority'),
        Index('ix_packs_project_status', 'project_id', 'status'),
        Index('ix_packs_assignee_status', 'assignee', 'status'),
    )
```

```python
class AuditChainEntry(Base, TimestampMixin):

    trace_id = Column(String(32))

    source_line = Column(Integer)
    
    __table_args__ = (
        Index('ix_audit_chain_entity', 'entity_type', 'entity_id'),
```

```python
# models/agent.py
class AgentTask(Base, TimestampMixin):
    __tablename__ = "agent_tasks"
    
    id = Column(String(24), primary_key=True, default=lambda: f"at_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:16]}")
    user_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("users.id"), nullable=False, index=True)
    
    # Agent绫诲瀷
    agent_type = Column(String(50), nullable=False, index=True)
    agent_name = Column(String(100))
    
    # 鐘舵€佹満
    status = Column(Enum(
        'queued', 'running', 'paused', 'completed', 'failed', 'cancelled',
        name='agent_task_status'
    ), default='queued', index=True)
    priority = Column(Integer, default=0, index=True)  # 0-10
    
    # 杈撳叆杈撳嚭
    intent = Column(String(100))  # 璇嗗埆鐨勬剰鍥?
    payload = Column(CompatibleJSON, nullable=False)  # 浠诲姟鍙傛暟
    result = Column(CompatibleJSON)  # 鎵ц缁撴灉
    error = Column(Text)  # 閿欒淇℃伅
    
    # 閲嶈瘯
    retry_count = Column(Integer, default=0)
    max_retries = Column(Integer, default=3)
    retry_delay = Column(Integer, default=60)  # 绉?
    
    # 骞傜瓑
    idempotency_key = Column(String(64), unique=True, index=True)
    
    # 杩借釜
    trace_id = Column(String(32), index=True)
    parent_task_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("agent_tasks.id"), index=True)
    session_id = Column(String(32), ForeignKey("agent_sessions.id"), index=True)
    
    # Octo鍏宠仈
    bot_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("agent_bots.id"), index=True)
    channel_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("agent_channels.id"), index=True)
    matter_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("agent_matters.id"), index=True)
    
    # 鏃堕棿
    queued_at = Column(DateTime, server_default=func.now())
    started_at = Column(DateTime)
    completed_at = Column(DateTime)
    
    # 杩涘害
    progress = Column(Float, default=0.0)  # 0-1
    progress_message = Column(Text)
    subtask_ids = Column(CompatibleJSON, default=[])
    
    # 涓婁笅鏂?
    context_snapshot = Column(CompatibleJSON)
    screen_context = Column(CompatibleJSON)  # Vida灞忓箷鎰熺煡涓婁笅鏂?
    
    # 瀹¤
    audit_chain_id = Column(String(24), ForeignKey("audit_chain_entries.id"))
    
    __table_args__ = (
        Index('ix_agent_tasks_status_priority', 'status', 'priority'),
        Index('ix_agent_tasks_user_status', 'user_id', 'status'),
        Index('ix_agent_tasks_bot_status', 'bot_id', 'status'),
    )
```

# 绗?4绔?鑳藉姏璁捐 鈥?鏁版嵁鐢熶骇鍏ㄩ摼璺兘鍔?(瀹屾暣閲嶅啓鐗?

### 14.1 鑳藉姏鍒嗙被浣撶郴 (鎸夋暟鎹敓浜у叏閾捐矾鍒嗗眰)

```python
# capabilities_v2/engine.py
class CapabilityCategory(str, Enum):
    # ================================================================
    # 涓€銆侀噰闆嗗眰 (Collection Layer) 鈥?浠庣湡瀹炴暟鎹簮鑾峰彇鍘熷鏁版嵁
    #    鉁?鐖櫕閲囬泦 路 API閲囬泦 路 鏂囦欢瀵煎叆 路 鏁版嵁闆嗗鍏?
    # ================================================================
    COLLECT = "collect"
    COLLECT_IMAGE = "collect_image"
    COLLECT_VIDEO = "collect_video"
    COLLECT_3D = "collect_3d"
    COLLECT_AUDIO = "collect_audio"
    COLLECT_TEXT = "collect_text"
    COLLECT_MULTIMODAL = "collect_multimodal"
    COLLECT_AGENT = "collect_agent"
    
    # ================================================================
    # 浜屻€佹竻娲楀眰 (Cleaning Layer) 鈥?鏁版嵁鍑€鍖栦笌鏍囧噯鍖?
    # ================================================================
    CLEAN = "clean"
    CLEAN_IMAGE = "clean_image"
    CLEAN_VIDEO = "clean_video"
    CLEAN_3D = "clean_3d"
    CLEAN_AUDIO = "clean_audio"
    CLEAN_TEXT = "clean_text"
    CLEAN_MULTIMODAL = "clean_multimodal"
    
    # ================================================================
    # 涓夈€佸幓閲嶅眰 (Dedupe Layer) 鈥?澶氱骇鍘婚噸
    # ================================================================
    DEDUPE = "dedupe"
    DEDUPE_URL = "dedupe_url"
    DEDUPE_CONTENT = "dedupe_content"
    DEDUPE_PHASH = "dedupe_phash"
    DEDUPE_SIMHASH = "dedupe_simhash"
    DEDUPE_SEMANTIC = "dedupe_semantic"
    
    # ================================================================
    # 鍥涖€佸悎鎴愬眰 (Synthesis Layer) 鈥?閫氳繃AI妯″瀷鎴栬鍒欑敓鎴愭暟鎹?
    #    鉁?鏂囩敓鍥惧悎鎴?路 鍥剧敓鍥惧悎鎴?路 鏂囩敓瑙嗛鍚堟垚 路 绛?
    # ================================================================
    SYNTHESIZE = "synthesize"
    SYNTHESIZE_T2I = "synthesize_t2i"
    SYNTHESIZE_I2I = "synthesize_i2i"
    SYNTHESIZE_EDIT = "synthesize_edit"
    SYNTHESIZE_MULTI_EDIT = "synthesize_multi_edit"
    SYNTHESIZE_T2V = "synthesize_t2v"
    SYNTHESIZE_I2V = "synthesize_i2v"
    SYNTHESIZE_MULTI_I2V = "synthesize_multi_i2v"
    SYNTHESIZE_T2D = "synthesize_t2d"
    SYNTHESIZE_I2D = "synthesize_i2d"
    SYNTHESIZE_MULTI_I2D = "synthesize_multi_i2d"
    SYNTHESIZE_AUDIO = "synthesize_audio"
    SYNTHESIZE_TEXT = "synthesize_text"
    SYNTHESIZE_AGENT = "synthesize_agent"
    
    # ================================================================
    # 浜斻€佹爣娉ㄥ眰 (Annotation Layer) 鈥?鑷姩鏍囨敞 + 浜哄伐鏍囨敞
    # ================================================================
    LABEL = "label"
    LABEL_AUTO = "label_auto"
    LABEL_HUMAN = "label_human"
    LABEL_CONSENSUS = "label_consensus"
    LABEL_REVIEW = "label_review"
    
    # ================================================================
    # 鍏€佽川妫€灞?(Quality Control Layer) 鈥?璐ㄩ噺鎺у埗
    # ================================================================
    QC = "qc"
    QC_FULL = "qc_full"
    QC_SAMPLE = "qc_sample"
    QC_AQL = "qc_aql"
    QC_IMAGE = "qc_image"
    QC_VIDEO = "qc_video"
    QC_3D = "qc_3d"
    QC_AUDIO = "qc_audio"
    QC_TEXT = "qc_text"
    
    # ================================================================
    # 涓冦€佸鍑哄眰 (Export Layer) 鈥?鏍煎紡杞崲涓庡鍑?
    # ================================================================
    EXPORT = "export"
    EXPORT_PRETRAIN = "export_pretrain"
    EXPORT_SFT = "export_sft"
    EXPORT_DPO = "export_dpo"
    EXPORT_RL = "export_rl"
    EXPORT_LORA = "export_lora"
    
    # ================================================================
    # 鍏€佹暟鎹増鏈鐞?(Version Management)
    # ================================================================
    VERSION = "version"
    VERSION_CREATE = "version_create"
    VERSION_BRANCH = "version_branch"
    VERSION_TAG = "version_tag"
    VERSION_ROLLBACK = "version_rollback"
    
    # ================================================================
    # 涔濄€佹暟鎹缂樼鐞?(Lineage Management)
    # ================================================================
    LINEAGE = "lineage"
    LINEAGE_TRACK = "lineage_track"
    LINEAGE_QUERY = "lineage_query"
    LINEAGE_IMPACT = "lineage_impact"
```

### 14.6 鑳藉姏璋冪敤瀹炵幇

```python
# capabilities_v2/engine.py
class CapabilityRegistry:
    def __init__(self):
        self._capabilities = {}
        self._load_all_definitions()  # 鍔犺浇217涓兘鍔涘畾涔?
    
    async def invoke(self, cap_id: str, inputs: Dict, actor: str = None, 
                     refs: Dict = None) -> CapabilityResult:
        cap = self._capabilities.get(cap_id)
        if not cap:
            raise CapabilityNotFoundError(cap_id)
        
        # 鏍规嵁鑳藉姏绫诲瀷璺敱鍒板搴旀墽琛屽櫒
        if cap.category.startswith("collect"):
            # 閲囬泦灞?鈥?鍙墽琛岀湡瀹炴暟鎹噰闆嗭紝缁濅笉鍚堟垚
            result = await self._execute_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category.startswith("synth"):
            # 鍚堟垚灞?鈥?鍙墽琛孉I妯″瀷鍚堟垚鐢熸垚
            result = await self._execute_synth(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category.startswith("clean"):
            result = await self._execute_clean(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category.startswith("dedupe"):
            result = await self._execute_dedupe(cap, inputs, refs)
        # ... 鍏朵粬灞傜骇
        
        # 瀹¤銆佽缂樸€佹寚鏍囪褰?
        await self._post_process(cap, inputs, result, actor)
        
        return CapabilityResult(status="success", outputs=result)
```

| **ComfyEngine** | `engines/comfy_engine.py` | ~1000 | ComfyUI宸ヤ綔娴?|

### 15.2 DatasetManager 鈥?鏁版嵁鐢熶骇鍏ㄩ摼璺紩鎿?(瀹屾暣瀹炵幇)

```python
# engines/dataset_manager.py
class DatasetManager:
    """
    鏁版嵁闆嗙鐞嗗紩鎿?鈥?鏁版嵁鐢熶骇鍏ㄩ摼璺牳蹇?
    瑕嗙洊: 鍒涘缓 鈫?閲囬泦 鈫?瀵煎叆 鈫?娓呮礂 鈫?鏍囨敞 鈫?璐ㄦ 鈫?瀵煎嚭 鈫?鐗堟湰绠＄悊
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.db = SessionLocal()
        self.crawler_engine = CrawlerEngine()
        self.cleaning_engine = CleaningEngine()
        self.dedupe_engine = DedupeEngine()
        self.label_engine = AutoLabelEngine()
        self.scoring_engine = ScoringEngine()
        self.qc_engine = InternalQCEngine()
        self.export_engine = ExportEngine()
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.metrics = ServiceMetrics()
    
    # ============ 1. 鍒涘缓鏁版嵁闆?============
    async def create_dataset(self, name: str, modality: str, 
                             project_id: str = None, 
                             config: Dict = None) -> Dataset:
        """鍒涘缓鏂版暟鎹泦"""
        dataset = Dataset(
            id=f"ds_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            name=name,
            modality=modality,
            status="draft",
            project_id=project_id,
            export_config=config or {},
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.db.add(dataset)
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="dataset.created",
            entity_type="dataset",
            entity_id=dataset.id,
            payload={"name": name, "modality": modality}
        )
        
        return dataset
    
    # ============ 2. 瀵煎叆鏁版嵁 (澶氱鏉ユ簮) ============
    async def import_data(self, dataset_id: str, source_type: str, 
                          source_config: Dict) -> ImportResult:
        """
        瀵煎叆鏁版嵁鍒版暟鎹泦
        鏀寔: 鏈湴鏂囦欢/OSS/S3/URL/閲囬泦浠诲姟
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        dataset.status = "importing"
        self.db.commit()
        
        imported_assets = []
        
        if source_type == "local":
            # 鏈湴鏂囦欢涓婁紶
            files = source_config.get("files", [])
            for file_path in files:
                asset = await self._import_local_file(file_path, dataset_id)
                imported_assets.append(asset)
                
        elif source_type == "oss":
            # OSS/S3瀵煎叆
            bucket = source_config.get("bucket")
            prefix = source_config.get("prefix")
            assets = await self._import_from_oss(bucket, prefix, dataset_id)
            imported_assets.extend(assets)
            
        elif source_type == "crawler":
            # 浠庨噰闆嗕换鍔″鍏?
            job_id = source_config.get("job_id")
            assets = await self._import_from_crawler(job_id, dataset_id)
            imported_assets.extend(assets)
            
        elif source_type == "url":
            # URL鍒楄〃瀵煎叆
            urls = source_config.get("urls", [])
            for url in urls:
                asset = await self._import_from_url(url, dataset_id)
                imported_assets.append(asset)
        
        # 鏇存柊缁熻
        dataset.total_samples = len(imported_assets)
        dataset.files_count = len(imported_assets)
        dataset.status = "processing"
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="dataset.imported",
            entity_type="dataset",
            entity_id=dataset_id,
            payload={"source_type": source_type, "count": len(imported_assets)}
        )
        
        return ImportResult(dataset_id=dataset_id, imported_count=len(imported_assets), 
                           assets=imported_assets)
    
    async def _import_local_file(self, file_path: str, dataset_id: str) -> Asset:
        """瀵煎叆鏈湴鏂囦欢"""
        file_type = self._detect_file_type(file_path)
        file_hash = self._compute_hash(file_path)
        
        # 鍘婚噸妫€鏌?
        existing = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.file_hash == file_hash,
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id
        ).first()
        if existing:
            return existing
        
        asset = Asset(
            id=f"asset_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}",
            name=os.path.basename(file_path),
            file_type=file_type,
            file_format=os.path.splitext(file_path)[1][1:],
            file_size=os.path.getsize(file_path),
            file_hash=file_hash,
            file_path=file_path,
            dataset_id=dataset_id,
            status="uploaded",
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        # 鎻愬彇濯掍綋淇℃伅
        if file_type == "image":
            from PIL import Image
            img = Image.open(file_path)
            asset.width = img.width
            asset.height = img.height
            asset.metadata["mode"] = img.mode
            
        elif file_type == "video":
            import cv2
            cap = cv2.VideoCapture(file_path)
            asset.width = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_WIDTH))
            asset.height = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_HEIGHT))
            asset.duration = cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_COUNT) / cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS)
            asset.frames = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_COUNT))
            cap.release()
            
        elif file_type == "audio":
            from pydub import AudioSegment
            audio = AudioSegment.from_file(file_path)
            asset.duration = len(audio) / 1000.0
            asset.channels = audio.channels
            asset.sample_rate = audio.frame_rate
            
        self.db.add(asset)
        self.db.commit()
        return asset
    
    # ============ 3. 鏁版嵁娓呮礂 ============
    async def clean_dataset(self, dataset_id: str, rules: Dict = None) -> CleanResult:
        """
        娓呮礂鏁版嵁闆?鈥?8妯℃€佹竻娲?
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id,
            Asset.status != "deleted"
        ).all()
        
        cleaned_assets = []
        rejected_assets = []
        
        for asset in assets:
            result = await self.cleaning_engine.clean(asset, rules or {})
            if result.rejected:
                rejected_assets.append(asset)
                asset.status = "rejected"
            else:
                cleaned_assets.append(asset)
                asset.status = "processed"
                # 鏇存柊娓呮礂鍚庣殑鍏冩暟鎹?
                asset.metadata.update(result.metadata)
        
        self.db.commit()
        
        return CleanResult(
            dataset_id=dataset_id,
            total=len(assets),
            cleaned=len(cleaned_assets),
            rejected=len(rejected_assets),
            rejected_assets=rejected_assets
        )
    
    # ============ 4. 鑷姩鎵撴爣 ============
    async def auto_label(self, dataset_id: str, schema: Dict) -> LabelResult:
        """
        鑷姩鎵撴爣 鈥?4绛栫暐
        """
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id,
            Asset.status == "processed"
        ).all()
        
        labeled = []
        for asset in assets:
            labels = await self.label_engine.label(asset, schema)
            asset.labels = labels
            labeled.append(asset)
        
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 鏇存柊鏍囩鍒嗗竷
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        dataset.label_distribution = self._compute_distribution(labeled)
        self.db.commit()
        
        return LabelResult(dataset_id=dataset_id, labeled_count=len(labeled))
    
    # ============ 5. 璐ㄩ噺璇勫垎 ============
    async def score_dataset(self, dataset_id: str, dimensions: List[str]) -> ScoreResult:
        """
        澶氱淮搴﹁瘎鍒?
        """
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id,
            Asset.status == "processed"
        ).all()
        
        scores = []
        for asset in assets:
            score = await self.scoring_engine.score(asset, dimensions)
            asset.quality_score = score.quality
            asset.aesthetic_score = score.aesthetic
            asset.custom_score = score.custom
            scores.append(score)
        
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 璁＄畻鏁版嵁闆嗗钩鍧囧垎
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        dataset.quality_score = sum(s.quality for s in scores) / len(scores) if scores else 0
        self.db.commit()
        
        return ScoreResult(dataset_id=dataset_id, scores=scores, avg_quality=dataset.quality_score)
    
    # ============ 6. 瀵煎嚭鏁版嵁闆?(18绉嶆牸寮? ============
    async def export_dataset(self, dataset_id: str, format: str, 
                             config: Dict = None) -> ExportResult:
        """
        瀵煎嚭鏁版嵁闆?鈥?18绉嶈缁冩牸寮?
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        dataset.status = "exporting"
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 鑾峰彇璧勪骇
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(
            Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id,
            Asset.status.in_(["processed", "labeled"])
        ).all()
        
        # 鏍规嵁鏍煎紡瀵煎嚭
        if format == "coco":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_coco(assets, config)
        elif format == "yolo":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_yolo(assets, config)
        elif format == "llava":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_llava(assets, config)
        elif format == "webdataset":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_webdataset(assets, config)
        elif format == "jsonl":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_jsonl(assets, config)
        elif format == "parquet":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_parquet(assets, config)
        elif format == "chatsml":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_chatml(assets, config)
        elif format == "dpo":
            export_url = await self.export_engine.export_dpo(assets, config)
        else:
            raise UnsupportedFormatError(format)
        
        dataset.status = "exported"
        dataset.export_config["last_export"] = {
            "format": format,
            "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "url": export_url
        }
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="dataset.exported",
            entity_type="dataset",
            entity_id=dataset_id,
            payload={"format": format, "export_url": export_url}
        )
        
        return ExportResult(dataset_id=dataset_id, format=format, export_url=export_url)
    
    # ============ 7. 鏁版嵁闆嗙増鏈鐞?============
    async def create_version(self, dataset_id: str, version: str = None, 
                             message: str = None) -> DatasetVersion:
        """
        鍒涘缓鏁版嵁闆嗙増鏈?
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        new_version = version or increment_version(dataset.version)
        
        # 澶嶅埗鏁版嵁闆?
        versioned = Dataset(
            id=f"ds_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            name=f"{dataset.name}_v{new_version}",
            modality=dataset.modality,
            version=new_version,
            parent_version_id=dataset.id,
            branch=dataset.branch,
            total_samples=dataset.total_samples,
            total_size_bytes=dataset.total_size_bytes,
            files_count=dataset.files_count,
            label_distribution=dataset.label_distribution,
            quality_score=dataset.quality_score,
            status="ready",
            project_id=dataset.project_id,
            created_by=dataset.created_by,
            owner=dataset.owner,
            storage_backend=dataset.storage_backend,
            storage_bucket=dataset.storage_bucket,
            storage_prefix=dataset.storage_prefix,
            export_config=dataset.export_config,
            source_chain=dataset.source_chain + [{"version": dataset.version, "at": datetime.now().isoformat()}],
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.db.add(versioned)
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="dataset.versioned",
            entity_type="dataset",
            entity_id=versioned.id,
            payload={"version": new_version, "parent": dataset.id}
        )
        
        return versioned
    
    # ============ 8. 鏁版嵁闆嗙粺璁?============
    async def get_stats(self, dataset_id: str) -> DatasetStats:
        """
        鑾峰彇鏁版嵁闆嗙粺璁′俊鎭?
        """
        dataset = self.db.query(Dataset).filter(Dataset.id == dataset_id).first()
        if not dataset:
            raise DatasetNotFoundError(dataset_id)
        
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(Asset.dataset_id == dataset_id).all()
        
        # 璁＄畻鍚勭被缁熻
        file_types = {}
        label_counts = {}
        quality_distribution = {"high": 0, "medium": 0, "low": 0}
        
        for asset in assets:
            file_types[asset.file_type] = file_types.get(asset.file_type, 0) + 1
            
            if asset.labels:
                for label in asset.labels:
                    label_counts[label.get("name")] = label_counts.get(label.get("name"), 0) + 1
            
            if asset.quality_score:
                if asset.quality_score >= 0.8:
                    quality_distribution["high"] += 1
                elif asset.quality_score >= 0.5:
                    quality_distribution["medium"] += 1
                else:
                    quality_distribution["low"] += 1
        
        return DatasetStats(
            dataset_id=dataset_id,
            name=dataset.name,
            modality=dataset.modality,
            total_samples=len(assets),
            file_types=file_types,
            label_distribution=label_counts,
            quality_distribution=quality_distribution,
            avg_quality_score=dataset.quality_score,
            versions=self._get_versions(dataset_id),
            created_at=dataset.created_at
        )
```

### 15.2.1 CapabilityRegistry 鈥?鏂板鍙岄€氶亾鎵ц閫昏緫

```python
# capabilities_v2/engine.py
class CapabilityRegistry:
    """鑳藉姏娉ㄥ唽涓績 鈥?鏀寔217涓兘鍔涳紝鍖哄垎閲囬泦/鍚堟垚鍙岄€氶亾"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self._capabilities = {}  # cap_id -> CapabilityDefinition
        self._load_all_definitions()  # 鍔犺浇217涓兘鍔涘畾涔?
    
    async def invoke(self, cap_id: str, inputs: Dict, actor: str = None, 
                     refs: Dict = None) -> CapabilityResult:
        cap = self._capabilities.get(cap_id)
        if not cap:
            raise CapabilityNotFoundError(cap_id)
        
        # 鏍规嵁鑳藉姏绫诲瀷璺敱鍒板搴旀墽琛屽櫒 (鍒嗗眰鎵ц)
        if cap.category == "collect":
            # 閲囬泦灞?鈥?鍙墽琛岀湡瀹炴暟鎹噰闆嗭紝缁濅笉鍚堟垚
            result = await self._execute_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "synth":
            # 鍚堟垚灞?鈥?鍙墽琛孉I妯″瀷鍚堟垚鐢熸垚
            result = await self._execute_synth(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "clean":
            result = await self._execute_clean(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "dedupe":
            result = await self._execute_dedupe(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "label":
            result = await self._execute_label(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "qc":
            result = await self._execute_qc(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "export":
            result = await self._execute_export(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "version":
            result = await self._execute_version(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif cap.category == "lineage":
            result = await self._execute_lineage(cap, inputs, refs)
        else:
            raise UnknownCategoryError(cap.category)
        
        # 瀹¤銆佽缂樸€佹寚鏍囪褰?
        await self._post_process(cap, inputs, result, actor)
        
        return CapabilityResult(status="success", outputs=result, 
                                category=cap.category, layer=cap.layer)
    
    async def _execute_collect(self, cap: CapabilityDefinition, inputs: Dict, 
                               refs: Dict) -> Dict:
        """
        閲囬泦灞傛墽琛屽櫒 鈥?浠呮墽琛岀湡瀹炴暟鎹噰闆嗭紝缁濅笉鍚堟垚
        
        閲囬泦鏂瑰紡:
        - crawl: Web鐖櫕閲囬泦
        - import: 鍏紑鏁版嵁闆嗗鍏?
        - upload: 鐢ㄦ埛涓婁紶
        
        閲囬泦娓犻亾: 83涓?
        """
        path = cap.path  # crawl / import / upload
        
        if path == "crawl":
            return await self._execute_crawler_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif path == "import":
            return await self._execute_import_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        elif path == "upload":
            return await self._execute_upload_collect(cap, inputs, refs)
        else:
            raise UnknownCollectPathError(path)
    
    async def _execute_synth(self, cap: CapabilityDefinition, inputs: Dict, 
                             refs: Dict) -> Dict:
        """
        鍚堟垚灞傛墽琛屽櫒 鈥?浠呮墽琛孉I妯″瀷/瑙勫垯鍚堟垚鐢熸垚
        
        鍚堟垚鏂规硶: 
        - 鎵╂暎妯″瀷 (鏂囩敓鍥?鍥剧敓鍥?鍥惧儚缂栬緫)
        - 瑙嗛鐢熸垚妯″瀷 (鏂囩敓瑙嗛/鍥剧敓瑙嗛/澶氬浘鐢熻棰?
        - 3D鐢熸垚妯″瀷 (鏂囩敓3D/鍥剧敓3D/澶氬浘鐢?D)
        - TTS/ASR妯″瀷
        - 璇█妯″瀷 (鏂囨湰/Agent/澶氭ā鎬?
        """
        model_type = cap.model_type
        phase = cap.phase
        
        # 鏍规嵁妯″瀷绫诲瀷璺敱
        if model_type == "text_to_image":
            return await self._synth_t2i(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "image_to_image":
            return await self._synth_i2i(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "image_edit":
            return await self._synth_edit(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "text_to_video":
            return await self._synth_t2v(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "image_to_video":
            return await self._synth_i2v(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "multi_image_to_video":
            return await self._synth_multi_i2v(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "text_to_3d":
            return await self._synth_t2d(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "image_to_3d":
            return await self._synth_i2d(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "audio":
            return await self._synth_audio(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "text":
            return await self._synth_text(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "agent":
            return await self._synth_agent(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        elif model_type == "multimodal":
            return await self._synth_mm(cap, inputs, phase, refs)
        else:
            raise UnknownModelTypeError(model_type)
    
    async def _synth_t2i(self, cap, inputs, phase, refs) -> Dict:
        """鏂囩敓鍥惧悎鎴?""
        # 璋冪敤鍥惧儚鐢熸垚Provider (Agnes/ComfyUI/SDXL/Flux)
        provider = self._select_provider("image_generation", phase)
        result = await provider.generate_image(
            prompt=inputs["prompt"],
            size=inputs.get("size", "1024x1024"),
            style=inputs.get("style"),
            negative_prompt=inputs.get("negative_prompt"),
            seed=inputs.get("seed"),
            steps=inputs.get("steps", 30)
        )
        return {"images": result.images, "metadata": result.metadata}
    
    async def _synth_t2v(self, cap, inputs, phase, refs) -> Dict:
        """鏂囩敓瑙嗛鍚堟垚"""
        provider = self._select_provider("video_generation", phase)
        result = await provider.generate_video(
            prompt=inputs["prompt"],
            duration=inputs.get("duration", 5),
            resolution=inputs.get("resolution", "1080p"),
            fps=inputs.get("fps", 24),
            style=inputs.get("style"),
            negative_prompt=inputs.get("negative_prompt"),
            seed=inputs.get("seed")
        )
        return {"video": result.video, "metadata": result.metadata}
    
    async def _synth_t2d(self, cap, inputs, phase, refs) -> Dict:
        """鏂囩敓3D鍚堟垚"""
        provider = self._select_provider("3d_generation", phase)
        result = await provider.generate_3d(
            prompt=inputs["prompt"],
            format=inputs.get("format", "glb"),
            resolution=inputs.get("resolution", "medium"),
            seed=inputs.get("seed")
        )
        return {"model": result.model, "metadata": result.metadata}
    
    # ... 鍏朵粬鍚堟垚鏂规硶 (i2i, edit, i2v, multi_i2v, i2d, multi_i2d, audio, text, agent, mm)
```

### 15.2.2 鏂板: DataProductionPipelineEngine (鏁版嵁鐢熶骇鍏ㄩ摼璺紪鎺掑紩鎿?

```python
# engines/data_production_pipeline_engine.py
class DataProductionPipelineEngine:
    """
    鏁版嵁鐢熶骇鍏ㄩ摼璺紪鎺掑紩鎿?鈥?涓茶仈閲囬泦鈫掓竻娲椻啋鍘婚噸鈫掑悎鎴愨啋鏍囨敞鈫掕川妫€鈫掑鍑?
    鏀寔鍙岄€氶亾 (閲囬泦閫氶亾 + 鍚堟垚閫氶亾) 骞惰鐢熶骇
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.capability_registry = CapabilityRegistry()
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.active_pipelines = {}
    
    async def create_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> str:
        """鍒涘缓鏁版嵁鐢熶骇绠＄嚎"""
        pipeline_id = f"pipe_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
        
        # 鏍规嵁閰嶇疆閫夋嫨閫氶亾
        if config.channel == "collection":
            # 閲囬泦閫氶亾: 閲囬泦 鈫?娓呮礂 鈫?鍘婚噸 鈫?鏍囨敞 鈫?璐ㄦ 鈫?瀵煎嚭
            stages = self._build_collection_pipeline(config)
        elif config.channel == "synthesis":
            # 鍚堟垚閫氶亾: 鍚堟垚 鈫?娓呮礂 鈫?鏍囨敞 鈫?璐ㄦ 鈫?瀵煎嚭
            stages = self._build_synthesis_pipeline(config)
        else:
            # 鍙岄€氶亾: (閲囬泦 + 鍚堟垚) 鈫?娓呮礂 鈫?鍘婚噸 鈫?鏍囨敞 鈫?璐ㄦ 鈫?瀵煎嚭
            stages = self._build_dual_pipeline(config)
        
        self.active_pipelines[pipeline_id] = {
            "id": pipeline_id,
            "config": config,
            "stages": stages,
            "status": "created"
        }
        
        return pipeline_id
    
    def _build_collection_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> List[Stage]:
        """鏋勫缓閲囬泦閫氶亾绠＄嚎"""
        return [
            Stage("collect", self._get_collect_capability(config)),
            Stage("clean", self._get_clean_capability(config)),
            Stage("dedupe", self._get_dedupe_capability(config)),
            Stage("label", self._get_label_capability(config)),
            Stage("qc", self._get_qc_capability(config)),
            Stage("export", self._get_export_capability(config))
        ]
    
    def _build_synthesis_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> List[Stage]:
        """鏋勫缓鍚堟垚閫氶亾绠＄嚎"""
        return [
            Stage("synth", self._get_synth_capability(config)),
            Stage("clean", self._get_clean_capability(config)),
            Stage("label", self._get_label_capability(config)),
            Stage("qc", self._get_qc_capability(config)),
            Stage("export", self._get_export_capability(config))
        ]
    
    def _build_dual_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> List[Stage]:
        """鏋勫缓鍙岄€氶亾绠＄嚎 (閲囬泦 + 鍚堟垚 骞惰)"""
        return [
            Stage("collect", self._get_collect_capability(config), parallel=True),
            Stage("synth", self._get_synth_capability(config), parallel=True),
            Stage("merge", self._merge_capabilities, depends_on=["collect", "synth"]),
            Stage("clean", self._get_clean_capability(config)),
            Stage("dedupe", self._get_dedupe_capability(config)),
            Stage("label", self._get_label_capability(config)),
            Stage("qc", self._get_qc_capability(config)),
            Stage("export", self._get_export_capability(config))
        ]
```


### 15.3 CrawlerEngine 鈥?鏅鸿兘閲囬泦寮曟搸 (瀹屾暣瀹炵幇)

```python
# engines/crawler_engine.py
class CrawlerEngine:
    """
    鏅鸿兘閲囬泦寮曟搸 鈥?83娓犻亾缁熶竴璋冨害
    鏍稿績鍔熻兘: 閲囬泦浠诲姟绠＄悊銆佹笭閬撹皟搴︺€佽繘搴︾洃鎺с€佹柇鐐圭画浼?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.channels = self._load_all_channels()
        self.active_jobs = {}
        self.crawler_pool = AsyncPool(max_workers=50)
        self.source_tracer = SourceTracer()
        self.dedupe_engine = DedupeEngine()
        self.cleaning_engine = CleaningEngine()
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.metrics = ServiceMetrics()
    
    def _load_all_channels(self) -> Dict:
        """鍔犺浇83涓笭閬?""
        return {
            # Web鐖櫕 (10)
            "playwright": PlaywrightCrawler,
            "selenium": SeleniumCrawler,
            "scrapy": ScrapyCrawler,
            "beautifulsoup": BeautifulSoupCrawler,
            # ... 鍏朵綑73涓?
        }
    
    async def start_crawl(self, config: CrawlerConfig) -> str:
        """
        鍚姩閲囬泦浠诲姟
        """
        job_id = f"crawl_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
        
        # 楠岃瘉閰嶇疆
        self._validate_config(config)
        
        # 鍒涘缓浠诲姟璁板綍
        self.active_jobs[job_id] = {
            "config": config,
            "status": "queued",
            "started_at": datetime.now(),
            "progress": 0,
            "total_estimated": self._estimate_total(config),
            "results": [],
            "errors": [],
            "logs": []
        }
        
        # 寮傛鎵ц
        asyncio.create_task(self._run_crawl(job_id))
        
        # 瀹¤璁板綍
        await audit_chain.append(
            action="crawler.start",
            actor=config.owner,
            payload={"job_id": job_id, "channel_type": config.channel_type, "seed_urls": config.seed_urls}
        )
        
        return job_id
    
    async def _run_crawl(self, job_id: str):
        """
        鎵ц閲囬泦浠诲姟鐨勬牳蹇冮€昏緫
        """
        job = self.active_jobs[job_id]
        config = job["config"]
        
        try:
            job["status"] = "running"
            
            # 鑾峰彇瀵瑰簲鐨勭埇铏?
            crawler = self._get_crawler(config.channel_type, config)
            
            # 鍚姩閲囬泦娴?
            async for raw_doc in crawler.crawl(config.seed_urls):
                # 1. 瀹炴椂鏇存柊杩涘害
                job["progress"] += 1
                
                # 2. 6绾у幓閲?
                unique_doc = await self.dedupe_engine.dedupe(raw_doc)
                if not unique_doc:
                    job["logs"].append({"type": "duplicate", "url": raw_doc.url})
                    continue
                
                # 3. 8妯℃€佹竻娲?
                clean_doc = await self.cleaning_engine.clean(unique_doc, config.cleaning_rules)
                if clean_doc.rejected:
                    job["logs"].append({"type": "rejected", "url": raw_doc.url, "reason": clean_doc.reason})
                    continue
                
                # 4. 鑷姩鎵撴爣 (濡傛灉閰嶇疆)
                if config.label_schema:
                    labels = await self.label_engine.label(clean_doc, config.label_schema)
                    clean_doc.labels = labels
                
                # 5. 璇勫垎 (濡傛灉閰嶇疆)
                if config.scoring_dimensions:
                    scores = await self.scoring_engine.score(clean_doc, config.scoring_dimensions)
                    clean_doc.scores = scores
                
                # 6. 娣卞害婧簮
                source_chain = await self.source_tracer.trace(clean_doc)
                clean_doc.source_chain = source_chain
                
                # 7. 瀛樺偍
                stored_doc = await self._store_document(clean_doc, config)
                job["results"].append(stored_doc.id)
                
                # 8. 鎺ㄩ€佷簨浠?
                await self.bus.record(
                    topic="crawler.document_collected",
                    entity_type="asset",
                    entity_id=stored_doc.id,
                    payload={
                        "job_id": job_id,
                        "source": config.channel_type,
                        "url": raw_doc.url,
                        "progress": job["progress"]
                    }
                )
                
                # 9. 閫熺巼闄愬埗
                await self._rate_limit(config.rate_limit_rps)
                
                # 10. 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚﹁揪鍒颁笂闄?
                if config.max_pages and job["progress"] >= config.max_pages:
                    break
            
            job["status"] = "completed"
            job["completed_at"] = datetime.now()
            
            await self.bus.record(
                topic="crawler.job_completed",
                entity_type="crawler_job",
                entity_id=job_id,
                payload={"total_documents": len(job["results"]), "errors": len(job["errors"])}
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            job["status"] = "failed"
            job["error"] = str(e)
            job["completed_at"] = datetime.now()
            
            await self.bus.record(
                topic="crawler.job_failed",
                entity_type="crawler_job",
                entity_id=job_id,
                payload={"error": str(e)}
            )
    
    def _get_crawler(self, channel_type: str, config: CrawlerConfig) -> BaseCrawler:
        """宸ュ巶鏂规硶鑾峰彇瀵瑰簲娓犻亾鐨勭埇铏?""
        crawler_class = self.channels.get(channel_type)
        if not crawler_class:
            raise UnsupportedChannelError(channel_type)
        return crawler_class(config)
    
    async def get_job_status(self, job_id: str) -> Dict:
        """鑾峰彇浠诲姟瀹炴椂鐘舵€?""
        job = self.active_jobs.get(job_id)
        if not job:
            return {"status": "not_found"}
        
        return {
            "status": job["status"],
            "progress": job["progress"],
            "total_estimated": job["total_estimated"],
            "started_at": job["started_at"],
            "completed_at": job.get("completed_at"),
            "results_count": len(job["results"]),
            "errors_count": len(job["errors"]),
            "progress_percentage": (job["progress"] / job["total_estimated"] * 100) if job["total_estimated"] else 0
        }
    
    async def pause_job(self, job_id: str) -> bool:
        """鏆傚仠浠诲姟 (鏀寔鏂偣缁紶)"""
        if job_id not in self.active_jobs:
            return False
        if self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] not in ["running", "queued"]:
            return False
        self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] = "paused"
        return True
    
    async def resume_job(self, job_id: str) -> bool:
        """鎭㈠浠诲姟"""
        if job_id not in self.active_jobs:
            return False
        if self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] != "paused":
            return False
        self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] = "running"
        asyncio.create_task(self._run_crawl(job_id))
        return True
    
    async def stop_job(self, job_id: str) -> bool:
        """鍋滄浠诲姟"""
        if job_id not in self.active_jobs:
            return False
        self.active_jobs[job_id]["status"] = "stopped"
        return True
    
    async def _store_document(self, doc: ProcessedDocument, config: CrawlerConfig) -> Asset:
        """瀛樺偍閲囬泦鍒扮殑鏂囨。"""
        asset = Asset(
            id=f"asset_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}",
            name=doc.filename or doc.url.split("/")[-1],
            file_type=doc.file_type,
            file_format=doc.file_format,
            file_size=doc.size,
            file_hash=doc.hash,
            file_path=await self._upload_to_storage(doc, config),
            source="crawled",
            source_url=doc.url,
            source_chain=doc.source_chain,
            labels=doc.labels,
            quality_score=doc.scores.get("quality") if doc.scores else None,
            aesthetic_score=doc.scores.get("aesthetic") if doc.scores else None,
            status="processed",
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.db.add(asset)
        self.db.commit()
        return asset
```

### 15.4 WorkbenchEngine 鈥?鏍囨敞宸ヤ綔鍙板紩鎿?(瀹屾暣瀹炵幇)

```python
# engines/workbench_engine.py
class WorkbenchEngine:
    """
    鏍囨敞宸ヤ綔鍙板紩鎿?鈥?鏀寔10绉嶅嚑浣曟爣娉?
    鍔熻兘: 浠诲姟鎷夊彇/蹇冭烦/鎻愪氦銆佹爣娉ㄤ繚瀛樸€丄I杈呭姪鏍囨敞銆丄ctive Learning
    """
    
    GEOMETRY_TYPES = {
        "rect": {"fields": ["x", "y", "w", "h"], "min": 0},
        "polygon": {"fields": ["points"], "min_points": 3},
        "point": {"fields": ["x", "y"]},
        "keypoint": {"fields": ["x", "y", "v"]},
        "obb": {"fields": ["x", "y", "w", "h", "theta"]},
        "mask": {"fields": ["rle", "bitmap_url"]},
        "3d_cuboid": {"fields": ["center", "size", "rotation"]},
        "lidar_pointcloud": {"fields": ["points", "intensity"]},
        "3d_bbox": {"fields": ["center", "size", "rotation"]},
        "panoptic": {"fields": ["segments", "relations"]}
    }
    
    TASK_STATES = ["pending", "assigned", "in_progress", "submitted", "approved", "rejected", "blocked"]
    REVIEW_STAGES = ["draft", "self_check", "peer_review", "final_review", "done"]
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.tasks = {}
        self.locks = {}
        self.annotations = {}
        self.db = SessionLocal()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def enqueue_task(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str = None) -> str:
        """灏嗕换鍔″姞鍏ラ槦鍒?""
        task_id = f"task_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"
        self.tasks[task_id] = {
            "id": task_id,
            "pack_id": pack_id,
            "status": "pending",
            "assigned_to": None,
            "created_at": datetime.now()
        }
        return task_id
    
    async def pull_next_task(self, worker_id: str, geometry_type: str = None) -> Optional[Dict]:
        """
        鎷夊彇涓嬩竴涓换鍔?(5鍒嗛挓閿?
        """
        # 鏌ユ壘鍙敤浠诲姟
        query = self.db.query(Pack).filter(
            Pack.status == "in_annotation",
            Pack.assignee == None
        )
        if geometry_type:
            query = query.filter(Pack.geometry_type == geometry_type)
        
        pack = query.order_by(Pack.priority.desc(), Pack.created_at).first()
        if not pack:
            return None
        
        # 鍔犻攣 (5鍒嗛挓)
        lock_key = f"lock_{pack.id}"
        if lock_key in self.locks:
            return None
        
        self.locks[lock_key] = {
            "worker": worker_id,
            "acquired_at": datetime.now(),
            "expires_at": datetime.now() + timedelta(minutes=5)
        }
        
        # 鏇存柊浠诲姟鐘舵€?
        pack.assignee = worker_id
        pack.status = "in_progress"
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 鑾峰彇璧勪骇
        assets = self.db.query(Asset).filter(Asset.id.in_(pack.asset_ids)).all()
        
        return {
            "pack_id": pack.id,
            "task_id": pack.id,
            "assets": [self._asset_to_dict(a) for a in assets],
            "geometry_type": pack.geometry_type,
            "label_schema": pack.label_schema,
            "lock_expires_at": self.locks[lock_key]["expires_at"]
        }
    
    async def heartbeat(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str) -> bool:
        """蹇冭烦缁攣"""
        lock_key = f"lock_{pack_id}"
        if lock_key not in self.locks:
            return False
        if self.locks[lock_key]["worker"] != worker_id:
            return False
        
        # 缁攣5鍒嗛挓
        self.locks[lock_key]["expires_at"] = datetime.now() + timedelta(minutes=5)
        return True
    
    async def release_task(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str) -> bool:
        """閲婃斁浠诲姟"""
        lock_key = f"lock_{pack_id}"
        if lock_key not in self.locks:
            return False
        if self.locks[lock_key]["worker"] != worker_id:
            return False
        
        del self.locks[lock_key]
        
        pack = self.db.query(Pack).filter(Pack.id == pack_id).first()
        if pack:
            pack.assignee = None
            pack.status = "ready"
            self.db.commit()
        
        return True
    
    async def save_annotation(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str, 
                              annotations: List[Dict]) -> bool:
        """
        淇濆瓨鏍囨敞 (鏀寔10绉嶅嚑浣曠被鍨?
        """
        # 楠岃瘉鍑犱綍绫诲瀷
        pack = self.db.query(Pack).filter(Pack.id == pack_id).first()
        if not pack:
            return False
        
        geometry_type = pack.geometry_type
        schema = self.GEOMETRY_TYPES.get(geometry_type)
        if not schema:
            raise UnsupportedGeometryError(geometry_type)
        
        # 楠岃瘉姣忎釜鏍囨敞
        for ann in annotations:
            self._validate_annotation(ann, schema)
        
        # 淇濆瓨
        annotation_id = f"ann_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"
        self.annotations[annotation_id] = {
            "id": annotation_id,
            "pack_id": pack_id,
            "worker_id": worker_id,
            "annotations": annotations,
            "geometry_type": geometry_type,
            "saved_at": datetime.now()
        }
        
        # 鏇存柊pack杩涘害
        pack.completed_items = pack.completed_items + 1
        pack.progress = pack.completed_items / pack.total_items if pack.total_items else 0
        self.db.commit()
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="annotation.saved",
            entity_type="pack",
            entity_id=pack_id,
            payload={"worker_id": worker_id, "count": len(annotations)}
        )
        
        return True
    
    async def submit_task(self, pack_id: str, worker_id: str) -> bool:
        """鎻愪氦浠诲姟"""
        pack = self.db.query(Pack).filter(Pack.id == pack_id).first()
        if not pack:
            return False
        
        # 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚︽墍鏈夐」鐩凡鏍囨敞
        if pack.completed_items < pack.total_items:
            return False
        
        pack.status = "annotated"
        self.db.commit()
        
        # 閲婃斁閿?
        lock_key = f"lock_{pack_id}"
        if lock_key in self.locks:
            del self.locks[lock_key]
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="annotation.submitted",
            entity_type="pack",
            entity_id=pack_id,
            payload={"worker_id": worker_id}
        )
        
        return True
    
    def _validate_annotation(self, ann: Dict, schema: Dict):
        """楠岃瘉鍗曚釜鏍囨敞鐨勫嚑浣曞悎娉曟€?""
        if "type" not in ann:
            raise ValidationError("Missing type field")
        
        if ann["type"] not in self.GEOMETRY_TYPES:
            raise ValidationError(f"Unsupported geometry type: {ann['type']}")
        
        schema = self.GEOMETRY_TYPES[ann["type"]]
        for field in schema["fields"]:
            if field not in ann:
                raise ValidationError(f"Missing field: {field}")
        
        # 澶氳竟褰㈢壒娈婇獙璇?
        if ann["type"] == "polygon":
            if len(ann.get("points", [])) < 3:
                raise ValidationError("Polygon must have at least 3 points")
        
        # 鐭╁舰楠岃瘉
        if ann["type"] == "rect":
            if ann.get("w", 0) <= 0 or ann.get("h", 0) <= 0:
                raise ValidationError("Rect must have positive width and height")
    
    def _asset_to_dict(self, asset: Asset) -> Dict:
        return {
            "id": asset.id,
            "name": asset.name,
            "file_type": asset.file_type,
            "file_format": asset.file_format,
            "file_path": asset.file_path,
            "width": asset.width,
            "height": asset.height,
            "metadata": asset.metadata
        }
```

### 16.2 Provider璺敱涓嶨ateway

```python
# providers/gateway.py
class AIGateway:
    """
    AI Gateway 鈥?缁熶竴Provider绠＄悊銆佽矾鐢便€丗allback銆佺紦瀛樸€佹垚鏈帶鍒?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.registry = ProviderRegistry()
        self.cache = TTLCache(max_size=10000, default_ttl=3600)
        self.circuit_breakers = {}
        self.cost_guard = CostGuard()
        self.metrics = ServiceMetrics()
    
    async def invoke(self, provider: str, model: str, prompt: str,
                     prefer: str = "balanced",
                     max_cost_cents: float = None,
                     stream: bool = False,
                     **kwargs) -> InvokeResult:
        """
        缁熶竴鐨凙I璋冪敤鎺ュ彛
        """
        # 1. 鎴愭湰妫€鏌?
        if max_cost_cents:
            estimated_cost = self._estimate_cost(provider, model, prompt)
            if estimated_cost > max_cost_cents:
                raise CostExceededError(f"Estimated cost {estimated_cost}c exceeds limit {max_cost_cents}c")
        
        # 2. 缂撳瓨妫€鏌?(闈炴祦寮?
        if not stream:
            cache_key = self._cache_key(provider, model, prompt, kwargs)
            cached = self.cache.get(cache_key)
            if cached:
                return cached
        
        # 3. 鐔旀柇鍣ㄦ鏌?
        circuit_key = f"{provider}:{model}"
        if circuit_key in self.circuit_breakers:
            if self.circuit_breakers[circuit_key].is_open():
                # Fallback
                return await self._fallback(provider, model, prompt, **kwargs)
        
        # 4. 鑾峰彇Provider
        provider_instance = self.registry.get(provider)
        if not provider_instance:
            raise ProviderNotFoundError(provider)
        
        # 5. 璋冪敤
        start = time.time()
        try:
            if stream:
                result = await provider_instance.stream(model, prompt, **kwargs)
            else:
                result = await provider_instance.generate(model, prompt, **kwargs)
            status = "success"
            duration = time.time() - start
            
            # 缂撳瓨缁撴灉
            if not stream:
                self.cache.set(cache_key, result)
            
            # 璁板綍鎸囨爣
            self.metrics.record_llm_call(provider, model, duration, status)
            
            return result
            
        except Exception as e:
            status = "failure"
            # 璁板綍澶辫触
            if circuit_key in self.circuit_breakers:
                self.circuit_breakers[circuit_key].record_failure()
            
            # 灏濊瘯Fallback
            return await self._fallback(provider, model, prompt, **kwargs)
    
    async def _fallback(self, primary_provider: str, model: str, prompt: str,
                        **kwargs) -> InvokeResult:
        """Fallback鍒板鐢≒rovider"""
        fallback_providers = self._get_fallback_chain(primary_provider)
        for provider in fallback_providers:
            try:
                provider_instance = self.registry.get(provider)
                result = await provider_instance.generate(model, prompt, **kwargs)
                result._fallback = True
                result._primary_provider = primary_provider
                return result
            except Exception:
                continue
        raise AllProvidersFailedError(f"All fallback providers failed for {primary_provider}")
    
    def _get_fallback_chain(self, provider: str) -> List[str]:
        """鑾峰彇Fallback閾?""
        chains = {
            "openai": ["claude", "deepseek", "qwen"],
            "claude": ["openai", "deepseek", "gemini"],
            "deepseek": ["qwen", "openai", "claude"],
            "agnes": ["deepseek", "qwen", "openai"],
        }
        return chains.get(provider, ["deepseek", "qwen", "openai"])
    
    def route(self, family: str, prefer: str = "cost") -> str:
        """鏍规嵁鍋忓ソ璺敱鍒版渶浣砅rovider"""
        candidates = self.registry.list_by_family(family)
        if not candidates:
            return "mock"
        
        if prefer == "speed":
            return min(candidates, key=lambda p: p.latency_p50).id
        elif prefer == "trust":
            return max(candidates, key=lambda p: p.trust_level).id
        elif prefer == "cost":
            return min(candidates, key=lambda p: p.price_per_1k_input + p.price_per_1k_output).id
        elif prefer == "free":
            free_candidates = [p for p in candidates if p.price_per_1k_input == 0]
            return free_candidates[0].id if free_candidates else candidates[0].id
        
        return candidates[0].id
```

### 16.3 Agnes AI Provider (鍏嶈垂鍏ㄦā鎬?

```python
# providers/agnes.py
class AgnesProvider:
    """
    Agnes AI Provider 鈥?鍏嶈垂鍏ㄦā鎬丄PI
    鏀寔: 鏂囨湰銆佸浘鍍忋€佽棰戙€佺煭鍓?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.base_url = "https://platform.agnes-ai.com/api/v1"
        self.api_key = os.getenv("AGNES_API_KEY")
        self.models = {
            "text": "agnes-2.0-flash",
            "image": "agnes-image-2.1-flash",
            "video": "agnes-video-2.0",
            "drama": "agnes-drama-1.0"
        }
    
    async def generate_image(self, prompt: str, size: str = "1024x1024", 
                             quality: str = "standard") -> ImageResult:
        """鐢熸垚鍥惧儚 (鍏嶈垂4K)"""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/images/generations"
        payload = {
            "model": self.models["image"],
            "prompt": prompt,
            "size": size,  # 1024x1024, 4096x4096
            "quality": quality,
            "n": 1
        }
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.post(url, json=payload, 
                                    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"}) as resp:
                data = await resp.json()
                return ImageResult(
                    url=data["data"][0]["url"],
                    prompt=prompt,
                    size=size
                )
    
    async def generate_video(self, prompt: str, duration: int = 5,
                             reference_images: List[str] = None) -> VideoResult:
        """鐢熸垚瑙嗛 (鍏嶈垂)"""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/videos/generations"
        payload = {
            "model": self.models["video"],
            "prompt": prompt,
            "duration": duration,
            "reference_images": reference_images or []
        }
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.post(url, json=payload,
                                    headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"}) as resp:
                data = await resp.json()
                return VideoResult(
                    url=data["url"],
                    duration=duration,
                    prompt=prompt
                )
```

### 18.4 璺ㄦā鎬丷AG (1024-d缁熶竴鍚戦噺绌洪棿)

```python
# multimodal/rag.py
class MultimodalRAG:
    """
    璺ㄦā鎬丷AG 鈥?1024-d缁熶竴鍚戦噺绌洪棿
    鏀寔: 鍥炬枃/瑙嗛鏂?闊虫枃璺ㄦā鎬佹绱?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.vector_store = VectorStore(dim=1024)
        self.encoders = {
            "text": TextEncoder(),
            "image": CLIPEncoder(),
            "audio": AudioEncoder(),
            "video": VideoEncoder()
        }
        self.bm25 = BM25Index()
    
    async def index(self, refs: List[MediaRef]) -> List[str]:
        """绱㈠紩澶氭ā鎬佹暟鎹?""
        ids = []
        for ref in refs:
            # 鎻愬彇鐗瑰緛
            embedding = await self.encoders[ref.modality].encode(ref.content)
            # 瀛樺偍
            doc_id = await self.vector_store.add(embedding, ref.metadata)
            # 鏂囨湰绱㈠紩 (BM25)
            if ref.text:
                self.bm25.add(doc_id, ref.text)
            ids.append(doc_id)
        return ids
    
    async def search(self, query: MediaRef, top_k: int = 5, 
                     hybrid: bool = True) -> List[RetrievedItem]:
        """璺ㄦā鎬佹绱?(娣峰悎妫€绱?"""
        # 鍚戦噺妫€绱?
        query_embedding = await self.encoders[query.modality].encode(query.content)
        vec_results = await self.vector_store.search(query_embedding, top_k)
        
        if not hybrid:
            return vec_results
        
        # BM25妫€绱?
        if query.text:
            bm25_results = self.bm25.search(query.text, top_k)
            # 铻嶅悎 (RRF)
            results = self._reciprocal_rank_fusion(vec_results, bm25_results)
            return results
        
        return vec_results
    
    async def answer(self, query: MediaRef, top_k: int = 5, 
                     llm_call=None) -> Dict:
        """RAG鍥炵瓟"""
        # 1. 妫€绱㈢浉鍏虫枃妗?
        results = await self.search(query, top_k)
        
        # 2. 鏋勫缓涓婁笅鏂?
        context = "\n".join([r.content for r in results])
        
        # 3. LLM鐢熸垚绛旀
        if llm_call:
            answer = await llm_call(context, query.text)
            return {
                "answer": answer,
                "sources": results,
                "context": context
            }
        
        return {"sources": results}
```

```python
    CLASSIFICATION = "classification"  # 鍒嗙被
```
