| **涓浗涓绘祦骞冲彴** | 8 | 灏忕孩涔? 鎶栭煶, 瑙嗛鍙? 鍏紬鍙? 蹇墜, 寰崥 | RedFox API |
| **鎷涜仒/鍟嗕笟** | 4 | Boss鐩磋仒, LinkedIn, 鑴夎剦, 浼佹煡鏌?| 鍏紑API |
| **P2P/鐗规畩** | 4 | IPFS, BitTorrent DHT, I2P, 瀛︽湳FTP | 涓撶敤鍗忚 |
| **鑷畾涔?MCP** | 3 | 鐢ㄦ埛鑷畾涔? LLM鐢熸垚, 澶栭儴MCP | 鍔ㄦ€佺敓鎴?|

### 19.2 娓犻亾閰嶇疆Schema

```python
# intelligence/crawler/config.py
@dataclass
class CrawlerConfig:
    """鐖櫕閰嶇疆 鈥?鎿嶄綔鍛樺彲鍏ㄧ淮搴﹂厤缃?""
    name: str
    channel_type: ChannelType
    seed_urls: List[str]
    
    # 鍚堣
    compliance: str = "strict"  # strict/internal/audit/research
    respect_robots_txt: bool = True
    respect_rate_limit: bool = True
    rate_limit_rps: float = 1.0
    
    # 鍙嶇埇
    user_agent_pool: List[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: DEFAULT_UA_POOL)
    proxy_pool: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    rotate_proxy_every: int = 10
    use_browser_fingerprint: bool = True
    captcha_solver: Optional[str] = None
    
    # 閫夋嫨鍣?
    selectors: Dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)
    wait_selectors: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    click_selectors: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    
    # 娣卞害
    max_depth: int = 0
    max_pages: int = 100
    same_domain_only: bool = True
    
    # 杩囨护
    url_include_patterns: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    url_exclude_patterns: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    min_content_length: int = 100
    language_filter: Optional[List[str]] = None
    
    # 娓呮礂瑙勫垯
    cleaning_rules: Dict = field(default_factory=dict)
    label_schema: Dict = field(default_factory=dict)
    scoring_dimensions: List[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: ["quality", "aesthetic"])
    
    # 杈撳嚭
    output_format: str = "raw"  # raw/markdown/structured/embedding
    extract_metadata: bool = True
    extract_links: bool = True
    extract_images: bool = True
    
    # 瀛樺偍
    storage_backend: str = "minio"
    storage_bucket: str = "imdf-crawled"
    storage_prefix: str = ""
    
    # 璋冨害
    parallel_workers: int = 4
    rate_per_worker: float = 0.5
    batch_size: int = 100
    
    # 鍏宠仈
    project_id: Optional[str] = None
    dataset_id: Optional[str] = None
    owner: Optional[str] = None
```

### 19.3 BaseCrawler鎶借薄鍩虹被

```python
# intelligence/crawler/base.py
class BaseCrawler(ABC):
    """鎵€鏈夌埇铏殑鍩虹被"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: CrawlerConfig):
        self.config = config
        self.metrics = CrawlerMetrics()
        self.audit_chain = AuditChain()
        self.compliance = ComplianceChecker(config.compliance)
        self.proxy_pool = ProxyPool(config.proxy_pool)
        self.ua_pool = UserAgentPool(config.user_agent_pool)
        self.session = None
    
    @abstractmethod
    async def fetch(self, url: str) -> RawDocument:
        """瀛愮被瀹炵幇鍏蜂綋鎶撳彇"""
        pass
    
    async def crawl(self, urls: List[str]) -> AsyncIterator[RawDocument]:
        """鏍囧噯crawl娴佺▼"""
        semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(self.config.parallel_workers)
        
        async def _process(url: str) -> Optional[RawDocument]:
            async with semaphore:
                # 鍚堣妫€鏌?
                if not await self.compliance.can_fetch(url):
                    self.metrics.blocked += 1
                    return None
                # 闄愰€?
                await self._rate_limit()
                # 鎶撳彇
                try:
                    doc = await self.fetch(url)
                    self.metrics.fetched += 1
                    return doc
                except Exception as e:
                    self.metrics.errors += 1
                    await self.audit_chain.append(
                        action="crawler.fetch_failed",
                        actor="system",
                        payload={"url": url, "error": str(e)}
                    )
                    return None
        
        tasks = [_process(url) for url in urls]
        for coro in asyncio.as_completed(tasks):
            doc = await coro
            if doc:
                yield doc
                self.metrics.success += 1
    
    async def _rate_limit(self):
        if self.config.respect_rate_limit:
            await asyncio.sleep(1.0 / self.config.rate_limit_rps)
```

### 19.4 WebCrawler瀹炵幇 (Playwright椹卞姩)

```python
# intelligence/crawler/web_crawler.py
class WebCrawler(BaseCrawler):
    """閫氱敤Web鐖櫕 - JavaScript娓叉煋鍙嬪ソ"""
    
    async def fetch(self, url: str) -> RawDocument:
        async with async_playwright() as p:
            browser = await p.chromium.launch(
                headless=self.config.headless,
                proxy={"server": self.proxy_pool.get_next()} if self.proxy_pool.has_proxies() else None
            )
            context = await browser.new_context(
                user_agent=self.ua_pool.get_next(),
                viewport={"width": 1920, "height": 1080},
                locale="en-US"
            )
            page = await context.new_page()
            await page.goto(url, wait_until="networkidle", timeout=30000)
            
            # 鏅鸿兘绛夊緟
            for sel in self.config.wait_selectors:
                try:
                    await page.wait_for_selector(sel, timeout=5000)
                except:
                    pass
            
            # 婊氬姩瑙﹀彂鎳掑姞杞?
            await page.evaluate("window.scrollTo(0, document.body.scrollHeight)")
            await page.wait_for_timeout(2000)
            
            # 鐐瑰嚮缈婚〉
            for sel in self.config.click_selectors:
                try:
                    await page.click(sel)
                    await page.wait_for_timeout(1000)
                except:
                    pass
            
            # 鎻愬彇
            html = await page.content()
            text = await page.evaluate("() => document.body.innerText")
            images = await page.query_selector_all("img")
            image_urls = [await img.get_attribute("src") for img in images]
            links = await page.query_selector_all("a")
            link_urls = [await link.get_attribute("href") for link in links]
            metadata = await page.evaluate("""() => ({
                title: document.title,
                description: document.querySelector('meta[name="description"]')?.content,
                keywords: document.querySelector('meta[name="keywords"]')?.content,
                og_image: document.querySelector('meta[property="og:image"]')?.content,
                author: document.querySelector('meta[name="author"]')?.content
            })""")
            
            await browser.close()
            
            return RawDocument(
                url=url,
                content=html,
                content_type="html",
                text=text,
                images=image_urls,
                links=link_urls,
                metadata=metadata,
                title=metadata["title"]
            )
```

### 19.5 鑷€傚簲鐖櫕鐢熸垚鍣?

```python
# intelligence/crawler/auto_generator.py
class AutoCrawlerGenerator:
    """
    鑷€傚簲鐖櫕鐢熸垚 鈥?LLM鍒嗘瀽椤甸潰缁撴瀯鑷姩鐢熸垚涓撶敤鐖櫕
    娴佺▼: 鎶撳彇鏍锋湰 鈫?LLM鍒嗘瀽DOM 鈫?鐢熸垚閫夋嫨鍣?鈫?楠岃瘉鈮?5% 鈫?娉ㄥ唽
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.llm = get_llm_provider()
        self.crawler_engine = CrawlerEngine()
    
    async def generate(self, seed_url: str, target_count: int = 100) -> CrawlerConfig:
        # 1. 鎶撳彇鏍锋湰 (10椤?
        samples = await self._fetch_samples(seed_url, n=10)
        
        # 2. LLM鍒嗘瀽缁撴瀯
        prompt = f"""
        Analyze these 10 pages and identify the CSS selectors for:
        1. Main content area
        2. Title
        3. Author
        4. Date
        5. Images
        6. Pagination
        7. Infinite scroll triggers
        8. Lazy loading triggers
        
        Pages:
        {samples}
        
        Return JSON with selectors.
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        structure = json.loads(response)
        
        # 3. 鐢熸垚閰嶇疆
        config = CrawlerConfig(
            name=f"auto_gen_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            channel_type=ChannelType.WEB,
            seed_urls=[seed_url],
            selectors=structure.get("selectors", {}),
            wait_selectors=structure.get("wait_selectors", []),
            click_selectors=structure.get("click_selectors", []),
            max_pages=target_count,
            respect_robots_txt=True,
            rate_limit_rps=2.0
        )
        
        # 4. 楠岃瘉鍑嗙‘鐜?(鈮?5%)
        accuracy = await self._validate(config)
        if accuracy < 0.95:
            raise InsufficientAccuracyError(f"Accuracy {accuracy:.2%} < 95%")
        
        # 5. 娉ㄥ唽鍒扮埇铏簱
        await self.crawler_engine.register_channel(config)
        
        return config
    
    async def _validate(self, config: CrawlerConfig) -> float:
        """楠岃瘉鐖櫕鍑嗙‘鐜?""
        crawler = WebCrawler(config)
        test_urls = config.seed_urls[:5]  # 娴嬭瘯5涓〉闈?
        
        correct = 0
        total = 0
        
        async for doc in crawler.crawl(test_urls):
            total += 1
            # 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚︽垚鍔熸彁鍙栦簡鍏抽敭鍐呭
            if doc.content and len(doc.content) > 100:
                correct += 1
        
        return correct / total if total > 0 else 0
```

### 20.2 6绾у幓閲嶅紩鎿?

```python
# intelligence/processing/dedupe.py
class DedupeEngine:
    """
    6绾у幓閲嶅紩鎿?
    Level 1: URL绮剧‘鍖归厤
    Level 2: URL瑙勮寖鍖栧尮閰?
    Level 3: 鍐呭SHA256 hash
    Level 4: 鎰熺煡hash pHash (鍥惧儚)
    Level 5: SimHash (鏂囨湰)
    Level 6: Embedding璇箟鑱氱被
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.url_exact = set()
        self.url_normalized = set()
        self.content_sha = {}
        self.phash_index = {}
        self.simhash_index = {}
        self.embedding_index = None
        self.phash_threshold = 8  # Hamming璺濈闃堝€?
        self.simhash_threshold = 4
    
    async def dedupe(self, doc: RawDocument) -> Optional[Document]:
        """澶氱骇鍘婚噸"""
        # Level 1: URL绮剧‘鍖归厤
        if doc.url in self.url_exact:
            return None
        self.url_exact.add(doc.url)
        
        # Level 2: URL瑙勮寖鍖?
        norm_url = self._normalize_url(doc.url)
        if norm_url in self.url_normalized:
            return None
        self.url_normalized.add(norm_url)
        
        # Level 3: 鍐呭SHA256
        content_hash = hashlib.sha256(doc.content.encode()).hexdigest()
        if content_hash in self.content_sha:
            return None
        self.content_sha[content_hash] = doc.url
        
        # Level 4: pHash (鍥惧儚)
        if doc.content_type == "image":
            phash = await self._compute_phash(doc.content)
            if phash:
                for existing_hash in self.phash_index:
                    if self._hamming_distance(phash, existing_hash) < self.phash_threshold:
                        return None
                self.phash_index[phash] = doc.url
        
        # Level 5: SimHash (鏂囨湰)
        if doc.content_type == "text":
            simhash = self._compute_simhash(doc.content)
            if simhash:
                for existing_hash in self.simhash_index:
                    if self._hamming_distance(simhash, existing_hash) < self.simhash_threshold:
                        return None
                self.simhash_index[simhash] = doc.url
        
        # Level 6: Embedding鑱氱被 (璇箟鍘婚噸)
        # 浣跨敤鍚戦噺鐩镐技搴?> 0.95 鍒ゅ畾涓洪噸澶?
        # 姝ゅ鐪佺暐鍏蜂綋瀹炵幇
        
        return Document(url=doc.url, content=doc.content, content_type=doc.content_type)
```

### 20.3 8妯℃€佹竻娲楀紩鎿?

```python
# intelligence/processing/cleaning.py
class CleaningEngine:
    """
    8妯℃€佹竻娲楀紩鎿?
    鏀寔: 鏂囨湰/鍥惧儚/瑙嗛/闊抽/3D/鐐逛簯/鍖荤枟褰卞儚/鍏ㄦ櫙
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.watermark_detector = WatermarkDetector()
        self.nsfw_detector = NSFWDetector()
        self.blur_detector = BlurDetector()
        self.html_cleaner = HTMLCleaner()
    
    async def clean(self, doc: Document, rules: Dict) -> CleanResult:
        """鏍规嵁妯℃€佹墽琛屾竻娲?""
        cleaners = {
            "text": self._clean_text,
            "image": self._clean_image,
            "video": self._clean_video,
            "audio": self._clean_audio,
            "3d": self._clean_3d,
            "pointcloud": self._clean_pointcloud,
            "dicom": self._clean_dicom,
            "panoptic": self._clean_panoptic
        }
        
        cleaner = cleaners.get(doc.content_type)
        if not cleaner:
            return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="Unsupported type")
        
        return await cleaner(doc, rules)
    
    async def _clean_text(self, doc: Document, rules: Dict) -> CleanResult:
        """鏂囨湰娓呮礂"""
        text = doc.content
        
        # HTML鍘婚櫎
        if rules.get("strip_html", True):
            text = BeautifulSoup(text, "html.parser").get_text()
        
        # 缂栫爜淇
        text = text.encode("utf-8", errors="ignore").decode("utf-8")
        
        # 璇█妫€娴?
        lang = detect(text)
        if rules.get("language_filter") and lang not in rules["language_filter"]:
            return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason=f"Language {lang} not allowed")
        
        # 闀垮害杩囨护
        if len(text) < rules.get("min_length", 100):
            return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="Too short")
        
        # 鏁忔劅璇嶈繃婊?
        if rules.get("sensitive_words"):
            for word in rules["sensitive_words"]:
                if word in text:
                    return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason=f"Sensitive word: {word}")
        
        return CleanResult(cleaned=True, content=text, metadata={"language": lang, "length": len(text)})
    
    async def _clean_image(self, doc: Document, rules: Dict) -> CleanResult:
        """鍥惧儚娓呮礂"""
        from PIL import Image
        img = Image.open(doc.path)
        
        # 灏哄杩囨护
        min_size = rules.get("min_size")
        if min_size:
            if img.width < min_size[0] or img.height < min_size[1]:
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason=f"Size {img.width}x{img.height} < {min_size}")
        
        # 姘村嵃妫€娴?
        if rules.get("no_watermark", True):
            if await self.watermark_detector.detect(img):
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="Watermark detected")
        
        # NSFW妫€娴?
        if rules.get("no_nsfw", True):
            if await self.nsfw_detector.detect(img):
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="NSFW")
        
        # 妯＄硦妫€娴?
        min_sharpness = rules.get("min_sharpness")
        if min_sharpness:
            sharpness = self._calc_sharpness(img)
            if sharpness < min_sharpness:
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason=f"Blurry ({sharpness:.2f})")
        
        return CleanResult(cleaned=True, content=img, 
                          metadata={"width": img.width, "height": img.height, "mode": img.mode})
    
    async def _clean_video(self, doc: Document, rules: Dict) -> CleanResult:
        """瑙嗛娓呮礂"""
        import cv2
        cap = cv2.VideoCapture(doc.path)
        
        # 榛戣竟妫€娴?
        if rules.get("no_black_bars", True):
            has_bars = await self._detect_black_bars(cap)
            if has_bars:
                cap.release()
                return CleanResult(cleaned=False, reason="Black bars detected")
        
        # 鍏抽敭甯ф彁鍙?
        if rules.get("extract_keyframes"):
            frames = await self._extract_keyframes(cap, rules.get("keyframe_count", 10))
        else:
            frames = []
        
        # 瀛楀箷鎻愬彇
        if rules.get("extract_subtitles"):
            subtitles = await self._extract_subtitles(doc.path)
        else:
            subtitles = []
        
        cap.release()
        
        return CleanResult(cleaned=True, 
                          metadata={"frames": frames, "subtitles": subtitles})
```


## 绗?1绔?娣卞害婧簮绯荤粺

```python
# intelligence/crawler/source_tracer.py
class SourceTracer:
    """
    娣卞害婧簮绯荤粺
    鑳藉姏: 娌胯缂樺洖婧?路 WHOS璁板綍 路 璁稿彲璇佽拷韪?路 C2PA楠岃瘉 路 鏁板瓧绛惧悕
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.c2pa_verifier = C2PAVerifier()
    
    async def trace(self, doc: Document) -> SourceChain:
        """杩芥函鏁版嵁鏉ユ簮"""
        chain = SourceChain()
        
        # 1. 鐩寸郴鏉ユ簮
        if doc.source_url:
            origin = await self._fetch_origin_page(doc.source_url)
            chain.add(origin)
        
        # 2. 娌胯缂樺弽鏌?
        lineage = await self.bus.lineage_for("document", doc.id)
        chain.add_ancestors(lineage)
        
        # 3. 璁稿彲璇侀獙璇?
        license_info = await self._resolve_license(doc)
        chain.license = license_info
        
        # 4. C2PA楠岃瘉 (鍐呭鐪熷疄鎬?
        c2pa_result = await self.c2pa_verifier.verify(doc.path)
        chain.c2pa = c2pa_result
        
        # 5. 鍒涗綔鑰呬俊鎭?(WHOS)
        whos_info = await self._get_whos_info(doc)
        chain.whos = whos_info
        
        return chain
    
    async def _fetch_origin_page(self, url: str) -> OriginInfo:
        """鑾峰彇鍘熷鏉ユ簮椤甸潰"""
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.get(url, timeout=10) as resp:
                html = await resp.text()
                soup = BeautifulSoup(html, "html.parser")
                return OriginInfo(
                    url=url,
                    title=soup.title.string if soup.title else None,
                    description=soup.find("meta", {"name": "description"}).get("content") if soup.find("meta", {"name": "description"}) else None,
                    author=soup.find("meta", {"name": "author"}).get("content") if soup.find("meta", {"name": "author"}) else None,
                    published_at=self._extract_date(soup)
                )
```


## 绗?2绔?鑷€傚簲鐖櫕鐢熸垚鍣?(瀹屾暣瀹炵幇)

```python
# intelligence/crawler/auto_generator.py (瀹屾暣)
class AutoCrawlerGenerator:
    """
    鑷€傚簲鐖櫕鐢熸垚鍣?鈥?LLM椹卞姩
    娴佺▼: 鎶撳彇鏍锋湰 鈫?LLM鍒嗘瀽DOM 鈫?鐢熸垚閫夋嫨鍣?鈫?楠岃瘉鈮?5% 鈫?娉ㄥ唽
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.llm = get_llm_provider()
        self.crawler_engine = CrawlerEngine()
        self.selector_validator = SelectorValidator()
    
    async def generate(self, seed_url: str, target_count: int = 100) -> CrawlerConfig:
        # 1. 鎶撳彇鏍锋湰
        samples = await self._fetch_samples(seed_url, n=10)
        
        # 2. LLM鍒嗘瀽DOM缁撴瀯
        structure = await self._analyze_structure(samples)
        
        # 3. 鐢熸垚閫夋嫨鍣?
        selectors = await self._generate_selectors(structure)
        
        # 4. 鏋勫缓閰嶇疆
        config = CrawlerConfig(
            name=f"auto_gen_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            channel_type=ChannelType.WEB,
            seed_urls=[seed_url],
            selectors=selectors,
            max_pages=target_count,
            respect_robots_txt=True,
            rate_limit_rps=2.0
        )
        
        # 5. 楠岃瘉
        accuracy = await self._validate(config)
        if accuracy < 0.95:
            raise InsufficientAccuracyError(accuracy)
        
        # 6. 娉ㄥ唽
        await self.crawler_engine.register_channel(config)
        
        return config
    
    async def _analyze_structure(self, samples: List[str]) -> Dict:
        """LLM鍒嗘瀽椤甸潰缁撴瀯"""
        prompt = f"""
        Analyze these {len(samples)} HTML samples and identify:
        1. Main content container CSS selector
        2. Title selector
        3. Author selector
        4. Date selector
        5. Image selectors
        6. Pagination selector
        7. Infinite scroll trigger pattern
        8. Lazy loading trigger pattern
        9. Next page link selector
        
        Samples (truncated to first 5000 chars each):
        {[s[:5000] for s in samples]}
        
        Return JSON with selectors.
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        return json.loads(response)
```

### 23.2 28绫绘剰鍥捐瘑鍒?

```python
# intelligence/agent_commands/intent_classifier.py
class IntentClassifier:
    """
    鎰忓浘鍒嗙被鍣?鈥?28绫绘剰鍥撅紝鍩轰簬LLM + Few-shot + 缂撳瓨
    """
    
    INTENTS = {
        # 鏁版嵁閲囬泦绫?(6)

        "data_export": "鏁版嵁瀵煎嚭",

        "agent_chat": "Agent瀵硅瘽",
        "agent_task": "Agent浠诲姟鎵ц",
        "agent_collab": "Agent鍗忎綔",
        "agent_memory": "Agent璁板繂绠＄悊",
        "agent_skill": "Agent鎶€鑳界鐞?,

        "multimodal_gen": "澶氭ā鎬佺敓鎴?,
        
        # 鏁版嵁鍒嗘瀽绫?(4)
        "redfox_search": "鑷獟浣撴暟鎹悳绱?,
        "trend_analysis": "瓒嬪娍鍒嗘瀽",
        "competitor_analysis": "绔炲搧鍒嗘瀽",
        "sentiment_analysis": "鎯呮劅鍒嗘瀽",
        
        # 鍗忎綔绠＄悊绫?(4)
        "project_manage": "椤圭洰绠＄悊",
        "workflow_manage": "宸ヤ綔娴佺鐞?,
        "team_collab": "鍥㈤槦鍗忎綔",
        "crowdsource_manage": "浼楀寘绠＄悊",
        
        # 绯荤粺绫?(4)
        "system_monitor": "绯荤粺鐩戞帶",
        "system_config": "绯荤粺閰嶇疆",
        "system_audit": "绯荤粺瀹¤",
        "system_governance": "AI娌荤悊"
    }
    
    def __init__(self, llm_provider: LLMProvider, cache: TTLCache):
        self.llm = llm_provider
        self.cache = cache
        self.few_shot_examples = self._load_few_shot_examples()
    
    async def classify(self, text: str, context: Dict = None) -> IntentResult:
        """鍒嗙被鐢ㄦ埛杈撳叆"""
        # 缂撳瓨妫€鏌?
        cache_key = f"intent:{hash(text)}"
        if cached := self.cache.get(cache_key):
            return cached
        
        # 鏋勫缓Prompt
        prompt = self._build_prompt(text, context)
        
        # LLM璋冪敤
        response = await self.llm.complete(
            prompt=prompt,
            response_format="json",
            temperature=0.1
        )
        
        result = IntentResult(**json.loads(response))
        result.raw_text = text
        result.confidence_score = self._calculate_confidence(result)
        
        # 缂撳瓨
        self.cache.set(cache_key, result, ttl=3600)
        
        return result
    
    def _build_prompt(self, text: str, context: Dict) -> str:
        return f"""
        You are an intent classification system for Magic-Octopus-Data-Verse, an AI data platform.
        
        Classify the following user request into one of {len(self.INTENTS)} intents:
        {json.dumps(self.INTENTS, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)}
        
        User request: "{text}"
        Context: {context}
        
        Return JSON:
        {{
            "primary_intent": "intent_name",
            "confidence": 0.0-1.0,
            "entities": {{"entity_type": "value", "count": 0, "filters": {{}}}},
            "clarifying_questions": [] if confident else ["question1", "question2"]
        }}
        
        Few-shot examples:
        {self.few_shot_examples}
        """
```

# intelligence/agent_commands/intent_classifier.py
class IntentClassifier:
    """鎰忓浘鍒嗙被鍣?鈥?鏄犲皠鍒?17涓兘鍔?""
    
    # 鎰忓浘鍒拌兘鍔涘眰鐨勬槧灏?
    INTENT_TO_LAYER = {
        # 閲囬泦绫绘剰鍥?鈫?閲囬泦灞傝兘鍔?
        "data_acquisition": "collect",
        "crawl_images": "collect",
        "import_dataset": "collect",
        "upload_data": "collect",
        
        # 娓呮礂绫绘剰鍥?鈫?娓呮礂灞傝兘鍔?
        "data_cleaning": "clean",
        "clean_images": "clean",
        "clean_videos": "clean",
        "clean_text": "clean",
        
        # 鍘婚噸绫绘剰鍥?鈫?鍘婚噸灞傝兘鍔?
        "dedupe_data": "dedupe",
        "dedupe_images": "dedupe",
        "semantic_dedupe": "dedupe",
        
        # 鍚堟垚绫绘剰鍥?鈫?鍚堟垚灞傝兘鍔?
        "text_to_image": "synth",
        "image_to_image": "synth",
        "image_edit": "synth",
        "text_to_video": "synth",
        "image_to_video": "synth",
        "multi_image_to_video": "synth",
        "text_to_3d": "synth",
        "image_to_3d": "synth",
        "synthesize_audio": "synth",
        "synthesize_text": "synth",
        "synthesize_agent": "synth",
        "synthesize_multimodal": "synth",
        
        # 鏍囨敞绫绘剰鍥?鈫?鏍囨敞灞傝兘鍔?
        "annotation": "label",
        "auto_label": "label",
        "human_label": "label",
        "consensus_label": "label",
        
        # 璐ㄦ绫绘剰鍥?鈫?璐ㄦ灞傝兘鍔?
        "quality_check": "qc",
        "aql_sampling": "qc",
        "qc_report": "qc",
        
        # 瀵煎嚭绫绘剰鍥?鈫?瀵煎嚭灞傝兘鍔?
        "export_data": "export",
        "export_pretrain": "export",
        "export_sft": "export",
        "export_dpo": "export",
        "export_lora": "export",
        
        # 鐗堟湰绫绘剰鍥?鈫?鐗堟湰绠＄悊鑳藉姏
        "version_manage": "version",
        "rollback": "version",
        
        # 琛€缂樼被鎰忓浘 鈫?琛€缂樼鐞嗚兘鍔?
        "lineage_query": "lineage",
        "impact_analysis": "lineage"
    }
    
    async def resolve_capability(self, intent: str, entities: Dict) -> str:
        """鏍规嵁鎰忓浘鍜屽疄浣撹В鏋愬叿浣撹兘鍔汭D"""
        layer = self.INTENT_TO_LAYER.get(intent)
        if not layer:
            return None
        
        # 鏍规嵁瀹炰綋鍜屽弬鏁板尮閰嶅叿浣撹兘鍔?
        # 渚嬪: intent="data_acquisition", entities={"model_type": "t2i", "phase": "sft", "source": "crawl"}
        # 鈫?"collect.t2i.sft.crawl"
        return self._match_capability(layer, entities)

# intelligence/agent_commands/command_parser.py
class CommandParser:
    """
    鍛戒护瑙ｆ瀽鍣?鈥?灏嗚嚜鐒惰瑷€杞崲涓虹粨鏋勫寲鍛戒护
    姣忎釜鎰忓浘瀵瑰簲涓€涓狫SON Schema
    """
    
    COMMAND_SCHEMAS = {
        "data_acquisition": {
            "type": "object",
            "required": ["entity", "count"],
            "properties": {
                "entity": {"type": "string", "enum": ["image", "video", "text", "audio", "multimodal", "3d", "panoptic"]},
                "sub_entity": {"type": "string", "enum": ["natural_image", "medical", "satellite", "face", "object"]},
                "category": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
                "count": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 1, "maximum": 10000000},
                "filters": {
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "min_size": {"type": "string", "pattern": "^\\d+x\\d+$"},
                        "max_size": {"type": "string", "pattern": "^\\d+x\\d+$"},
                        "no_watermark": {"type": "boolean"},
                        "quality_threshold": {"type": "number", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 1},
                        "language": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
                        "license": {"type": "string", "enum": ["cc-by", "cc-by-sa", "public-domain", "apache", "internal"]},
                        "min_duration": {"type": "number"},
                        "max_duration": {"type": "number"},
                        "min_frames": {"type": "integer"},
                        "max_frames": {"type": "integer"},
                        "min_resolution": {"type": "string"},
                        "max_resolution": {"type": "string"},
                        "no_nsfw": {"type": "boolean"},
                        "no_people": {"type": "boolean"},
                        "with_people": {"type": "boolean"},
                        "min_sharpness": {"type": "number"},
                        "min_aesthetic": {"type": "number"}
                    }
                },
                "channels": {
                    "type": "array",
                    "items": {"type": "string", "enum": [
                        "google_images", "open_images", "flickr", "unsplash", "pixabay",
                        "reddit", "twitter", "xiaohongshu", "douyin", "bilibili",
                        "youtube", "arxiv", "pubmed", "github", "huggingface"
                    ]}
                },
                "compliance": {"type": "string", "enum": ["strict", "internal", "audit", "research"]},
                "output_format": {"type": "string", "enum": ["raw", "structured", "embedding"]},
                "auto_label": {"type": "boolean", "default": True},
                "auto_clean": {"type": "boolean", "default": True},
                "auto_score": {"type": "boolean", "default": True}
            }
        },
        "short_drama": {
            "type": "object",
            "required": ["title", "genre"],
            "properties": {
                "title": {"type": "string", "maxLength": 50},
                "genre": {"type": "string", "enum": ["鐜勫够", "浠欎緺", "閮藉競", "鐢滃疇", "绉戝够", "鎮枒", "鍠滃墽", "瑷€鎯?, "绌胯秺", "閲嶇敓"]},
                "style": {"type": "string", "enum": ["鐪熶汉鍐欏疄", "鐪熶汉濂抽鐢滃疇", "鏃ユ湰鍔ㄦ极", "3D_CG", "鐜勫够鍘氭秱", "姘村ⅷ椋?, "璧涘崥鏈嬪厠"]},
                "episodes": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 1, "maximum": 100},
                "duration_per_episode": {"type": "integer", "minimum": 30, "maximum": 300},
                "characters": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
                "plot": {"type": "string", "maxLength": 1000},
                "tone": {"type": "string", "enum": ["杞绘澗", "涓ヨ們", "鎰熶汉", "鎮枒", "骞介粯", "鐑"]},
                "target_audience": {"type": "string", "enum": ["濂虫€?, "鐢锋€?, "閫氱敤"]}
            }
        },
        "agent_collab": {
            "type": "object",
            "required": ["action"],
            "properties": {
                "action": {"type": "string", "enum": [
                    "create_bot", "create_channel", "create_matter", 
                    "assign_matter", "run_collab", "review_matter"
                ]},
                "bot_name": {"type": "string"},
                "bot_capabilities": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
                "channel_name": {"type": "string"},
                "channel_members": {"type": "array", "items": {"type": "string"}},
                "matter_title": {"type": "string"},
                "matter_deliverable": {"type": "object"},
                "collab_mode": {"type": "string", "enum": ["solo", "roundtable", "critic", "pipeline", "split", "swarm"]}
            }
        },
        # 鏇村Schema...
    }
    
    async def parse(self, text: str, intent: IntentResult) -> Command:
        """瑙ｆ瀽鑷劧璇█涓虹粨鏋勫寲鍛戒护"""
        schema = self.COMMAND_SCHEMAS.get(intent.primary_intent)
        if not schema:
            return await self._dynamic_extract(text, intent)
        
        prompt = f"""
        Extract structured parameters from the user request.
        Schema: {json.dumps(schema, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)}
        Request: "{text}"
        Intent: {intent.primary_intent}
        
        Return JSON matching the schema. Use default values when applicable.
        """
        
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        params = json.loads(response)
        
        return Command(
            intent=intent.primary_intent,
            action=intent.sub_intent,
            params=params,
            raw_text=text,
            session_id=intent.session_id
        )

### 23.4 浼氳瘽绠＄悊鍣?(SessionManager)

```python
# intelligence/agent_commands/session_manager.py
class SessionManager:
    """
    浼氳瘽绠＄悊鍣?鈥?绠＄悊Agent瀵硅瘽鐨勭姸鎬併€佸巻鍙层€佷笂涓嬫枃
    鏀寔澶氳疆瀵硅瘽銆佽法浼氳瘽璁板繂銆佷笂涓嬫枃鎽樿銆佽蹇嗗帇缂?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.sessions = {}  # session_id -> Session
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.memory_store = AgentMemoryStore()
        self.context_compressor = ContextCompressor()
        self.max_history = 100
        self.max_tokens = 8000
    
    async def create_session(self, user_id: str, context: Dict = None) -> Session:
        """鍒涘缓鏂颁細璇?""
        session = Session(
            id=f"sess_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:16]}",
            user_id=user_id,
            history=[],
            context=context or {},
            memory=await self.memory_store.load(user_id),
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            last_activity=datetime.now(),
            status="active"
        )
        self.sessions[session.id] = session
        await self._save_session_to_db(session)
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="agent.session_created",
            entity_type="agent_session",
            entity_id=session.id,
            payload={"user_id": user_id}
        )
        
        return session
    
    async def add_message(self, session_id: str, role: str, content: str,
                          attachments: List[str] = None,
                          metadata: Dict = None) -> str:
        """娣诲姞娑堟伅鍒颁細璇?""
        session = self.sessions.get(session_id)
        if not session:
            raise ValueError(f"Session {session_id} not found")
        
        message = Message(
            id=f"msg_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            role=role,  # user/assistant/system/tool
            content=content,
            attachments=attachments or [],
            metadata=metadata or {},
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )
        session.history.append(message)
        session.last_activity = datetime.now()
        
        # 鍘嗗彶璁板綍瓒呴檺 鈫?鍘嬬缉
        if self._should_compress(session):
            session.history = await self.context_compressor.compress(session.history)
            session.context["compressed"] = True
            session.context["compressed_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
        
        await self._update_session_in_db(session)
        
        # 鏇存柊闀挎湡璁板繂
        if role == "assistant" and len(content) > 100:
            await self._extract_and_store_memory(session, content)
        
        return message.id
    
    async def get_context(self, session_id: str, limit: int = 20) -> Dict:
        """鑾峰彇褰撳墠浼氳瘽鐨勫畬鏁翠笂涓嬫枃"""
        session = self.sessions.get(session_id)
        if not session:
            return {}
        
        return {
            "history": [m.to_dict() for m in session.history[-limit:]],
            "memory": session.memory,
            "context": session.context,
            "user_id": session.user_id,
            "active_tasks": await self._get_active_tasks(session_id),
            "current_intent": session.context.get("current_intent"),
            "last_action": session.context.get("last_action")
        }
    
    async def update_memory(self, session_id: str, key: str, value: Any):
        """鏇存柊Agent鐨勯暱鏈熻蹇?""
        session = self.sessions.get(session_id)
        if not session:
            return
        
        session.memory[key] = value
        await self.memory_store.save(session.user_id, key, value)
        
        # 鏇存柊鍚戦噺绱㈠紩
        await self._index_memory(session.user_id, key, value)
        
        await self._update_session_in_db(session)
    
    async def _extract_and_store_memory(self, session: Session, content: str):
        """浠庡璇濅腑鎻愬彇骞跺瓨鍌ㄩ暱鏈熻蹇?""
        # 浣跨敤LLM鎻愬彇鍏抽敭淇℃伅
        prompt = f"""
        Extract key information from this conversation response that should be remembered:
        {content}
        
        Return JSON with keys: topics, preferences, decisions, facts
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        memory_data = json.loads(response)
        
        for key, value in memory_data.items():
            if value:
                await self.update_memory(session.id, key, value)
    
    def _should_compress(self, session: Session) -> bool:
        """鍒ゆ柇鏄惁闇€瑕佸帇缂╀笂涓嬫枃"""
        # 瓒呰繃100鏉℃秷鎭垨鎬籺oken瓒呰繃8000
        return len(session.history) > self.max_history or \
               self._estimate_tokens(session.history) > self.max_tokens
    
    async def close_session(self, session_id: str) -> bool:
        """鍏抽棴浼氳瘽"""
        session = self.sessions.get(session_id)
        if not session:
            return False
        
        session.status = "closed"
        session.closed_at = datetime.now()
        await self._update_session_in_db(session)
        del self.sessions[session_id]
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="agent.session_closed",
            entity_type="agent_session",
            entity_id=session_id,
            payload={"user_id": session.user_id}
        )
        
        return True
```

### 23.5 鍛戒护璺敱鍣?(CommandRouter)

```python
# intelligence/agent_commands/command_router.py
class CommandRouter:
    """
    鍛戒护璺敱鍣?鈥?灏嗙粨鏋勫寲鍛戒护璺敱鍒板搴旂殑Agent
    鏀寔鍚屾/寮傛鎵ц銆佷换鍔＄紪鎺掋€佽繘搴﹁拷韪€佸閿?
    """
    
    AGENT_MAP = {
        # 鏁版嵁绫?
        "data_acquisition": DataAcquisitionAgent,
        "data_cleaning": CleaningAgent,
        "data_labeling": AnnotationAgent,
        "data_quality": QualityAgent,
        "data_export": ExportAgent,
        "data_version": VersionAgent,
        
        # Agent绫?
        "agent_chat": ChatAgent,
        "agent_task": TaskAgent,
        "agent_collab": OctoAgent,
        "agent_memory": MemoryAgent,
        "agent_skill": SkillAgent,
        
        # 鍒涙剰绫?
        "short_drama": ShortDramaAgent,
        "video_gen": VideoAgent,
        "image_gen": ImageAgent,
        "comfy_workflow": ComfyAgent,
        "multimodal_gen": MultiModalAgent,
        
        # 鍒嗘瀽绫?
        "redfox_search": RedFoxAgent,
        "trend_analysis": TrendAgent,
        "competitor_analysis": CompetitorAgent,
        "sentiment_analysis": SentimentAgent,
        
        # 鍗忎綔绫?
        "project_manage": ProjectAgent,
        "workflow_manage": WorkflowAgent,
        "team_collab": TeamAgent,
        "crowdsource_manage": CrowdsourceAgent,
        
        # 绯荤粺绫?
        "system_monitor": MonitorAgent,
        "system_config": ConfigAgent,
        "system_audit": AuditAgent,
        "system_governance": MetaKimAgent
    }
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.active_tasks = {}
        self.task_queue = asyncio.Queue()
        self.worker_pool = AsyncPool(max_workers=20)
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def route(self, command: Command, session: Session) -> TaskResult:
        """璺敱鍛戒护鍒板搴旂殑Agent (鍚屾鎵ц)"""
        agent_class = self.AGENT_MAP.get(command.intent)
        if not agent_class:
            return TaskResult(
                status="failed",
                error=f"No agent found for intent: {command.intent}"
            )
        
        agent = agent_class(session=session)
        task_id = await self._start_task(command, session)
        
        try:
            result = await agent.handle(command)
            await self._complete_task(task_id, result)
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            await self._fail_task(task_id, str(e))
            return TaskResult(status="failed", error=str(e))
    
    async def route_async(self, command: Command, session: Session) -> str:
        """寮傛璺敱 鈥?鐢ㄤ簬闀挎椂闂翠换鍔?""
        task_id = await self._start_task(command, session)
        
        # 鏀惧叆浠诲姟闃熷垪
        await self.task_queue.put({
            "task_id": task_id,
            "command": command,
            "session": session
        })
        
        # 鍚姩宸ヤ綔绾跨▼
        asyncio.create_task(self._worker_loop())
        
        return task_id
    
    async def _worker_loop(self):
        """鍚庡彴宸ヤ綔绾跨▼寰幆"""
        while True:
            try:
                item = await self.task_queue.get()
                await self._run_async_task(
                    item["task_id"],
                    item["command"],
                    item["session"]
                )
            except Exception as e:
                logging.error(f"Worker error: {e}")
    
    async def _run_async_task(self, task_id: str, command: Command, session: Session):
        """寮傛鎵ц浠诲姟骞舵洿鏂拌繘搴?""
        agent_class = self.AGENT_MAP.get(command.intent)
        agent = agent_class(session=session)
        
        try:
            # 鍒涘缓杩涘害娴?
            progress_stream = ProgressStream(task_id)
            
            # 鎵цAgent (鏀寔娴佸紡杩涘害)
            result = await agent.handle_with_progress(command, progress_stream)
            
            # 鎺ㄩ€佸畬鎴愪簨浠?
            await self._complete_task(task_id, result)
            await progress_stream.finish(result)
            
        except Exception as e:
            await self._fail_task(task_id, str(e))
    
    async def get_task_status(self, task_id: str) -> Dict:
        """鑾峰彇浠诲姟鐘舵€?""
        task = self.active_tasks.get(task_id)
        if not task:
            return {"status": "not_found"}
        
        return {
            "task_id": task_id,
            "status": task["status"],
            "progress": task.get("progress", 0),
            "started_at": task["started_at"],
            "completed_at": task.get("completed_at"),
            "result": task.get("result"),
            "error": task.get("error")
        }
    
    async def cancel_task(self, task_id: str) -> bool:
        """鍙栨秷浠诲姟"""
        task = self.active_tasks.get(task_id)
        if not task:
            return False
        
        if task["status"] in ["completed", "failed", "cancelled"]:
            return False
        
        task["status"] = "cancelled"
        task["cancelled_at"] = datetime.now()
        return True
```

### 24.2 DataAcquisitionAgent 鈥?鏁版嵁閲囬泦Agent (瀹屾暣瀹炵幇)

```python
# intelligence/platform_agents/data_acquisition_agent.py
class DataAcquisitionAgent:
    """
    鏁版嵁閲囬泦Agent 鈥?璐熻矗鏅鸿兘鏁版嵁閲囬泦鍏ㄦ祦绋?
    鑳藉姏: 鎰忓浘鐞嗚В 鈫?娓犻亾閫夋嫨 鈫?浠诲姟瑙勫垝 鈫?鎵ц閲囬泦 鈫?澶勭悊 鈫?浜や粯
    """
    
    def __init__(self, session: Session = None):
        self.session = session
        self.crawler_engine = CrawlerEngine()
        self.dedupe_engine = DedupeEngine()
        self.cleaning_engine = CleaningEngine()
        self.label_engine = AutoLabelEngine()
        self.scoring_engine = ScoringEngine()
        self.dataset_manager = DatasetManager()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def handle(self, command: Command) -> TaskResult:
        """澶勭悊閲囬泦鍛戒护"""
        params = command.params
        intent = command.intent
        
        if intent == "data_acquisition":
            return await self._handle_acquisition(params)
        elif intent == "data_cleaning":
            return await self._handle_cleaning(params)
        elif intent == "data_labeling":
            return await self._handle_labeling(params)
        else:
            return TaskResult(status="failed", error=f"Unknown intent: {intent}")
    
    async def _handle_acquisition(self, params: Dict) -> TaskResult:
        """澶勭悊鏁版嵁閲囬泦"""
        entity = params.get("entity", "image")
        count = params.get("count", 1000)
        channels = params.get("channels", [])
        filters = params.get("filters", {})
        output_format = params.get("output_format", "raw")
        
        # 1. 鑷姩閫夋嫨娓犻亾 (濡傛灉鏈寚瀹?
        if not channels:
            channels = self._auto_select_channels(entity, filters)
        
        # 2. 鍒涘缓閲囬泦浠诲姟
        job_id = await self.crawler_engine.start_crawl(
            CrawlerConfig(
                name=f"agent_acquisition_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
                channel_type=channels[0],  # 涓绘笭閬?
                seed_urls=[],  # 鐢盇gent鑷姩鐢熸垚
                max_pages=count,
                cleaning_rules=filters,
                label_schema=params.get("auto_label") and self._build_label_schema(entity),
                scoring_dimensions=params.get("auto_score") and ["quality", "aesthetic"],
                owner=self.session.user_id if self.session else None
            )
        )
        
        # 3. 瀹炴椂鐩戞帶杩涘害 (閫氳繃WebSocket鎺ㄩ€?
        if self.session:
            await self._monitor_and_notify(job_id)
        
        # 4. 閲囬泦瀹屾垚鍚庤嚜鍔ㄥ鐞?
        result = await self._wait_for_completion(job_id)
        
        # 5. 鍒涘缓鏁版嵁闆?
        dataset_id = None
        if result["status"] == "completed" and result["results"]:
            dataset = await self.dataset_manager.create_dataset(
                name=f"閲囬泦_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}",
                modality=entity,
                project_id=params.get("project_id")
            )
            # 瀵煎叆閲囬泦鐨勬暟鎹?
            await self.dataset_manager.import_data(
                dataset_id=dataset.id,
                source_type="crawler",
                source_config={"job_id": job_id}
            )
            dataset_id = dataset.id
        
        return TaskResult(
            status=result["status"],
            result={
                "job_id": job_id,
                "dataset_id": dataset_id,
                "total_collected": result.get("results_count", 0),
                "channels_used": channels
            }
        )
    
    def _auto_select_channels(self, entity: str, filters: Dict) -> List[str]:
        """鏍规嵁瀹炰綋绫诲瀷鍜岃繃婊ゆ潯浠惰嚜鍔ㄩ€夋嫨閲囬泦娓犻亾"""
        channel_map = {
            "image": ["google_images", "open_images", "flickr", "unsplash", "pixabay"],
            "video": ["youtube", "bilibili", "tiktok", "vimeo"],
            "text": ["arxiv", "pubmed", "github", "wikipedia"],
            "audio": ["youtube", "music"],
            "multimodal": ["huggingface", "open_images", "github"]
        }
        
        channels = channel_map.get(entity, ["google_images"])
        
        # 鏍规嵁杩囨护鏉′欢璋冩暣
        if filters.get("license") == "internal":
            channels = ["internal_asset"]  # 鍐呴儴璧勪骇浼樺厛
        elif filters.get("language"):
            if "zh" in filters.get("language", []):
                channels = ["bilibili", "xiaohongshu", "douyin", "baidu"]
        
        return channels
    
    async def _monitor_and_notify(self, job_id: str):
        """鐩戞帶閲囬泦杩涘害骞堕€氳繃WebSocket鎺ㄩ€?""
        # 閫氳繃EventBus璁㈤槄閲囬泦杩涘害浜嬩欢
        async def on_progress(event):
            await self.session.ws.send({
                "type": "progress",
                "job_id": job_id,
                "progress": event["progress"],
                "total": event["total"]
            })
        
        self.bus.subscribe(f"crawler.progress.{job_id}", on_progress)
    
    async def handle_with_progress(self, command: Command, 
                                   progress_stream: ProgressStream) -> TaskResult:
        """甯﹁繘搴︽祦鐨勫鐞?""
        await progress_stream.send({"status": "started", "message": "寮€濮嬮噰闆嗕换鍔?})
        
        # 鎵ц閲囬泦
        result = await self._handle_acquisition(command.params)
        
        # 鍙戦€佹渶缁堣繘搴?
        await progress_stream.send({"status": "completed", "result": result})
        
        return result
```

### 24.3 AnnotationAgent 鈥?鏍囨敞Agent

```python
# intelligence/platform_agents/annotation_agent.py
class AnnotationAgent:
    """
    鏍囨敞Agent 鈥?璐熻矗鏅鸿兘鏍囨敞鍏ㄦ祦绋?
    鑳藉姏: 浠诲姟鍒嗛厤銆丄I棰勬爣銆佽繘搴︾洃鎺с€佽川閲忔帶鍒?
    """
    
    def __init__(self, session: Session = None):
        self.session = session
        self.workbench_engine = WorkbenchEngine()
        self.crowdsource_manager = CrowdsourceManager()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def handle(self, command: Command) -> TaskResult:
        params = command.params
        
        if command.action == "create_tasks":
            return await self._create_tasks(params)
        elif command.action == "ai_prelabel":
            return await self._ai_prelabel(params)
        elif command.action == "assign":
            return await self._assign_tasks(params)
        elif command.action == "monitor":
            return await self._monitor_progress(params)
        else:
            return TaskResult(status="failed", error=f"Unknown action: {command.action}")
    
    async def _create_tasks(self, params: Dict) -> TaskResult:
        """鍒涘缓鏍囨敞浠诲姟"""
        dataset_id = params.get("dataset_id")
        count = params.get("count", 1000)
        geometry_type = params.get("geometry_type", "rect")
        label_schema = params.get("label_schema", {})
        
        # 鑾峰彇鏁版嵁闆嗚祫浜?
        assets = await self.dataset_manager.get_assets(dataset_id)
        selected_assets = assets[:count]
        
        # 鍒涘缓鏁版嵁鍖?
        pack = await self.pack_engine.create_task_pack(
            name=f"鏍囨敞浠诲姟_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}",
            asset_ids=[a.id for a in selected_assets],
            geometry_type=geometry_type,
            label_schema=label_schema
        )
        
        # 濡傛灉鍚敤AI棰勬爣
        if params.get("ai_prelabel", False):
            await self._ai_prelabel({"pack_id": pack.id})
        
        # 鍒嗛厤浠诲姟
        if params.get("assignees"):
            await self._assign_tasks({
                "pack_id": pack.id,
                "assignees": params["assignees"]
            })
        
        return TaskResult(
            status="success",
            result={"pack_id": pack.id, "total_tasks": len(selected_assets)}
        )
    
    async def _ai_prelabel(self, params: Dict) -> TaskResult:
        """AI棰勬爣"""
        pack_id = params.get("pack_id")
        model = params.get("model", "sam")
        
        # 鑾峰彇鏁版嵁鍖呰祫浜?
        pack = await self.pack_engine.get_pack(pack_id)
        assets = await self.asset_manager.get_assets(pack.asset_ids)
        
        prelabeled = []
        for asset in assets:
            if asset.file_type == "image":
                if model == "sam":
                    annotations = await self._sam_predict(asset)
                elif model == "grounding_dino":
                    annotations = await self._grounding_dino_predict(asset, params.get("text_prompt"))
                else:
                    continue
                
                prelabeled.append({
                    "asset_id": asset.id,
                    "annotations": annotations,
                    "model": model
                })
        
        # 淇濆瓨棰勬爣缁撴灉
        for result in prelabeled:
            await self.workbench_engine.save_annotation(
                pack_id=pack_id,
                worker_id="ai_prelabel",
                annotations=result["annotations"]
            )
        
        return TaskResult(
            status="success",
            result={"prelabeled_count": len(prelabeled)}
        )
    
    async def _assign_tasks(self, params: Dict) -> TaskResult:
        """鍒嗛厤浠诲姟缁欐爣娉ㄥ憳"""
        pack_id = params.get("pack_id")
        assignees = params.get("assignees", [])
        strategy = params.get("strategy", "by_skill")
        
        # 鑾峰彇鏁版嵁鍖?
        pack = await self.pack_engine.get_pack(pack_id)
        
        # 鍒嗛厤绛栫暐
        if strategy == "by_skill":
            # 鎸夋妧鑳藉尮閰嶅害鍒嗛厤
            assignments = await self._assign_by_skill(pack, assignees)
        elif strategy == "by_workload":
            # 鎸夎礋杞藉潎琛″垎閰?
            assignments = await self._assign_by_workload(pack, assignees)
        elif strategy == "random":
            # 闅忔満鍒嗛厤
            assignments = await self._assign_random(pack, assignees)
        else:
            # 娣峰悎绛栫暐
            assignments = await self._assign_hybrid(pack, assignees)
        
        return TaskResult(
            status="success",
            result={"assignments": assignments}
        )
```

### 24.4 OctoAgent 鈥?Agent鍗忎綔Agent

```python
# intelligence/platform_agents/octo_agent.py
class OctoAgent:
    """
    Octo鍗忎綔Agent 鈥?璐熻矗Agent鍗忎綔缃戠粶绠＄悊
    鑳藉姏: Bot绠＄悊銆丆hannel绠＄悊銆丮atter绠＄悊銆佸崗浣滄ā寮忔墽琛?
    """
    
    def __init__(self, session: Session = None):
        self.session = session
        self.octo_engine = OctoEngine()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def handle(self, command: Command) -> TaskResult:
        params = command.params
        
        if command.action == "create_bot":
            return await self._create_bot(params)
        elif command.action == "create_channel":
            return await self._create_channel(params)
        elif command.action == "create_matter":
            return await self._create_matter(params)
        elif command.action == "run_collab":
            return await self._run_collaboration(params)
        elif command.action == "review_matter":
            return await self._review_matter(params)
        else:
            return TaskResult(status="failed", error=f"Unknown action: {command.action}")
    
    async def _create_bot(self, params: Dict) -> TaskResult:
        """鍒涘缓Agent Bot"""
        bot = await self.octo_engine.create_bot(
            name=params.get("name", "Unnamed Bot"),
            agent_type=params.get("agent_type", "generic"),
            capabilities=params.get("capabilities", []),
            system_prompt=params.get("system_prompt")
        )
        
        return TaskResult(status="success", result={"bot_id": bot.id})
    
    async def _create_channel(self, params: Dict) -> TaskResult:
        """鍒涘缓鍗忎綔棰戦亾"""
        channel = await self.octo_engine.create_channel(
            name=params.get("name", "New Channel"),
            description=params.get("description", ""),
            members=params.get("members", []),
            project_id=params.get("project_id")
        )
        
        return TaskResult(status="success", result={"channel_id": channel.id})
    
    async def _create_matter(self, params: Dict) -> TaskResult:
        """鍒涘缓浜や粯鐗?""
        matter = await self.octo_engine.create_matter(
            channel_id=params.get("channel_id"),
            title=params.get("title", "New Matter"),
            assignee_type=params.get("assignee_type", "user"),
            assignee_id=params.get("assignee_id"),
            deliverable=params.get("deliverable", {}),
            acceptance_criteria=params.get("acceptance_criteria", [])
        )
        
        return TaskResult(status="success", result={"matter_id": matter.id})
    
    async def _run_collaboration(self, params: Dict) -> TaskResult:
        """鎵ц鍗忎綔妯″紡"""
        matter_id = params.get("matter_id")
        mode = params.get("mode", "solo")
        
        result = await self.octo_engine.run_collaboration(matter_id, mode)
        
        return TaskResult(
            status="success",
            result={"mode": mode, "result": result}
        )
```


## 绗?5绔?Agent鍗忎綔缃戠粶 (Octo瀹屾暣瀹炵幇)

### 25.1 鏍稿績姒傚康

### 25.2 Bot绠＄悊瀹炵幇

```python
# engines/octo_engine.py (Bot閮ㄥ垎)
class OctoEngine:
    """Agent鍗忎綔寮曟搸 鈥?Bot/Channel/Matter绠＄悊"""
    
    # ============ Bot 绠＄悊 ============
    async def create_bot(self, name: str, agent_type: str, 
                         capabilities: List[str], 
                         system_prompt: str = None) -> AgentBot:
        """鍒涘缓涓€涓狝gent Bot"""
        bot = AgentBot(
            id=f"bot_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            name=name,
            agent_type=agent_type,
            capabilities=capabilities,
            agent_card=AgentCard(
                owner="system",
                ability_description=f"鎿呴暱: {', '.join(capabilities)}",
                work_history=[]
            ),
            status="active",
            system_prompt=system_prompt or self._default_prompt(agent_type),
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.bots[bot.id] = bot
        await self._save_bot_to_db(bot)
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="octo.bot_created",
            entity_type="agent_bot",
            entity_id=bot.id,
            payload={"name": name, "agent_type": agent_type}
        )
        
        return bot
    
    async def assign_skill_to_bot(self, bot_id: str, skill_id: str) -> bool:
        """涓築ot鍒嗛厤鎶€鑳?""
        if bot_id not in self.bots:
            return False
        
        skill = await self.skill_engine.get_skill(skill_id)
        if not skill:
            return False
        
        self.bots[bot_id].capabilities.append(skill_id)
        self.bots[bot_id].agent_card.ability_description += f"\n- 鎶€鑳? {skill.name}"
        await self._update_bot_in_db(self.bots[bot_id])
        return True
    
    def _default_prompt(self, agent_type: str) -> str:
        """榛樿绯荤粺鎻愮ず璇?""
        prompts = {
            "coder": "浣犳槸涓€涓笓涓氱殑浠ｇ爜寮€鍙戝姪鎵嬶紝鎿呴暱Python銆丣avaScript銆乀ypeScript銆?,
            "reviewer": "浣犳槸涓€涓弗鏍肩殑浠ｇ爜瀹℃煡鑰咃紝鍏虫敞浠ｇ爜璐ㄩ噺銆佸畨鍏ㄦ€с€佸彲缁存姢鎬с€?,
            "writer": "浣犳槸涓€涓笓涓氱殑鍐呭鍒涗綔鑰咃紝鎿呴暱鎶€鏈枃妗ｃ€佽惀閿€鏂囨銆佸崥瀹㈡枃绔犮€?,
            "analyst": "浣犳槸涓€涓暟鎹垎鏋愪笓瀹讹紝鎿呴暱鏁版嵁澶勭悊銆佺粺璁″垎鏋愩€佸彲瑙嗗寲銆?,
            "researcher": "浣犳槸涓€涓爺绌跺姪鎵嬶紝鎿呴暱鏂囩尞妫€绱€佷俊鎭暣鐞嗐€佺爺绌舵姤鍛娿€?,
            "generic": "浣犳槸涓€涓€氱敤鐨凙I鍔╂墜锛屼箰浜庡府鍔╃敤鎴峰畬鎴愬悇绉嶄换鍔°€?
        }
        return prompts.get(agent_type, prompts["generic"])
```

### 25.3 Channel绠＄悊瀹炵幇

```python
# engines/octo_engine.py (Channel閮ㄥ垎)
    # ============ Channel 绠＄悊 ============
    async def create_channel(self, name: str, description: str,
                             members: List[str], project_id: str = None) -> Channel:
        """鍒涘缓涓€涓崗浣滈閬?(绫讳技椤圭洰缇?"""
        channel = Channel(
            id=f"chan_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            name=name,
            description=description,
            members=members,  # 鍙互鏄?user_id 鎴?bot_id
            threads=[],
            project_id=project_id,
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.channels[channel.id] = channel
        await self._save_channel_to_db(channel)
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="octo.channel_created",
            entity_type="agent_channel",
            entity_id=channel.id,
            payload={"name": name, "members": members}
        )
        
        return channel
    
    async def add_member_to_channel(self, channel_id: str, member_id: str) -> bool:
        """鍚戦閬撴坊鍔犳垚鍛?(浜烘垨Bot)"""
        if channel_id not in self.channels:
            return False
        if member_id not in self.channels[channel_id].members:
            self.channels[channel_id].members.append(member_id)
            await self._update_channel_in_db(self.channels[channel_id])
        return True
    
    async def remove_member_from_channel(self, channel_id: str, member_id: str) -> bool:
        """浠庨閬撶Щ闄ゆ垚鍛?""
        if channel_id not in self.channels:
            return False
        if member_id in self.channels[channel_id].members:
            self.channels[channel_id].members.remove(member_id)
            await self._update_channel_in_db(self.channels[channel_id])
        return True
```

### 25.4 Matter绠＄悊瀹炵幇

```python
# engines/octo_engine.py (Matter閮ㄥ垎)
    # ============ Matter 绠＄悊 ============
    async def create_matter(self, channel_id: str, title: str,
                            assignee_type: str, assignee_id: str,
                            deliverable: Dict, acceptance_criteria: List[str]) -> Matter:
        """鍒涘缓涓€涓氦浠樼墿 (鎶婅亰澶╁彉鎴愯鍔?"""
        if channel_id not in self.channels:
            raise ValueError(f"Channel {channel_id} not found")
        
        matter = Matter(
            id=f"mat_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            channel_id=channel_id,
            title=title,
            assignee_type=assignee_type,  # "user" or "bot"
            assignee_id=assignee_id,
            deliverable=deliverable,
            acceptance_criteria=acceptance_criteria,
            status="draft",
            created_at=datetime.now(),
            updated_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.matters[matter.id] = matter
        
        # 娣诲姞鍒癈hannel鐨凾hread
        thread = Thread(
            id=f"thr_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            title=title,
            messages=[{
                "role": "system",
                "content": f"鍒涘缓浜哅atter: {title}",
                "timestamp": datetime.now()
            }]
        )
        self.channels[channel_id].threads.append(thread)
        
        await self._save_matter_to_db(matter)
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="octo.matter_created",
            entity_type="agent_matter",
            entity_id=matter.id,
            payload={"title": title, "assignee": assignee_id}
        )
        
        return matter
    
    async def assign_matter(self, matter_id: str, assignee_id: str) -> bool:
        """鍒嗛厤浜や粯鐗╃粰鎸囧畾鐨勪汉鎴朆ot"""
        if matter_id not in self.matters:
            return False
        self.matters[matter_id].assignee_id = assignee_id
        self.matters[matter_id].status = "assigned"
        self.matters[matter_id].updated_at = datetime.now()
        await self._update_matter_in_db(self.matters[matter_id])
        return True
    
    async def complete_matter(self, matter_id: str, result: Dict) -> bool:
        """瀹屾垚浜や粯鐗?""
        if matter_id not in self.matters:
            return False
        self.matters[matter_id].status = "review"
        self.matters[matter_id].deliverable["result"] = result
        self.matters[matter_id].updated_at = datetime.now()
        await self._update_matter_in_db(self.matters[matter_id])
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="octo.matter_completed",
            entity_type="agent_matter",
            entity_id=matter_id,
            payload={"result": result}
        )
        return True
    
    async def review_matter(self, matter_id: str, decision: str, feedback: str) -> bool:
        """瀹℃煡浜や粯鐗?(Humans decide.)"""
        if matter_id not in self.matters:
            return False
        
        matter = self.matters[matter_id]
        if decision == "accept":
            matter.status = "done"
            matter.feedback = {"decision": "accept", "feedback": feedback}
        elif decision == "reject":
            matter.status = "assigned"
            matter.feedback = {"decision": "reject", "feedback": feedback}
            await self._reassign_and_rerun(matter)
        elif decision == "revise":
            matter.status = "in_progress"
            matter.feedback = {"decision": "revise", "feedback": feedback}
        else:
            return False
        
        matter.updated_at = datetime.now()
        await self._update_matter_in_db(matter)
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="octo.matter_reviewed",
            entity_type="agent_matter",
            entity_id=matter_id,
            payload={"decision": decision, "feedback": feedback}
        )
        return True
```

### 25.5 鍏鍗忎綔妯″紡瀹炵幇

```python
# engines/octo_engine.py (鍗忎綔妯″紡)
class CollaborationMode(str, Enum):
    SOLO = "solo"            # 鍗曚汉瀹屾垚
    ROUNDTABLE = "roundtable"  # 鍦嗘璁ㄨ
    CRITIC = "critic"        # 鐙珛瀹℃牳
    PIPELINE = "pipeline"    # 娴佹按绾?
    SPLIT = "split"          # 鍒嗗ご骞?
    SWARM = "swarm"          # 绔為€夋嫨浼?

class OctoEngine:
    # 鍗忎綔妯″紡鎵ц
    
    async def run_collaboration(self, matter_id: str, mode: CollaborationMode) -> Dict:
        """鎵ц鍏鍗忎綔妯″紡涔嬩竴"""
        matter = self.matters.get(matter_id)
        if not matter:
            raise ValueError(f"Matter {matter_id} not found")
        
        # 鏍规嵁妯″紡鎵ц
        if mode == CollaborationMode.SOLO:
            return await self._run_solo(matter)
        elif mode == CollaborationMode.ROUNDTABLE:
            return await self._run_roundtable(matter)
        elif mode == CollaborationMode.CRITIC:
            return await self._run_critic(matter)
        elif mode == CollaborationMode.PIPELINE:
            return await self._run_pipeline(matter)
        elif mode == CollaborationMode.SPLIT:
            return await self._run_split(matter)
        elif mode == CollaborationMode.SWARM:
            return await self._run_swarm(matter)
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unknown mode: {mode}")
    
    async def _run_solo(self, matter: Matter) -> Dict:
        """鍗曚汉瀹屾垚妯″紡 鈥?涓€涓狟ot鑷繁瀹屾垚"""
        assignee = self._resolve_assignee(matter.assignee_type, matter.assignee_id)
        result = await assignee.execute(matter.deliverable)
        return {"mode": "solo", "result": result, "status": "completed"}
    
    async def _run_roundtable(self, matter: Matter) -> Dict:
        """鍦嗘璁ㄨ妯″紡 鈥?澶氫釜Bot鍏紑璁ㄨ"""
        bots = self._get_bots_in_channel(matter.channel_id)
        results = await asyncio.gather(*[
            bot.discuss(matter.title, matter.deliverable) for bot in bots
        ])
        # 姹囨€昏璁虹粨鏋?
        summary = await self._summarize_discussion(results)
        return {"mode": "roundtable", "summary": summary, "individual_results": results}
    
    async def _run_critic(self, matter: Matter) -> Dict:
        """鐙珛瀹℃牳妯″紡 鈥?涓€涓仛锛屼竴涓"""
        exec_bot = self._resolve_assignee(matter.assignee_type, matter.assignee_id)
        critic_bot = self._get_critic_bot(matter.channel_id)
        
        # 鎵ц
        result = await exec_bot.execute(matter.deliverable)
        # 瀹℃牳
        review = await critic_bot.review(result)
        
        if review["approved"]:
            return {"mode": "critic", "result": result, "review": review, "status": "approved"}
        else:
            # 鎵撳洖閲嶅仛
            revised_result = await exec_bot.revise(result, review["feedback"])
            return {"mode": "critic", "result": revised_result, "review": review, "revised": True}
    
    async def _run_pipeline(self, matter: Matter) -> Dict:
        """娴佹按绾挎ā寮?鈥?A鍋氬畬浜ょ粰B锛孊鍋氬畬浜ょ粰C"""
        bots = self._get_bots_by_order(matter.channel_id, matter.deliverable.get("pipeline_order", []))
        current_data = matter.deliverable.get("initial_data", {})
        
        results = []
        for bot in bots:
            result = await bot.execute(current_data)
            results.append({"bot": bot.name, "result": result})
            current_data = result  # 涓嬩竴姝ョ殑杈撳叆
        
        return {"mode": "pipeline", "results": results, "final_output": current_data}
    
    async def _run_split(self, matter: Matter) -> Dict:
        """鍒嗗ご骞叉ā寮?鈥?澶т换鍔℃媶鎴愬嚑鍧楀苟琛?""
        sub_tasks = matter.deliverable.get("sub_tasks", [])
        bots = self._get_bots_by_capability(matter.channel_id, sub_tasks)
        
        results = await asyncio.gather(*[
            bot.execute(sub_task) for bot, sub_task in zip(bots, sub_tasks)
        ])
        
        # 鍚堝苟缁撴灉
        merged = await self._merge_results(results, matter.deliverable.get("merge_strategy", "concat"))
        
        return {"mode": "split", "results": results, "merged": merged}
    
    async def _run_swarm(self, matter: Matter) -> Dict:
        """绔為€夋嫨浼樻ā寮?鈥?鍚屼竴棰樼洰澶氫釜Bot锛岄€夋渶浣?""
        bots = self._get_bots_by_capability(matter.channel_id, matter.deliverable.get("required_capability"))
        results = await asyncio.gather(*[
            bot.execute(matter.deliverable) for bot in bots
        ])
        
        # 閫夋嫨鏈€浣虫柟妗?
        best = await self._select_best_result(results, matter.acceptance_criteria)
        return {"mode": "swarm", "best_result": best, "all_results": results}
```


## 绗?6绔?灞忓箷鎰熺煡鍨嬩富鍔ˋgent (Vida瀹屾暣瀹炵幇)

### 26.1 Vida鏍稿績鏋舵瀯

```python
# engines/vida_engine.py
class VidaEngine:
    """
    Vida灞忓箷鎰熺煡寮曟搸 鈥?鎸佺画鐞嗚В涓婁笅鏂囥€佺Н绱蹇嗐€侀鍒ゆ剰鍥俱€佷富鍔ㄨ鍔?
    鏍稿績: "涓嶇瓑寰呮寚浠わ紝涓诲姩鍗忓姪"
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.screen_capture = ScreenCapture()
        self.context_analyzer = ContextAnalyzer()
        self.intent_predictor = IntentPredictor()
        self.action_executor = ActionExecutor()
        self.memory_store = AgentMemoryStore()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def perceive_and_act(self, user_id: str) -> Dict:
        """鎰熺煡-鐞嗚В-棰勬祴-琛屽姩 瀹屾暣寰幆"""
        # 1. 鎰熺煡灞忓箷
        screen_data = await self.screen_capture.capture()
        
        # 2. 鐞嗚В涓婁笅鏂?
        context = await self.context_analyzer.analyze(screen_data, user_id)
        
        # 3. 鍔犺浇璁板繂
        memory = await self.memory_store.load(user_id)
        
        # 4. 棰勬祴鎰忓浘
        intent = await self.intent_predictor.predict(context, memory)
        
        # 5. 鍐冲畾琛屽姩
        if intent.confidence > 0.7:
            action = await self._decide_action(intent, context)
            if action:
                result = await self.action_executor.execute(action)
                await self._save_action_result(user_id, action, result)
                
                # 鐢熸垚鎴樻姤
                await self._generate_daily_report(user_id)
                
                return {
                    "context": context,
                    "intent": intent,
                    "action": action,
                    "result": result
                }
        
        return {"context": context, "intent": intent, "action": None}
    
    async def generate_daily_report(self, user_id: str) -> Report:
        """鐢熸垚浠婃棩鎴樻姤鍗?""
        # 鑾峰彇浠婃棩鎵€鏈夎涓?
        actions = await self._get_today_actions(user_id)
        
        # 缁熻
        completed = [a for a in actions if a["status"] == "completed"]
        in_progress = [a for a in actions if a["status"] == "in_progress"]
        
        # 鐢熸垚鎶ュ憡
        report = {
            "date": datetime.now().date().isoformat(),
            "completed_count": len(completed),
            "in_progress_count": len(in_progress),
            "completed_items": [{"title": a["title"], "result": a["result"]} for a in completed[:5]],
            "key_words": await self._extract_key_words(actions),
            "tomorrow_plan": await self._suggest_tomorrow_plan(actions),
            "time_distribution": self._calculate_time_distribution(actions)
        }
        
        return report
```

### 26.2 灞忓箷鎹曡幏涓庝笂涓嬫枃鐞嗚В

```python
# intelligence/vida/screen_capture.py
class ScreenCapture:
    """灞忓箷鎹曡幏 鈥?澶氬钩鍙版敮鎸?""
    
    async def capture(self) -> ScreenData:
        """鎹曡幏褰撳墠灞忓箷"""
        if sys.platform == "darwin":
            return await self._capture_macos()
        elif sys.platform == "win32":
            return await self._capture_windows()
        else:
            return await self._capture_linux()
    
    async def _capture_macos(self) -> ScreenData:
        """macOS灞忓箷鎹曡幏"""
        import pyautogui
        screenshot = pyautogui.screenshot()
        
        # 鑾峰彇褰撳墠娲诲姩绐楀彛
        from AppKit import NSWorkspace
        active_app = NSWorkspace.sharedWorkspace().activeApplication()
        
        return ScreenData(
            image=screenshot,
            active_app=active_app.get("NSApplicationName"),
            active_window_title=active_app.get("NSApplicationName"),
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )
    
    async def _capture_windows(self) -> ScreenData:
        """Windows灞忓箷鎹曡幏"""
        import win32gui
        import win32ui
        import win32con
        
        hwnd = win32gui.GetForegroundWindow()
        window_title = win32gui.GetWindowText(hwnd)
        
        # 鎴浘
        hwnd_dc = win32gui.GetWindowDC(hwnd)
        mfc_dc = win32ui.CreateDCFromHandle(hwnd_dc)
        save_dc = mfc_dc.CreateCompatibleDC()
        
        # ... 鎴浘閫昏緫
        
        return ScreenData(
            image=screenshot,
            active_app=window_title,
            active_window_title=window_title,
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )

# intelligence/vida/context_analyzer.py
class ContextAnalyzer:
    """涓婁笅鏂囧垎鏋?鈥?璇嗗埆鐢ㄦ埛褰撳墠宸ヤ綔鍦烘櫙"""
    
    async def analyze(self, screen_data: ScreenData, user_id: str) -> Context:
        """鍒嗘瀽灞忓箷鍐呭锛岀悊瑙ｄ笂涓嬫枃"""
        # OCR鎻愬彇鏂囧瓧
        text = await self._extract_text(screen_data.image)
        
        # 璇嗗埆搴旂敤鍦烘櫙
        app_scenario = self._identify_scenario(screen_data.active_app, text)
        
        # 鎻愬彇鍏抽敭淇℃伅
        key_info = await self._extract_key_info(text, app_scenario)
        
        return Context(
            app=screen_data.active_app,
            scenario=app_scenario,
            text=text[:500],  # 闄愬埗闀垮害
            key_info=key_info,
            timestamp=screen_data.timestamp,
            user_id=user_id
        )
    
    def _identify_scenario(self, app: str, text: str) -> str:
        """璇嗗埆宸ヤ綔鍦烘櫙"""
        scenarios = {
            "code": ["vscode", "pycharm", "cursor", "claude code", "codex"],
            "chat": ["wechat", "寰俊", "slack", "discord", "telegram"],
            "document": ["word", "notion", "obsidian", "椋炰功", "google docs"],
            "research": ["chrome", "firefox", "safari", "browser"],
            "email": ["mail", "outlook", "gmail"],
            "terminal": ["terminal", "iterm", "command", "bash", "zsh"]
        }
        
        app_lower = app.lower()
        for scenario, keywords in scenarios.items():
            for keyword in keywords:
                if keyword in app_lower or keyword in text.lower():
                    return scenario
        return "unknown"
```

### 26.3 鎰忓浘棰勬祴涓庝富鍔ㄨ鍔?

```python
# intelligence/vida/intent_predictor.py
class IntentPredictor:
    """鎰忓浘棰勬祴 鈥?鍩轰簬涓婁笅鏂囧拰鍘嗗彶琛屼负棰勬祴鐢ㄦ埛鎰忓浘"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.llm = get_llm_provider()
    
    async def predict(self, context: Context, memory: Dict) -> Intent:
        """棰勬祴鐢ㄦ埛鎰忓浘"""
        prompt = f"""
        Based on the following context and user history, predict what the user is likely to do next.
        
        Current Application: {context.app}
        Scenario: {context.scenario}
        Screen Text: {context.text[:200]}
        Key Information: {context.key_info}
        User Memory: {memory}
        
        Return JSON:
        {{
            "intent_type": "write_code|reply_message|research|read_document|email|other",
            "confidence": 0.0-1.0,
            "suggested_action": "What action would be helpful?",
            "parameters": {{}}
        }}
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        return Intent(**json.loads(response))

# intelligence/vida/action_executor.py
class ActionExecutor:
    """琛屽姩鎵ц 鈥?鎵ц涓诲姩琛屽姩"""
    
    async def execute(self, action: Action) -> ActionResult:
        """鎵ц涓诲姩琛屽姩"""
        if action.type == "summarize":
            # 鎬荤粨褰撳墠鍐呭
            return await self._summarize(action.parameters)
        elif action.type == "reply":
            # 鐢熸垚鍥炲寤鸿
            return await self._suggest_reply(action.parameters)
        elif action.type == "organize":
            # 鏁寸悊鏂囦欢
            return await self._organize_files(action.parameters)
        elif action.type == "search":
            # 鎼滅储淇℃伅
            return await self._search(action.parameters)
        elif action.type == "remind":
            # 璁剧疆鎻愰啋
            return await self._set_reminder(action.parameters)
        elif action.type == "draft":
            # 璧疯崏鍐呭
            return await self._draft(action.parameters)
        elif action.type == "analyze":
            # 鍒嗘瀽鏁版嵁
            return await self._analyze(action.parameters)
        else:
            return ActionResult(success=False, error=f"Unknown action: {action.type}")
    
    async def _summarize(self, params: Dict) -> ActionResult:
        """鎬荤粨褰撳墠鍐呭"""
        content = params.get("content", "")
        length = params.get("length", "short")
        summary = await self.llm.summarize(content, length)
        return ActionResult(success=True, result={"summary": summary})
    
    async def _suggest_reply(self, params: Dict) -> ActionResult:
        """鐢熸垚鍥炲寤鸿"""
        message = params.get("message", "")
        context = params.get("context", "")
        replies = await self.llm.generate_replies(message, context, n=3)
        return ActionResult(success=True, result={"replies": replies})
```

鈹? 鈹? 6. 瀹℃煡楠岃瘉 (Verify) 鈥?楠岃瘉缁撴灉鏄惁绗﹀悎鎴愬姛鏍囧噯                       鈹傗攤

鈹?                                   鈫?                                        鈹?
鈹? 鈹屸攢鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹€鈹愨攤
