### 27.2 瀹屾暣娌荤悊瀹炵幇

```python
# engines/meta_kim_engine.py
class MetaKimEngine:
    """
    AI娌荤悊寮曟搸 鈥?纭繚AI宸ヤ綔鍙不鐞嗐€佸彲杩芥函銆佸彲瀛︿範
    鏍稿績寰幆: 婢勬竻鈫掓悳绱⑩啋閫夋嫨鈫掓媶鍒嗏啋鎵ц鈫掑鏌モ啋楠岃瘉鈫掑涔?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.capability_registry = CapabilityRegistry()
        self.run_history = []
        self.learned_skills = []
        self.failure_knowledge_base = []
        self.llm = get_llm_provider()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def govern_run(self, request: str, context: Dict = None) -> GovernedRun:
        """鎵ц涓€涓畬鏁寸殑娌荤悊杩愯"""
        run_id = f"gov_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
        
        # 1. 鎰忓浘婢勬竻
        intent = await self._clarify_intent(request, context)
        
        # 2. 鑳藉姏鎼滅储
        capabilities = await self._search_capabilities(intent)
        
        # 3. 鎵€鏈夋潈閫夋嫨
        owner = await self._select_owner(capabilities, intent)
        
        # 4. 浠诲姟鎷嗗垎
        tasks = await self._split_tasks(intent, capabilities)
        
        # 5. 鎵ц
        results = await self._execute_tasks(tasks, owner)
        
        # 6. 瀹℃煡楠岃瘉
        verified = await self._verify_results(results, intent.success_standard)
        
        # 7. 缁忛獙鍥炲啓
        lessons = await self._extract_lessons(verified)
        await self._write_back_lessons(lessons)
        
        # 8. 鐢熸垚娌荤悊鎶ュ憡
        report = self._generate_report(run_id, intent, tasks, results, verified, lessons)
        
        run = GovernedRun(
            id=run_id,
            request=request,
            intent=intent,
            tasks=tasks,
            results=results,
            verified=verified,
            lessons=lessons,
            report=report,
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        self.run_history.append(run)
        await self._save_run_to_db(run)
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="meta_kim.run_completed",
            entity_type="governance_run",
            entity_id=run_id,
            payload={"intent": intent.intent_type, "task_count": len(tasks), "success": verified.succeeded}
        )
        
        return run
    
    async def _clarify_intent(self, request: str, context: Dict) -> Intent:
        """鎰忓浘婢勬竻 鈥?灏嗘ā绯婅姹傝浆涓烘槑纭殑鎰忓浘鍜屾垚鍔熸爣鍑?""
        prompt = f"""
        You are an AI governance system. Analyze the following user request and clarify the intent.
        If the request is ambiguous, ask clarifying questions.
        
        Request: "{request}"
        Context: {context}
        
        Return a structured intent with:
        1. intent_type: what the user wants to achieve (be specific)
        2. description: clear description of the intent
        3. success_standard: how to measure success (quantifiable)
        4. constraints: any limitations or requirements
        5. clarifying_questions: list of questions if ambiguous (max 3)
        6. confidence: 0.0-1.0
        
        JSON format:
        {{
            "intent_type": "data_acquisition|data_cleaning|annotation|export|etc",
            "description": "...",
            "success_standard": {{"metric": "accuracy", "threshold": 0.95}},
            "constraints": {{"time_limit": "1h", "cost_limit": "$10"}},
            "clarifying_questions": [],
            "confidence": 0.9
        }}
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        intent_data = json.loads(response)
        
        # 濡傛灉闇€瑕佹緞娓?
        if intent_data.get("clarifying_questions") and intent_data["confidence"] < 0.8:
            return await self._ask_clarifying_questions(intent_data["clarifying_questions"])
        
        return Intent(**intent_data)
    
    async def _search_capabilities(self, intent: Intent) -> List[Capability]:
        """鑳藉姏鎼滅储 鈥?鍩轰簬鎰忓浘鎵惧埌鍙敤鐨勮兘鍔?""
        # 璇箟鎼滅储
        embedding = await self._embed(intent.description)
        capabilities = await self.capability_registry.search(
            embedding=embedding,
            top_k=10,
            filter_by_category=intent.intent_type
        )
        
        # 鐩稿叧鎬ф帓搴?
        sorted_caps = sorted(capabilities, key=lambda c: self._relevance_score(c, intent), reverse=True)
        return sorted_caps[:5]
    
    async def _select_owner(self, capabilities: List[Capability], intent: Intent) -> str:
        """鎵€鏈夋潈閫夋嫨 鈥?鍐冲畾璋佹潵鎵ц"""
        # 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚︽湁鍚堥€傜殑Bot
        bots = await self.octo_engine.get_bots_by_capability([c.id for c in capabilities])
        if bots:
            # 閫夋嫨璐熻浇鏈€杞荤殑Bot
            selected = min(bots, key=lambda b: b.workload)
            return f"bot:{selected.id}"
        else:
            # 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚﹀彲鑷姩鍖?
            if all(c.automatable for c in capabilities):
                return "system:auto"
            else:
                return "human:required"
    
    async def _split_tasks(self, intent: Intent, capabilities: List[Capability]) -> List[Task]:
        """浠诲姟鎷嗗垎 鈥?灏嗗ぇ浠诲姟鎷嗘垚鏈夎竟鐣岀殑瀛愪换鍔?""
        prompt = f"""
        Split the following intent into subtasks:
        Intent: {intent.description}
        Available capabilities: {[c.id for c in capabilities]}
        
        Return a list of subtasks, each with:
        - name: short name
        - description: what to do
        - capability_id: which capability to use
        - dependencies: list of task names that must complete first
        - estimated_duration: in minutes
        
        JSON format:
        [
            {{"name": "...", "description": "...", "capability_id": "...", "dependencies": [], "estimated_duration": 10}},
            ...
        ]
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        tasks_data = json.loads(response)
        return [Task(**t) for t in tasks_data]
    
    async def _verify_results(self, results: Dict, success_standard: Dict) -> VerifiedResult:
        """瀹℃煡楠岃瘉 鈥?纭繚缁撴灉绗﹀悎鎴愬姛鏍囧噯"""
        criteria = success_standard.get("criteria", [])
        failures = []
        
        for criterion in criteria:
            if criterion["type"] == "human_review":
                # 闇€瑕佷汉绫诲鏌?
                return VerifiedResult(
                    succeeded=False,
                    requires_human_review=True,
                    message=f"Human review required for: {criterion['description']}",
                    failures=[criterion["description"]]
                )
            elif criterion["type"] == "automated_test":
                # 鑷姩娴嬭瘯楠岃瘉
                passed = await self._run_automated_test(criterion["test_id"], results)
                if not passed:
                    failures.append(f"Automated test failed: {criterion['description']}")
            elif criterion["type"] == "quality_threshold":
                # 璐ㄩ噺闃堝€奸獙璇?
                quality_score = await self._measure_quality(results, criterion["metric"])
                if quality_score < criterion["threshold"]:
                    failures.append(f"Quality below threshold: {quality_score:.2f} < {criterion['threshold']}")
            elif criterion["type"] == "count_check":
                # 鏁伴噺妫€鏌?
                count = results.get("count", 0)
                if count < criterion["min_count"]:
                    failures.append(f"Count {count} < minimum {criterion['min_count']}")
        
        if failures:
            return VerifiedResult(
                succeeded=False,
                requires_human_review=False,
                message="; ".join(failures),
                failures=failures
            )
        
        return VerifiedResult(
            succeeded=True,
            requires_human_review=False,
            message="All criteria met",
            score=quality_score if 'quality_score' in locals() else 1.0
        )
    
    async def _extract_lessons(self, verified: VerifiedResult) -> List[Lesson]:
        """鎻愬彇鍙鐢ㄧ殑缁忛獙"""
        lessons = []
        
        if verified.succeeded:
            # 鎴愬姛缁忛獙 鈫?鎻愮偧涓烘妧鑳?
            lesson = Lesson(
                type="success",
                description="A task was successfully completed",
                action="create_skill",
                content={
                    "name": f"auto_skill_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
                    "description": verified.task_details.get("description", ""),
                    "steps": verified.task_details.get("steps", []),
                    "trigger_phrases": verified.task_details.get("trigger_phrases", [])
                }
            )
            lessons.append(lesson)
        else:
            # 澶辫触缁忛獙 鈫?璁板綍涓洪渶瑕佹敼杩涚殑鐐?
            for failure in verified.failures:
                lesson = Lesson(
                    type="failure",
                    description=f"Task failed: {failure}",
                    action="needs_improvement",
                    content={
                        "failure": failure,
                        "context": verified.task_details,
                        "suggestion": await self._suggest_improvement(failure)
                    }
                )
                lessons.append(lesson)
        
        return lessons
    
    async def _write_back_lessons(self, lessons: List[Lesson]):
        """鍥炲啓缁忛獙鍒扮郴缁?""
        for lesson in lessons:
            if lesson.type == "success" and lesson.action == "create_skill":
                # 灏嗘垚鍔熺殑娴佺▼鍥哄寲涓烘妧鑳?
                await self.skill_engine.create_skill(
                    name=lesson.content["name"],
                    description=lesson.content["description"],
                    steps=lesson.content["steps"],
                    trigger_phrases=lesson.content.get("trigger_phrases", [])
                )
            elif lesson.type == "failure":
                # 璁板綍澶辫触妯″紡鍒扮煡璇嗗簱
                self.failure_knowledge_base.append({
                    "failure": lesson.content["failure"],
                    "context": lesson.content["context"],
                    "suggestion": lesson.content.get("suggestion"),
                    "timestamp": datetime.now()
                })
```

### 28.3 涓撳鍔犺浇涓庝娇鐢?

```python
# intelligence/agency/loader.py
class AgencyLoader:
    """涓撳搴撳姞杞藉櫒"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.experts = {}
        self._load_all_experts()
    
    def _load_all_experts(self):
        """鍔犺浇鎵€鏈?32涓笓瀹?""
        experts_dir = Path(__file__).parent / "experts"
        for dept_dir in experts_dir.iterdir():
            if dept_dir.is_dir():
                for expert_file in dept_dir.glob("*.md"):
                    expert = self._parse_expert(expert_file)
                    self.experts[expert.name] = expert
    
    def _parse_expert(self, file_path: Path) -> Expert:
        """瑙ｆ瀽涓撳Markdown鏂囦欢"""
        content = file_path.read_text()
        # 瑙ｆ瀽鍚勪釜閮ㄥ垎
        sections = self._parse_sections(content)
        return Expert(
            name=sections.get("瑙掕壊鍚嶇О", file_path.stem),
            identity=sections.get("浣犳槸璋?, ""),
            skills=sections.get("浣犳搮闀夸粈涔?, "").split("\n"),
            rules=sections.get("浣犻伒寰殑瑙勫垯", "").split("\n"),
            output_format=sections.get("浣犵殑杈撳嚭搴旇鏄粈涔堟牱鐨?, "").split("\n"),
            workflow=sections.get("浣犵殑宸ヤ綔娴?, "").split("\n"),
            file_path=str(file_path)
        )
    
    def get_expert(self, name: str) -> Optional[Expert]:
        """鏍规嵁鍚嶇О鑾峰彇涓撳"""
        return self.experts.get(name)
    
    def search_experts(self, query: str, top_k: int = 5) -> List[Expert]:
        """鎼滅储涓撳 (鍩轰簬鎶€鑳藉尮閰?"""
        results = []
        query_lower = query.lower()
        for expert in self.experts.values():
            score = 0
            # 鍖归厤鍚嶇О
            if query_lower in expert.name.lower():
                score += 3
            # 鍖归厤鎶€鑳?
            for skill in expert.skills:
                if query_lower in skill.lower():
                    score += 1
            if score > 0:
                results.append((expert, score))
        
        results.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        return [e for e, s in results[:top_k]]
```


# 绗竷閮ㄥ垎: 鍒涙剰涓庡唴瀹圭敓浜х郴缁?

## 绗?9绔?AI鐭墽鐢熶骇绯荤粺 (鍓уぇ铏惧畬鏁磋瀺鍚?

### 29.1 鐭墽Harness瀹屾暣瀹炵幇

```python
# creative/short_drama/harness.py
class ShortDramaHarness:
    """
    鐭墽Harness 鈥?闈㈠悜鍒涗綔鑰呯殑鏅鸿兘鍒涗綔绯荤粺
    瀹屾暣娴佺▼: 闇€姹傜悊瑙ｂ啋鍓ф湰鐢熸垚鈫掕鑹茶璁♀啋鍦烘櫙璁捐鈫掑垎闀滄媶瑙ｂ啋瑙嗛鐢熸垚鈫掗厤闊斥啋鎴愮墖
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.llm = get_llm_provider()
        self.image_gen = get_image_generator()
        self.video_gen = get_video_generator()
        self.audio_gen = get_audio_generator()
        self.asset_manager = DramaAssetManager()
        self.character_consistency = CharacterConsistencyEngine()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    # ============ 1. 闇€姹傜悊瑙ｄ笌鍓ф湰鐢熸垚 ============
    async def generate_script(self, prompt: str, config: DramaConfig) -> Script:
        """浠庝竴鍙ヨ瘽鐢熸垚瀹屾暣鍓ф湰"""
        # 鍐呭绫诲瀷璇嗗埆
        content_type = await self._classify_content(prompt)
        
        # 鍓ф湰鐢熸垚
        script_prompt = f"""
        Generate a short drama script based on the following:
        - Theme: {prompt}
        - Genre: {config.genre}
        - Number of episodes: {config.episodes}
        - Duration per episode: {config.duration_per_episode}s
        - Style: {config.style}
        - Tone: {config.tone}
        - Target Audience: {config.target_audience}
        
        The script must include:
        1. Overall plot summary (with logline)
        2. Episode breakdown (each episode: scene, characters, dialogue, action, emotion)
        3. Character list with descriptions, personalities, relationships
        4. Key dramatic moments (climax, turning points)
        5. Visual style notes
        6. Setting descriptions
        
        Return JSON:
        {{
            "title": "...",
            "genre": "...",
            "logline": "...",
            "episodes": [
                {{"number": 1, "title": "...", "scenes": [{{"characters": [], "dialogue": [], "action": "", "emotion": ""}}]}}
            ],
            "characters": [{{"name": "", "description": "", "personality": "", "role": "protagonist|antagonist|supporting"}}],
            "visual_notes": "",
            "settings": [{{"name": "", "description": ""}}]
        }}
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(script_prompt, temperature=0.8)
        script_data = json.loads(response)
        
        script = Script(
            drama_id=f"drama_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            title=script_data["title"],
            genre=script_data["genre"],
            style=config.style,
            logline=script_data["logline"],
            episodes=script_data["episodes"],
            characters=script_data["characters"],
            visual_notes=script_data["visual_notes"],
            settings=script_data["settings"],
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="drama.script_generated",
            entity_type="short_drama",
            entity_id=script.drama_id,
            payload={"title": script.title, "episodes": len(script.episodes)}
        )
        
        return script
    
    # ============ 2. 瑙掕壊璁捐 ============
    async def design_characters(self, script: Script, style: str) -> List[Character]:
        """璁捐瑙掕壊骞剁敓鎴愬弬鑰冨浘"""
        characters = []
        for char_desc in script.characters:
            # 鐢熸垚瑙掕壊褰㈣薄
            image_prompt = f"""
            Generate a character design for:
            Name: {char_desc['name']}
            Description: {char_desc['description']}
            Personality: {char_desc.get('personality', '')}
            Role: {char_desc.get('role', 'supporting')}
            Style: {style}
            Setting: {script.visual_notes}
            
            Requirements:
            - Full body, front view
            - High quality, detailed
            - Consistent with the style
            """
            reference_image = await self.image_gen.generate(image_prompt)
            
            character = Character(
                id=f"char_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
                name=char_desc['name'],
                description=char_desc['description'],
                personality=char_desc.get('personality', ''),
                role=char_desc.get('role', 'supporting'),
                reference_image=reference_image,
                style=style,
                consistency_vector=self.character_consistency.generate_vector(reference_image),
                created_at=datetime.now()
            )
            characters.append(character)
            await self.asset_manager.save_character(character)
        
        return characters
    
    # ============ 3. 鍦烘櫙璁捐 ============
    async def design_scenes(self, script: Script, style: str) -> List[Scene]:
        """璁捐鍦烘櫙骞剁敓鎴愬弬鑰冨浘"""
        scenes = []
        for setting in script.settings:
            image_prompt = f"""
            Generate a scene design for:
            Name: {setting['name']}
            Description: {setting['description']}
            Style: {style}
            Visual Notes: {script.visual_notes}
            
            Requirements:
            - Wide shot, landscape orientation
            - Detailed environment
            - Atmospheric lighting
            """
            reference_image = await self.image_gen.generate(image_prompt)
            
            scene = Scene(
                id=f"scene_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
                name=setting['name'],
                description=setting['description'],
                reference_image=reference_image,
                style=style,
                created_at=datetime.now()
            )
            scenes.append(scene)
            await self.asset_manager.save_scene(scene)
        
        return scenes
    
    # ============ 4. 鏅鸿兘鍒嗛暅鎷嗚В ============
    async def split_shots(self, script: Script, characters: List[Character],
                          scenes: List[Scene]) -> List[Shot]:
        """灏嗗墽鏈媶瑙ｄ负鍙墽琛岀殑鍒嗛暅"""
        shots = []
        shot_id_counter = 0
        
        for episode in script.episodes:
            for scene in episode.get("scenes", []):
                # 灏嗗満鏅枃鏈媶瑙ｄ负闀滃ご
                shot_descriptions = await self._split_scene_to_shots(
                    scene, characters, scenes
                )
                
                for shot_desc in shot_descriptions:
                    shot_id_counter += 1
                    shot = Shot(
                        id=f"shot_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}",
                        number=shot_id_counter,
                        episode=episode["number"],
                        scene=shot_desc.get("scene_name", ""),
                        character_ids=[c.id for c in shot_desc.get("characters", [])],
                        action=shot_desc.get("action", ""),
                        emotion=shot_desc.get("emotion", ""),
                        composition=shot_desc.get("composition", "medium_shot"),
                        duration=shot_desc.get("duration", 5),
                        prompt=self._build_shot_prompt(shot_desc, characters, scenes),
                        status="pending",
                        created_at=datetime.now()
                    )
                    shots.append(shot)
        
        return shots
    
    def _build_shot_prompt(self, shot_desc: Dict, characters: List[Character],
                          scenes: List[Scene]) -> str:
        """鏋勫缓鍒嗛暅鐢熸垚鎻愮ず璇?""
        char_names = [c.name for c in shot_desc.get("characters", [])]
        scene_name = shot_desc.get("scene_name", "")
        
        scene_ref = next((s for s in scenes if s.name == scene_name), None)
        
        return f"""
        {shot_desc.get('action', '')}
        Characters: {', '.join(char_names)}
        Scene: {scene_name}
        Emotion: {shot_desc.get('emotion', 'neutral')}
        Composition: {shot_desc.get('composition', 'medium_shot')}
        Duration: {shot_desc.get('duration', 5)}s
        Style: cinematic, high quality, 1080p
        {f'Scene Reference: {scene_ref.reference_image}' if scene_ref else ''}
        """
    
    # ============ 5. 瑙嗛鐢熸垚 ============
    async def generate_videos(self, shots: List[Shot], config: DramaConfig) -> List[Video]:
        """鎵归噺鐢熸垚鍒嗛暅瑙嗛"""
        videos = []
        total = len(shots)
        
        for idx, shot in enumerate(shots):
            if shot.status == "pending":
                # 鑾峰彇瑙掕壊鍜屽満鏅弬鑰冨浘
                character_images = await self.asset_manager.get_character_images(shot.character_ids)
                scene_image = await self.asset_manager.get_scene_image(shot.scene)
                
                # 鐢熸垚瑙嗛
                video = await self.video_gen.generate(
                    prompt=shot.prompt,
                    reference_images=character_images + ([scene_image] if scene_image else []),
                    duration=shot.duration,
                    style=config.style,
                    consistency=True,
                    resolution=config.resolution or "1080p"
                )
                
                shot.status = "completed"
                shot.video_url = video.url
                shot.generated_at = datetime.now()
                await self._update_shot_in_db(shot)
                
                videos.append(Video(
                    shot_id=shot.id,
                    url=video.url,
                    duration=shot.duration,
                    status="completed",
                    generated_at=datetime.now()
                ))
                
                # 鎺ㄩ€佽繘搴?
                await self.bus.record(
                    topic="drama.shot_generated",
                    entity_type="drama_shot",
                    entity_id=shot.id,
                    payload={"progress": (idx + 1) / total, "remaining": total - idx - 1}
                )
        
        return videos
    
    # ============ 6. 閰嶉煶鍚堟垚 ============
    async def generate_audio(self, script: Script, shots: List[Shot]) -> Audio:
        """鐢熸垚閰嶉煶 (鏃佺櫧+瑙掕壊鍙拌瘝)"""
        # 鎻愬彇鎵€鏈夊璇?
        dialogues = []
        for episode in script.episodes:
            for scene in episode.get("scenes", []):
                for dialogue in scene.get("dialogues", []):
                    dialogues.append({
                        "character": dialogue.get("character", "鏃佺櫧"),
                        "text": dialogue.get("text", ""),
                        "emotion": dialogue.get("emotion", "neutral"),
                        "duration": len(dialogue.get("text", "")) * 0.3  # 绮楃暐浼拌
                    })
        
        # 鐢熸垚闊抽
        audio = await self.audio_gen.generate(
            dialogues=dialogues,
            voice_profile=script.style,
            background_music=script.genre
        )
        
        return audio
    
    # ============ 7. 鎴愮墖鍚堟垚 ============
    async def assemble(self, script: Script, characters: List[Character],
                       scenes: List[Scene], shots: List[Shot],
                       videos: List[Video], audio: Audio) -> Drama:
        """鍚堟垚瀹屾暣鐨勭煭鍓ф垚鐗?""
        # 鎸夐『搴忔帓鍒?
        sorted_shots = sorted(shots, key=lambda s: (s.episode, s.number))
        
        # 鏋勫缓鎴愮墖
        drama = Drama(
            id=f"drama_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            title=script.title,
            genre=script.genre,
            style=script.style,
            episodes=script.episodes,
            characters=characters,
            scenes=scenes,
            shots=sorted_shots,
            videos=videos,
            audio=audio,
            status="assembling",
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        # 鍚堟垚瑙嗛
        final_video = await self._assemble_video(sorted_shots, videos, audio)
        drama.final_video_url = final_video.url
        drama.status = "completed"
        drama.assembled_at = datetime.now()
        drama.duration = sum(s.duration for s in sorted_shots)
        
        # 淇濆瓨
        await self._save_drama_to_db(drama)
        
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="drama.assembled",
            entity_type="short_drama",
            entity_id=drama.id,
            payload={
                "title": drama.title,
                "episodes": len(drama.episodes),
                "duration": drama.duration,
                "shots": len(shots)
            }
        )
        
        return drama
    
    # ============ 8. 鐭墽缂栬緫 ============
    async def edit_drama(self, drama_id: str, edits: Dict) -> Drama:
        """缂栬緫鐭墽 (鏀寔灞€閮ㄤ慨鏀?"""
        drama = await self._get_drama_from_db(drama_id)
        if not drama:
            raise ValueError(f"Drama {drama_id} not found")
        
        # 搴旂敤缂栬緫
        if "title" in edits:
            drama.title = edits["title"]
        
        if "style" in edits:
            drama.style = edits["style"]
            await self._regenerate_visuals(drama, edits["style"])
        
        if "replace_shots" in edits:
            for shot_edit in edits["replace_shots"]:
                await self._regenerate_shot(shot_edit["shot_id"], shot_edit.get("feedback", ""))
        
        if "extend" in edits:
            # 鎵╁睍鐭墽 (鏂板鍓ч泦)
            await self._extend_drama(drama, edits["extend"])
        
        drama.updated_at = datetime.now()
        await self._update_drama_in_db(drama)
        
        return drama
    
    # ============ 9. 鐭墽瀵煎嚭 ============
    async def export_drama(self, drama_id: str, format: str = "mp4") -> ExportResult:
        """瀵煎嚭鐭墽"""
        drama = await self._get_drama_from_db(drama_id)
        if not drama:
            raise ValueError(f"Drama {drama_id} not found")
        
        if format == "mp4":
            export_url = drama.final_video_url
        elif format == "jsonl":
            # 瀵煎嚭鍓ф湰涓篔SONL
            export_url = await self._export_script_jsonl(drama)
        elif format == "storyboard":
            # 瀵煎嚭琛?
            export_url = await self._export_storyboard(drama)
        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported format: {format}")
        
        return ExportResult(drama_id=drama_id, format=format, export_url=export_url)
```


## 绗?0绔?ComfyUI鍒涙剰宸ヤ綔娴?(Comfy MCP瀹屾暣铻嶅悎)

### 30.1 Comfy MCP闆嗘垚

```python
# creative/comfy/mcp_integration.py
class ComfyMCPIntegration:
    """
    Comfy MCP闆嗘垚 鈥?Agent閫氳繃鑷劧璇█鎿嶄綔ComfyUI
    鑳藉姏: 宸ヤ綔娴佸垱寤?杩愯/缂栬緫/鍏变韩銆佹ā鍨?鑺傜偣妫€绱€佹ā鏉垮姞杞姐€佹壒閲忔墽琛?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.comfy_client = ComfyClient()
        self.workflow_builder = WorkflowBuilder()
        self.model_retriever = ModelRetriever()
        self.node_retriever = NodeRetriever()
        self.llm = get_llm_provider()
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def run_workflow(self, instruction: str, params: Dict = None) -> GenerationResult:
        """
        鑷劧璇█ 鈫?ComfyUI宸ヤ綔娴?鈫?鎵ц
        绀轰緥: "鐢–omfyUI宸ヤ綔娴佺敓鎴?0鐗堜骇鍝佸箍鍛婂浘"
        """
        # 1. 鐞嗚В鎰忓浘
        intent = await self._parse_instruction(instruction)
        
        # 2. 妫€绱㈡垨鍒涘缓宸ヤ綔娴?
        workflow = await self._get_or_create_workflow(intent, params)
        
        # 3. 妫€绱㈡ā鍨嬪拰鑺傜偣
        models = await self.model_retriever.search(intent.model_requirements)
        nodes = await self.node_retriever.search(intent.node_requirements)
        
        # 4. 鏋勫缓瀹屾暣宸ヤ綔娴?
        full_workflow = await self.workflow_builder.build(workflow, models, nodes)
        
        # 5. 鎵ц
        if params and params.get("batch_count", 1) > 1:
            # 鎵归噺鎵ц
            results = await self._batch_execute(full_workflow, params["batch_count"])
        else:
            results = [await self.comfy_client.run(full_workflow)]
        
        # 6. 淇濆瓨缁撴灉
        result_ids = []
        for result in results:
            saved = await self._save_result(result, intent)
            result_ids.append(saved.id)
        
        # 7. 璁板綍
        await self.bus.record(
            topic="comfy.workflow_executed",
            entity_type="comfy_result",
            entity_id=",".join(result_ids),
            payload={"instruction": instruction, "count": len(results)}
        )
        
        return GenerationResult(
            workflow_id=workflow.id,
            result_ids=result_ids,
            results=results,
            count=len(results)
        )
    
    async def create_workflow(self, description: str) -> Workflow:
        """鑷劧璇█鍒涘缓ComfyUI宸ヤ綔娴?""
        prompt = f"""
        Create a ComfyUI workflow from the following description:
        {description}
        
        Return JSON with:
        - nodes: list of nodes with type, position, inputs, outputs
        - connections: list of connections between nodes
        - metadata: name, description, tags
        
        Available node types: ['LoadImage', 'CLIPTextEncode', 'KSampler', 'VAEDecode', 
                               'SaveImage', 'CheckpointLoaderSimple', 'CLIPImageEncode',
                               'ControlNetLoader', 'IPAdapter', 'FaceDetailer']
        """
        response = await self.llm.complete(prompt, response_format="json")
        workflow_data = json.loads(response)
        
        workflow = Workflow(
            id=f"comfy_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}",
            name=workflow_data.get("name", "Unnamed"),
            description=description,
            nodes=workflow_data.get("nodes", []),
            connections=workflow_data.get("connections", []),
            metadata=workflow_data.get("metadata", {}),
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        await self._save_workflow_to_db(workflow)
        
        return workflow
    
    async def _batch_execute(self, workflow: Workflow, count: int) -> List[Result]:
        """鎵归噺鎵ц宸ヤ綔娴?""
        tasks = []
        for i in range(count):
            # 姣忎釜浠诲姟鐙珛鍙傛暟
            task_params = self._generate_variant_params(workflow, i, count)
            tasks.append(self.comfy_client.run(workflow, task_params))
        
        results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
        return results
```

### 30.2 鏀寔鐨凜omfyUI妯″瀷

```python
# creative/comfy/model_retriever.py
class ModelRetriever:
    """ComfyUI妯″瀷妫€绱?""
    
    MODELS = {
        "sdxl": {
            "name": "SDXL 1.0",
            "type": "text_to_image",
            "checkpoint": "sd_xl_base_1.0.safetensors",
            "resolution": 1024,
            "capabilities": ["text_to_image", "image_to_image", "inpainting"]
        },
        "sdxl_turbo": {
            "name": "SDXL Turbo",
            "type": "text_to_image",
            "checkpoint": "sd_xl_turbo_1.0.safetensors",
            "resolution": 512,
            "capabilities": ["text_to_image", "fast_inference"]
        },
        "sd_15": {
            "name": "Stable Diffusion 1.5",
            "type": "text_to_image",
            "checkpoint": "v1-5-pruned.safetensors",
            "resolution": 512,
            "capabilities": ["text_to_image", "image_to_image", "inpainting", "controlnet"]
        },
        "sd_3": {
            "name": "Stable Diffusion 3",
            "type": "text_to_image",
            "checkpoint": "sd3_medium.safetensors",
            "resolution": 1024,
            "capabilities": ["text_to_image", "image_to_image", "text_rendering"]
        },
        "flux": {
            "name": "FLUX.1",
            "type": "text_to_image",
            "checkpoint": "flux1-dev.safetensors",
            "resolution": 1024,
            "capabilities": ["text_to_image", "image_to_image", "high_quality"]
        },
        "animate_diff": {
            "name": "AnimateDiff",
            "type": "text_to_video",
            "checkpoint": "animate_diff.ckpt",
            "capabilities": ["text_to_video", "video_to_video"]
        },
        "ip_adapter": {
            "name": "IP-Adapter",
            "type": "image_to_image",
            "checkpoint": "ip-adapter_sd15.safetensors",
            "capabilities": ["image_to_image", "style_transfer", "subject_consistency"]
        },
        "controlnet": {
            "name": "ControlNet",
            "type": "conditioning",
            "checkpoint": "control_v11p_sd15.safetensors",
            "capabilities": ["depth", "canny", "pose", "scribble", "segmentation"]
        }
    }
    
    async def search(self, query: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """鎼滅储妯″瀷"""
        query_lower = query.lower()
        results = []
        for model_id, model_info in self.MODELS.items():
            score = 0
            if query_lower in model_info["name"].lower():
                score += 3
            if query_lower in model_info["type"].lower():
                score += 2
            for cap in model_info.get("capabilities", []):
                if query_lower in cap:
                    score += 1
            if score > 0:
                results.append({**model_info, "id": model_id, "score": score})
        
        results.sort(key=lambda x: x["score"], reverse=True)
        return results[:5]
```


## 绗?1绔?鑷獟浣撴暟鎹櫤鑳?(RedFox瀹屾暣铻嶅悎)

### 31.1 RedFox瀹㈡埛绔疄鐜?

```python
# redfox/client.py
class RedFoxClient:
    """
    RedFox鏁版嵁鏅鸿兘瀹㈡埛绔?鈥?11骞冲彴缁熶竴API
    鏀寔: 灏忕孩涔︺€佹姈闊炽€佽棰戝彿銆佸叕浼楀彿銆佸揩鎵嬨€丅绔欍€佸井鍗氥€佷粖鏃ュご鏉°€佺櫨瀹跺彿銆佺煡涔?
    """
    
    def __init__(self, api_key: str = None):
        self.api_key = api_key or os.getenv("REDFOX_API_KEY")
        self.base_url = "https://redfox.hk/api/v1"
        self.cache = TTLCache(max_size=10000, default_ttl=3600)
        self.platforms = ["xiaohongshu", "douyin", "wechat", "kuaishou", 
                          "bilibili", "weibo", "toutiao", "baijiahao", "zhihu"]
    
    async def search(self, platform: str, keyword: str, 
                     page: int = 1, size: int = 20) -> SearchResult:
        """鎼滅储骞冲彴鍐呭"""
        cache_key = f"search:{platform}:{keyword}:{page}:{size}"
        if cached := self.cache.get(cache_key):
            return cached
        
        url = f"{self.base_url}/search"
        params = {
            "platform": platform,
            "keyword": keyword,
            "page": page,
            "size": size
        }
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.get(url, params=params, 
                                   headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"}) as resp:
                data = await resp.json()
                result = self._normalize_result(data, platform)
                self.cache.set(cache_key, result)
                return result
    
    async def get_hot(self, platform: str, date: str = None) -> HotList:
        """鑾峰彇鐑棬姒滃崟"""
        cache_key = f"hot:{platform}:{date or 'today'}"
        if cached := self.cache.get(cache_key):
            return cached
        
        url = f"{self.base_url}/hot"
        params = {"platform": platform}
        if date:
            params["date"] = date
        
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.get(url, params=params,
                                   headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"}) as resp:
                data = await resp.json()
                result = self._normalize_hot(data, platform)
                self.cache.set(cache_key, result)
                return result
    
    async def get_account(self, platform: str, account_id: str) -> AccountInfo:
        """鑾峰彇璐﹀彿淇℃伅"""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/account"
        params = {"platform": platform, "account_id": account_id}
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.get(url, params=params,
                                   headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"}) as resp:
                data = await resp.json()
                return self._normalize_account(data, platform)
    
    async def get_post(self, platform: str, post_id: str) -> Post:
        """鑾峰彇浣滃搧璇︽儏"""
        url = f"{self.base_url}/post"
        params = {"platform": platform, "post_id": post_id}
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            async with session.get(url, params=params,
                                   headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {self.api_key}"}) as resp:
                data = await resp.json()
                return self._normalize_post(data, platform)
    
    def _normalize_result(self, data: Dict, platform: str) -> SearchResult:
        """褰掍竴鍖栨悳绱㈢粨鏋?""
        items = data.get("data", [])
        normalized = []
        for item in items:
            normalized.append({
                "id": item.get("id"),
                "title": item.get("title", ""),
                "content": item.get("content", ""),
                "author": item.get("author", {}).get("name", ""),
                "like_count": item.get("like_count", 0),
                "comment_count": item.get("comment_count", 0),
                "share_count": item.get("share_count", 0),
                "view_count": item.get("view_count", 0),
                "published_at": item.get("published_at"),
                "url": item.get("url"),
                "platform": platform
            })
        return SearchResult(total=data.get("total", 0), items=normalized, platform=platform)
```

## 绗?2绔?Agent浜掕仈缃戣兘鍔?(Agent Reach瀹屾暣铻嶅悎)

### 32.1 缁熶竴浜掕仈缃戞帴鍙?

```python
# intelligence/agent_reach/integration.py
class AgentReachIntegration:
    """
    Agent Reach闆嗘垚 鈥?璁〢gent鑾峰緱瀹屾暣鐨勪簰鑱旂綉璁块棶鑳藉姏
    14涓厤璐规笭閬? web, twitter, youtube, bilibili, reddit, xiaohongshu,
    github, rss, exa_search, linkedin, instagram, wechat, douyin, zhihu
    """
    
    CHANNELS = {
        "web": {"handler": "JinaReader", "free": True},
        "twitter": {"handler": "TwitterAPI", "free": True},
        "youtube": {"handler": "YouTubeDL", "free": True},
        "bilibili": {"handler": "BilibiliDL", "free": True},
        "reddit": {"handler": "RedditAPI", "free": True},
        "xiaohongshu": {"handler": "RedFox", "free": True},
        "github": {"handler": "GitHubAPI", "free": True},
        "rss": {"handler": "FeedParser", "free": True},
        "exa_search": {"handler": "ExaSearch", "free": True},
        "linkedin": {"handler": "LinkedInMCP", "free": True},
        "instagram": {"handler": "Instaloader", "free": True},
        "wechat": {"handler": "WeChatMCP", "free": True},
        "douyin": {"handler": "DouyinAPI", "free": True},
        "zhihu": {"handler": "ZhihuAPI", "free": True}
    }
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.cache = TTLCache(max_size=5000, default_ttl=300)
        self.health_status = {}
    
    async def fetch(self, channel: str, query: str, **kwargs) -> FetchResult:
        """缁熶竴鎺ュ彛 鈥?浠讳綍娓犻亾閫氳繃鑷劧璇█璁块棶"""
        if channel not in self.CHANNELS:
            raise ValueError(f"Unsupported channel: {channel}")
        
        cache_key = f"{channel}:{query}:{json.dumps(kwargs, sort_keys=True)}"
        if cached := self.cache.get(cache_key):
            return cached
        
        handler_name = self.CHANNELS[channel]["handler"]
        handler = self._get_handler(handler_name)
        
        try:
            result = await handler.fetch(query, **kwargs)
            self.cache.set(cache_key, result)
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            return FetchResult(success=False, error=str(e), channel=channel)
    
    def _get_handler(self, handler_name: str):
        """鑾峰彇娓犻亾澶勭悊鍣?""
        handlers = {
            "JinaReader": JinaReader,
            "TwitterAPI": TwitterAPI,
            "YouTubeDL": YouTubeDL,
            "BilibiliDL": BilibiliDL,
            "RedditAPI": RedditAPI,
            "RedFox": RedFoxClient,
            "GitHubAPI": GitHubAPI,
            "FeedParser": FeedParser,
            "ExaSearch": ExaSearch
        }
        handler_class = handlers.get(handler_name)
        if handler_class:
            return handler_class()
        raise ValueError(f"Handler not found: {handler_name}")
    
    async def health_check(self) -> Dict:
        """涓€閿瘖鏂墍鏈夋笭閬撳仴搴风姸鎬?""
        results = {}
        for channel, config in self.CHANNELS.items():
            try:
                handler = self._get_handler(config["handler"])
                status = await handler.ping()
                results[channel] = {"status": "healthy" if status else "unhealthy"}
            except Exception as e:
                results[channel] = {"status": "error", "error": str(e)}
        
        self.health_status = results
        return results
    
    async def search(self, query: str, channels: List[str] = None) -> MultiChannelResult:
        """澶氭笭閬撴悳绱?""
        if not channels:
            channels = ["exa_search", "web", "reddit", "twitter"]
        
        results = {}
        for channel in channels:
            if channel in self.CHANNELS:
                result = await self.fetch(channel, query)
                results[channel] = result
        
        return MultiChannelResult(results=results, query=query)
```

### 32.2 JinaReader瀹炵幇 (Web璁块棶)

```python
# intelligence/agent_reach/channels/web.py
class JinaReader:
    """Jina Reader 鈥?鍏嶈垂缃戦〉鎶撳彇"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.base_url = "https://r.jina.ai"
        self.timeout = 30
    
    async def fetch(self, url: str, **kwargs) -> FetchResult:
        """鎶撳彇缃戦〉鍐呭"""
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
            try:
                full_url = f"{self.base_url}/{url}"
                async with session.get(full_url, timeout=self.timeout) as resp:
                    if resp.status == 200:
                        content = await resp.text()
                        return FetchResult(
                            success=True,
                            content=content,
                            url=url,
                            content_type="html",
                            metadata={"status": resp.status}
                        )
                    else:
                        return FetchResult(
                            success=False,
                            error=f"HTTP {resp.status}",
                            url=url
                        )
            except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                return FetchResult(success=False, error="Timeout", url=url)
    
    async def ping(self) -> bool:
        """鍋ュ悍妫€鏌?""
        try:
            async with aiohttp.ClientSession() as session:
                async with session.get(f"{self.base_url}/ping", timeout=5) as resp:
                    return resp.status == 200
        except:
            return False
```

### 33.2 EventBus瀹屾暣瀹炵幇

```python
# orchestration/bus.py
class EventBus:
    """
    浜嬩欢鎬荤嚎 鈥?璺ㄦā鍧楅€氫俊鏍稿績
    鏀寔: 鍚屾/寮傛浜嬩欢銆佽闃呮ā寮忋€佽缂樿拷韪€佸璁?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.subscribers = {}  # topic -> [handlers]
        self.event_store = EventStore()
        self.lineage_store = LineageStore()
        self.buffer = []
        self.buffer_size = 100
        self.flush_interval = 5  # 绉?
    
    async def publish(self, topic: str, event: DomainEvent, 
                      sync: bool = False) -> str:
        """鍙戝竷浜嬩欢"""
        event_id = f"evt_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
        event.topic = topic
        event.event_id = event_id
        event.timestamp = datetime.now()
        
        # 鍐欏叆瀛樺偍
        await self.event_store.save(event)
        
        # 璁板綍琛€缂?
        if event.entity_type and event.entity_id:
            await self._record_lineage_from_event(event)
        
        # 閫氱煡璁㈤槄鑰?
        handlers = self.subscribers.get(topic, [])
        if sync:
            for handler in handlers:
                await handler(event)
        else:
            for handler in handlers:
                asyncio.create_task(handler(event))
        
        # 瀹¤
        await audit_chain.append(
            action=f"event.{topic}",
            actor=event.actor or "system",
            payload={"event_id": event_id, "data": event.dict()}
        )
        
        return event_id
    
    def subscribe(self, topic: str, handler: Callable):
        """璁㈤槄浜嬩欢"""
        if topic not in self.subscribers:
            self.subscribers[topic] = []
        self.subscribers[topic].append(handler)
    
    def unsubscribe(self, topic: str, handler: Callable):
        """鍙栨秷璁㈤槄"""
        if topic in self.subscribers:
            self.subscribers[topic].remove(handler)
    
    async def _record_lineage_from_event(self, event: DomainEvent):
        """浠庝簨浠惰嚜鍔ㄨ褰曡缂?""
        # 瑙ｆ瀽浜嬩欢涓殑鍏崇郴
        relations = self._extract_relations(event)
        for rel in relations:
            await self.lineage_store.save(rel)
    
    def _extract_relations(self, event: DomainEvent) -> List[LineageLink]:
        """浠庝簨浠朵腑鎻愬彇琛€缂樺叧绯?""
        links = []
        topic = event.topic
        
        # 鏍规嵁topic瑙ｆ瀽鍏崇郴
        if topic.startswith("project."):
            # project.created, project.archived
            links.append(LineageLink(
                parent_type="user",
                parent_id=event.actor,
                child_type="project",
                child_id=event.entity_id,
                relation="created" if "created" in topic else "modified"
            ))
        elif topic.startswith("dataset."):
            if "imported" in topic:
                links.append(LineageLink(
                    parent_type="asset",
                    parent_id=event.payload.get("asset_id"),
                    child_type="dataset",
                    child_id=event.entity_id,
                    relation="imported_to"
                ))
            elif "exported" in topic:
                links.append(LineageLink(
                    parent_type="dataset",
                    parent_id=event.entity_id,
                    child_type="export",
                    child_id=event.payload.get("export_id"),
                    relation="exported_to"
                ))
        elif topic.startswith("annotation."):
            links.append(LineageLink(
                parent_type="pack",
                parent_id=event.payload.get("pack_id"),
                child_type="annotation",
                child_id=event.entity_id,
                relation="annotated"
            ))
        elif topic.startswith("qc."):
            links.append(LineageLink(
                parent_type="pack",
                parent_id=event.payload.get("pack_id"),
                child_type="qc_record",
                child_id=event.entity_id,
                relation="qc_checked"
            ))
        elif topic.startswith("crawler."):
            if "document_collected" in topic:
                links.append(LineageLink(
                    parent_type="crawler_job",
                    parent_id=event.payload.get("job_id"),
                    child_type="asset",
                    child_id=event.entity_id,
                    relation="collected"
                ))
        
        return links
    
    async def get_lineage(self, entity_type: str, entity_id: str, 
                           direction: str = "both") -> Dict:
        """鑾峰彇瀹炰綋鐨勮缂樺叧绯?""
        ancestors = []
        descendants = []
        
        if direction in ["up", "both"]:
            ancestors = await self.lineage_store.get_ancestors(entity_type, entity_id)
        if direction in ["down", "both"]:
            descendants = await self.lineage_store.get_descendants(entity_type, entity_id)
        
        return {
            "entity": {"type": entity_type, "id": entity_id},
            "ancestors": ancestors,
            "descendants": descendants,
            "timestamp": datetime.now()
        }
    
    async def get_impact_analysis(self, entity_type: str, entity_id: str) -> Dict:
        """褰卞搷鍒嗘瀽 鈥?鍙樻洿璇ュ疄浣撳奖鍝嶅摢浜涗笅娓?""
        descendants = await self.lineage_store.get_descendants(entity_type, entity_id)
        
        # 鎸夌被鍨嬪垎缁?
        impacted = {}
        for desc in descendants:
            if desc.child_type not in impacted:
                impacted[desc.child_type] = []
            impacted[desc.child_type].append({
                "id": desc.child_id,
                "relation": desc.relation,
                "depth": desc.depth
            })
        
        return {
            "entity": {"type": entity_type, "id": entity_id},
            "impacted": impacted,
            "total_impacted": len(descendants),
            "timestamp": datetime.now()
        }
```

### 33.3 鏁版嵁娴佽浆杩借釜鍣?

```python
# orchestration/dataflow_tracker.py
class DataFlowTracker:
    """
    鏁版嵁娴佽浆杩借釜鍣?鈥?鍙鍖栨暟鎹湪绯荤粺鍚勯樁娈电殑娴佽浆
    鏀寔: 瀹炴椂杩借釜銆佸巻鍙插洖鏀俱€佹€ц兘鍒嗘瀽銆佸紓甯告娴?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.flow_store = FlowStore()
        self.stage_times = defaultdict(list)
        self.bottleneck_detector = BottleneckDetector()
    
    async def track_flow(self, flow_id: str, entity_type: str, entity_id: str):
        """杩借釜涓€涓暟鎹祦鐨勫畬鏁寸敓鍛藉懆鏈?""
        flow = {
            "id": flow_id,
            "entity_type": entity_type,
            "entity_id": entity_id,
            "stages": [],
            "started_at": datetime.now(),
            "status": "in_progress"
        }
        
        # 璁㈤槄璇ュ疄浣撶浉鍏充簨浠?
        def on_event(event):
            stage = {
                "name": event.topic,
                "timestamp": event.timestamp,
                "actor": event.actor,
                "payload": event.payload
            }
            flow["stages"].append(stage)
            
            # 璁＄畻鍚勯樁娈佃€楁椂
            if len(flow["stages"]) > 1:
                prev = flow["stages"][-2]
                duration = (stage["timestamp"] - prev["timestamp"]).total_seconds()
                self.stage_times[prev["name"]].append(duration)
            
            # 妫€娴嬬摱棰?
            self.bottleneck_detector.check(flow["stages"])
        
        self.bus.subscribe(f"{entity_type}.{entity_id}", on_event)
        
        # 瀛樺偍
        await self.flow_store.save(flow)
        
        return flow
    
    async def get_flow_status(self, flow_id: str) -> Dict:
        """鑾峰彇娴佽浆鐘舵€?""
        flow = await self.flow_store.get(flow_id)
        if not flow:
            return {"status": "not_found"}
        
        stages = flow.get("stages", [])
        current_stage = stages[-1] if stages else None
        
        return {
            "flow_id": flow_id,
            "status": flow.get("status", "unknown"),
            "current_stage": current_stage,
            "stages_count": len(stages),
            "started_at": flow.get("started_at"),
            "updated_at": current_stage.get("timestamp") if current_stage else None,
            "bottlenecks": self.bottleneck_detector.get_bottlenecks(flow_id)
        }
    
    async def visualize_flow(self, flow_id: str) -> Dict:
        """鐢熸垚娴佽浆鍙鍖栨暟鎹?""
        flow = await self.flow_store.get(flow_id)
        if not flow:
            return {"error": "Flow not found"}
        
        # 鏋勫缓DAG
        stages = flow.get("stages", [])
        nodes = []
        edges = []
        
        for i, stage in enumerate(stages):
            nodes.append({
                "id": i,
                "label": stage["name"],
                "stage": i,
                "timestamp": stage["timestamp"].isoformat(),
                "duration": self._calc_duration(stages, i)
            })
            if i > 0:
                edges.append({
                    "source": i - 1,
                    "target": i,
                    "duration": nodes[i]["duration"]
                })
        
        return {
            "flow_id": flow_id,
            "nodes": nodes,
            "edges": edges,
            "total_duration": self._calc_total_duration(stages)
        }
```

### 33.4 鏁版嵁娴佽浆鐘舵€佹満

```python
# orchestration/flow_state_machine.py
class FlowStateMachine:
    """
    鏁版嵁娴佽浆鐘舵€佹満 鈥?绠＄悊鏁版嵁鍦ㄥ悇闃舵鐨勭姸鎬佽浆鎹?
    """
    
    STATES = {
        "raw": ["collected", "imported", "uploaded"],
        "collected": ["cleaning", "deduping"],
        "cleaning": ["cleaned", "failed"],
        "cleaned": ["labeling", "scoring"],
        "labeling": ["labeled", "review_required"],
        "labeled": ["reviewing", "qc_pending"],
        "reviewing": ["approved", "rejected"],
        "qc_pending": ["qc_passed", "qc_failed"],
        "qc_passed": ["ready", "exporting"],
        "exporting": ["exported", "failed"],
        "exported": ["delivered", "archived"],
        "failed": ["retrying", "manual_review"]
    }
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.current_state = "raw"
        self.history = []
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    async def transition(self, new_state: str, metadata: Dict = None) -> bool:
        """鐘舵€佽浆鎹?""
        if new_state not in self.STATES.get(self.current_state, []):
            # 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚︽槸鍚堟硶杞崲
            valid = False
            for states in self.STATES.values():
                if self.current_state in states and new_state in states:
                    valid = True
                    break
            if not valid:
                raise InvalidStateTransitionError(
                    f"Cannot transition from {self.current_state} to {new_state}"
                )
        
        old_state = self.current_state
        self.current_state = new_state
        self.history.append({
            "from": old_state,
            "to": new_state,
            "timestamp": datetime.now(),
            "metadata": metadata or {}
        })
        
        # 鍙戝竷鐘舵€佸彉鏇翠簨浠?
        await self.bus.publish(
            topic=f"flow.state_changed",
            event=DomainEvent(
                entity_type="flow",
                entity_id=self.flow_id,
                payload={
                    "old_state": old_state,
                    "new_state": new_state,
                    "metadata": metadata
                },
                actor=metadata.get("actor") if metadata else "system"
            )
        )
        
        return True
```

### 34.2 绠＄嚎缂栨帓鍣?

```python
# orchestration/pipeline_orchestrator.py
class PipelineOrchestrator:
    """
    绠＄嚎缂栨帓鍣?鈥?绠＄悊12闃舵绠＄嚎鐨勬墽琛?
    鏀寔: 椤哄簭鎵ц銆佸苟琛屾墽琛屻€佹潯浠跺垎鏀€侀噸璇曘€佸洖婊?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.stages = self._build_stages()
        self.active_pipelines = {}
        self.bus = EventBus()
        self.metrics = ServiceMetrics()
    
    def _build_stages(self) -> List[Stage]:
        """鏋勫缓12涓樁娈?""
        return [
            Stage("collection", "鏅鸿兘閲囬泦", CollectionExecutor()),
            Stage("processing", "鏁版嵁澶勭悊", ProcessingExecutor()),
            Stage("auto_label", "鑷姩鏍囨敞", AutoLabelExecutor()),
            Stage("scoring", "璐ㄩ噺璇勫垎", ScoringExecutor()),
            Stage("packing", "鏁版嵁鎵撳寘", PackingExecutor()),
            Stage("annotation", "浜哄伐鏍囨敞", AnnotationExecutor()),
            Stage("review", "瀹℃牳", ReviewExecutor()),
            Stage("qc", "璐ㄦ", QCExecutor()),
            Stage("acceptance", "楠屾敹", AcceptanceExecutor()),
            Stage("delivery", "浜や粯鍒嗕韩", DeliveryExecutor()),
            Stage("export", "璁粌闆嗗鍑?, ExportExecutor()),
            Stage("collaboration", "Agent鍗忎綔", CollaborationExecutor())
        ]
    
    async def start_pipeline(self, config: PipelineConfig) -> str:
        """鍚姩绠＄嚎"""
        pipeline_id = f"pipe_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
        
        pipeline = {
            "id": pipeline_id,
            "config": config,
            "stages": [],
            "current_stage": 0,
            "status": "running",
            "started_at": datetime.now(),
            "results": {}
        }
        self.active_pipelines[pipeline_id] = pipeline
        
        # 寮傛鎵ц
        asyncio.create_task(self._run_pipeline(pipeline_id))
        
        return pipeline_id
    
    async def _run_pipeline(self, pipeline_id: str):
        """鎵ц绠＄嚎"""
        pipeline = self.active_pipelines[pipeline_id]
        config = pipeline["config"]
        
        # 纭畾鎵ц椤哄簭 (鍙兘璺宠繃鏌愪簺闃舵)
        stages_to_run = self._filter_stages(config)
        
        for idx, stage in enumerate(stages_to_run):
            pipeline["current_stage"] = idx
            
            try:
                # 鎵ц闃舵
                result = await stage.executor.execute(
                    pipeline["results"],
                    config.get(stage.name, {})
                )
                pipeline["results"][stage.name] = result
                
                # 璁板綍闃舵瀹屾垚
                pipeline["stages"].append({
                    "name": stage.name,
                    "status": "completed",
                    "result": result,
                    "timestamp": datetime.now()
                })
                
                # 鍙戝竷浜嬩欢
                await self.bus.publish(
                    topic=f"pipeline.stage_completed",
                    event=DomainEvent(
                        entity_type="pipeline",
                        entity_id=pipeline_id,
                        payload={
                            "stage": stage.name,
                            "result": result
                        }
                    )
                )
                
                # 妫€鏌ユ槸鍚﹀簲璇ョ户缁?
                if not config.get("continue_on_stage_failure", False):
                    if result.get("status") == "failed":
                        pipeline["status"] = "failed"
                        break
                
            except Exception as e:
                pipeline["status"] = "failed"
                pipeline["error"] = str(e)
                pipeline["stages"].append({
                    "name": stage.name,
                    "status": "failed",
                    "error": str(e),
                    "timestamp": datetime.now()
                })
                break
        
        if pipeline["status"] != "failed":
            pipeline["status"] = "completed"
        pipeline["completed_at"] = datetime.now()
        
        # 鍙戝竷绠＄嚎瀹屾垚浜嬩欢
        await self.bus.publish(
            topic=f"pipeline.completed",
            event=DomainEvent(
                entity_type="pipeline",
                entity_id=pipeline_id,
                payload={
                    "status": pipeline["status"],
                    "stages": len(pipeline["stages"])
                }
            )
        )
    
    def _filter_stages(self, config: Dict) -> List[Stage]:
        """鏍规嵁閰嶇疆杩囨护闇€瑕佹墽琛岀殑闃舵"""
        skip_stages = config.get("skip_stages", [])
        return [s for s in self.stages if s.name not in skip_stages]
    
    async def get_pipeline_status(self, pipeline_id: str) -> Dict:
        """鑾峰彇绠＄嚎鐘舵€?""
        pipeline = self.active_pipelines.get(pipeline_id)
        if not pipeline:
            return {"status": "not_found"}
        
        return {
            "id": pipeline_id,
            "status": pipeline["status"],
            "current_stage": pipeline["current_stage"],
            "stages": pipeline["stages"],
            "started_at": pipeline["started_at"],
            "completed_at": pipeline.get("completed_at"),
            "error": pipeline.get("error"),
            "progress": len(pipeline["stages"]) / len(self.stages) * 100
        }
```


## 绗?5绔?宸ヤ綔娴佺紪鎺?(鎵╁睍鑷?5+妯℃澘)

### 35.1 宸ヤ綔娴佸紩鎿庡畬鏁村疄鐜?

```python
# workflow_builder/engine.py
class WorkflowEngine:
    """
    宸ヤ綔娴佸紩鎿?鈥?DAG缂栨帓鎵ц
    鏀寔: 25+妯℃澘銆?40+鑺傜偣绫诲瀷銆佸彉閲忔浛鎹€佹嫇鎵戞帓搴忋€佸紓姝ユ墽琛?
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.templates = self._load_templates()
        self.node_registry = NodeRegistry()
        self.active_runs = {}
        self.bus = EventBus()
    
    def _load_templates(self) -> Dict:
        """鍔犺浇25+宸ヤ綔娴佹ā鏉?""

                ]
            },
            "wf_collect_videos": {

                "nodes": [
                    {"id": "n1", "capability": "crawler.video", "label": "瑙嗛閲囬泦"},
                    {"id": "n2", "capability": "cleaning.video", "label": "瑙嗛娓呮礂"},
                    {"id": "n3", "capability": "scoring.quality", "label": "璐ㄩ噺璇勫垎"},
                    {"id": "n4", "capability": "dataset.create", "label": "鍒涘缓鏁版嵁闆?}
                ],
                "edges": [
                    {"source": "n1", "target": "n2"},
                    {"source": "n2", "target": "n3"},
                    {"source": "n3", "target": "n4"}
                ]
            },
            # 鏍囨敞绫?(5)

    async def run_workflow(self, workflow_id: str, params: Dict) -> WorkflowResult:
        """杩愯宸ヤ綔娴?""
        template = self.templates.get(workflow_id)
        if not template:
            raise ValueError(f"Workflow template not found: {workflow_id}")
        
        # 鏋勫缓DAG
        nodes = template["nodes"]
        edges = template["edges"]
        
        # 鎷撴墤鎺掑簭
        sorted_nodes = self._topological_sort(nodes, edges)
        
        # 鎵ц
        results = {}
        for node in sorted_nodes:
            # 鍙橀噺鏇挎崲
            inputs = self._expand_variables(node.get("inputs", {}), results)
            
            # 璋冪敤鑳藉姏
            cap_result = await self.capability_registry.invoke(
                cap_id=node["capability"],
                inputs=inputs,
                actor=params.get("actor"),
                refs={"workflow_id": workflow_id, "node_id": node["id"]}
            )
            
            results[node["id"]] = cap_result.outputs
        
        return WorkflowResult(
            workflow_id=workflow_id,
            node_results=results,
            status="completed",
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )
    
    def _topological_sort(self, nodes: List[Dict], edges: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """Kahn绠楁硶鎷撴墤鎺掑簭 + 鐜娴?""
        # 鏋勫缓鍥?
        graph = {n["id"]: [] for n in nodes}
        in_degree = {n["id"]: 0 for n in nodes}
        
        for edge in edges:
            graph[edge["source"]].append(edge["target"])
            in_degree[edge["target"]] += 1
        
        # 鍏ュ害涓?鐨勮妭鐐?
        queue = [nid for nid, deg in in_degree.items() if deg == 0]
        sorted_ids = []
        
        while queue:
            nid = queue.pop(0)
            sorted_ids.append(nid)
            for neighbor in graph[nid]:
                in_degree[neighbor] -= 1
                if in_degree[neighbor] == 0:
                    queue.append(neighbor)
        
        # 鐜娴?
        if len(sorted_ids) != len(nodes):
            raise CircularDependencyError("Workflow contains circular dependency")
        
        # 鎸夋帓搴忚繑鍥炶妭鐐?
        node_map = {n["id"]: n for n in nodes}
        return [node_map[nid] for nid in sorted_ids]
    
    def _expand_variables(self, inputs: Dict, results: Dict) -> Dict:
        """鍙橀噺鏇挎崲 ${n1.outputs.field}"""
        expanded = {}
        for key, value in inputs.items():
            if isinstance(value, str):
                # 鏇挎崲 ${...}
                def replacer(match):
                    expr = match.group(1)
                    parts = expr.split(".")
                    if len(parts) >= 2:
                        node_id = parts[0]
                        field = ".".join(parts[1:])
                        if node_id in results:
                            return str(self._get_nested(results[node_id], field))
                    return match.group(0)
                
                import re
                pattern = r"\$\{([\w.]+)\}"
                expanded[key] = re.sub(pattern, replacer, value)
            else:
                expanded[key] = value
        return expanded
```
